  distribution_channel_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.channel. Business justification: Restrictions (stop-sell, min LOS, CTA/CTD) are applied per distribution channel. Revenue managers close channels selectively based on demand - essential inventory control operation. Enables channel-sp']
  dynamic_rate_rule_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to revenue.dynamic_rate_rule. Business justification: Rate restrictions in IDeaS G3 RMS can be automatically triggered by Dynamic Rate Rules (DRRs) — the rms_recommendation_flag on rate_restriction indicates RMS-driven restrictions. Adding dynamic_rate_r']
  market_segment_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to revenue.market_segment. Business justification: Rate restrictions can be scoped to market segments (e.g., restrict Leisure segment on peak dates). rate_restriction has market_segment_code (STRING) which should be normalized to FK. N rate_restrictio']
  promotion_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.promotion. Business justification: Loyalty promotions frequently grant restriction exemptions (e.g., a promotion waives minimum LOS for Platinum members). The existing is_loyalty_exempt flag is a denormalized boolean; replacing it with']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the property (hotel/resort) to which this rate restriction applies. Enables property-level yield optimization and restriction management across the portfolio.']
  reservation_group_block_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the group block associated with this restriction, when the restriction is applied to protect inventory for a specific group booking or MICE event. Null for transient/individual restrictions.']
  revenue_rate_plan_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the rate plan to which this restriction applies. Links to the rate plan master in the CRS/RMS (e.g., BAR, LRA, NRR, DRR). A restriction may apply to one or multiple rate plans; this field captures the primary rate plan association.']
  room_type_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the specific room type to which this restriction applies. When null, the restriction applies to all room types under the associated rate plan. Enables granular inventory control by room category.']
  seasonal_calendar_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.seasonal_calendar. Business justification: rate_restriction has a plain \'season_code\' attribute — a direct denormalization of seasonal_calendar. Rate restrictions (CTA, CTD, min/max LOS) are operationally defined by season. FK to seasonal_cale']
  advance_purchase_days varchar [note: 'Minimum number of days prior to arrival that a booking must be made to qualify for this rate plan. Supports NRR (Non-Refundable Rate) and advance purchase yield strategies. Null when restriction type is not ADVANCE_PURCHASE.']
  applied_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this rate restriction was activated and distributed to connected channels (CRS, GDS, OTA). Represents the principal business event time — when the restriction became operationally effective in the distribution ecosystem. Formatted as yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss.SSSXXX.']
  created_by_user varchar [note: 'Username or employee identifier of the revenue manager or system process that created this rate restriction record. Supports SOX financial controls audit trail and accountability for yield management decisions.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this rate restriction record was first created in the source system. Used for audit trail, data lineage, and SLA compliance tracking. Formatted as yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss.SSSXXX.']
  days_of_week_mask bigint [note: '7-character binary string indicating which days of the week the restriction applies, ordered Monday through Sunday (e.g., \'1111100\' = Mon–Fri only, \'0000011\' = Sat–Sun only). Enables day-of-week yield strategies such as weekend minimum stay requirements.']
  demand_forecast_level decimal [note: 'Demand forecast classification at the time this restriction was created or last updated, as determined by the RMS (IDeaS G3 or Infor EzRMS). Provides context for why the restriction was applied and supports post-hoc yield strategy analysis.']
  distribution_status varchar [note: 'Indicates the current distribution state of this restriction across connected channels via Sabre SynXis CRS. \'pending\' = queued for distribution; \'distributed\' = successfully pushed to all channels; \'failed\' = distribution error; \'partial\' = distributed to some but not all channels.']
  effective_date date [note: 'The calendar date from which this rate restriction becomes active and enforceable. Corresponds to the stay date (not booking date) unless the restriction type is ADVANCE_PURCHASE. Formatted as yyyy-MM-dd per model conventions.']
  expiry_date date [note: 'The last calendar date on which this rate restriction is enforceable (inclusive). Null indicates an open-ended restriction with no defined end. Formatted as yyyy-MM-dd per model conventions.']
  hurdle_rate_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Minimum acceptable rate (in the property\'s base currency) below which a booking will be rejected for this rate plan on the restricted date(s). A key RMS yield control used to protect ADR during high-demand periods. Null when restriction type is not HURDLE_RATE.']
  is_blackout boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the effective date range is designated as a blackout period, during which the rate plan is completely closed to new bookings. Commonly applied during peak demand events, holidays, or sold-out periods.']
  is_cta boolean [note: 'Indicates whether arrivals are blocked on the effective date(s) for this rate plan and room type. When True, guests cannot check in on the restricted date, preventing short-stay bookings that fragment inventory during high-demand periods.']
  is_ctd boolean [note: 'Indicates whether departures are blocked on the effective date(s) for this rate plan and room type. When True, guests cannot check out on the restricted date, used to extend stays through high-demand nights and maximize occupancy continuity.']
  last_distributed_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this restriction was last successfully distributed to external channels (OTA, GDS) via Sabre SynXis CRS. Used to monitor distribution latency and SLA compliance for rate parity management.']
  max_advance_purchase_days varchar [note: 'Maximum number of days prior to arrival within which a booking must be made to qualify for this rate plan. Defines the booking window ceiling for advance purchase restrictions, preventing bookings made too far in advance at promotional rates.']
  max_los varchar [note: 'Maximum number of nights a guest is permitted to stay under this rate plan on the restricted date(s). Used to prevent long-stay bookings at discounted rates during high-demand periods. Null when restriction type is not MAX_LOS.']
  min_los varchar [note: 'Minimum number of nights a guest must stay to be eligible to book under this rate plan on the restricted date(s). A core yield optimization lever in revenue management. Null when restriction type is not MIN_LOS.']
  notes varchar [note: 'Free-text field for additional operational notes or context provided by the revenue manager regarding this restriction. May include references to specific events, competitive intelligence, or strategy rationale not captured in structured fields.']
  override_allowed boolean [note: 'Indicates whether a revenue manager or front desk supervisor is permitted to manually override this restriction for individual bookings. When False, the restriction is hard-enforced and cannot be bypassed in the PMS or CRS.']
  override_authorization_level bigint [note: 'Minimum staff authorization level required to override this restriction when override_allowed is True. Ensures appropriate governance over yield control exceptions. Null when override_allowed is False.']
  priority_rank varchar [note: 'Numeric priority rank used to resolve conflicts when multiple restrictions apply to the same rate plan, room type, and date. Lower values indicate higher priority. Ensures deterministic restriction enforcement when overlapping rules exist in the RMS.']
  restriction_code varchar [note: 'Externally-known alphanumeric code uniquely identifying this rate restriction rule as defined in IDeaS G3 RMS or Sabre SynXis CRS. Used for cross-system reconciliation and distribution to OTA and GDS channels.']
  restriction_name varchar [note: 'Human-readable name describing the rate restriction rule (e.g., \'Weekend Min 2-Night Stay\', \'Holiday CTA Block\'). Used by revenue managers and front desk staff to identify restrictions in PMS and RMS interfaces.']
  restriction_reason varchar [note: 'Free-text or coded explanation for why this restriction was applied (e.g., \'Peak demand event\', \'Holiday blackout\', \'Group block protection\', \'RMS auto-recommendation\'). Supports revenue strategy documentation and post-stay performance analysis.']
  restriction_scope varchar [note: 'Defines the level at which this restriction is applied: \'property\' = entire property; \'room_type\' = specific room category; \'rate_plan\' = specific rate plan only; \'channel\' = specific distribution channel (OTA, GDS, direct). Determines how broadly the restriction is enforced across inventory.']
  restriction_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle state of the rate restriction record. \'active\' = currently enforced; \'inactive\' = disabled but retained for history; \'pending\' = scheduled but not yet effective; \'expired\' = past end date; \'overridden\' = manually superseded by a revenue manager.']
  restriction_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the restriction mechanism applied. MIN_LOS = Minimum Length of Stay; MAX_LOS = Maximum Length of Stay; CTA = Closed to Arrival; CTD = Closed to Departure; ADVANCE_PURCHASE = minimum days before arrival required to book; BLACKOUT = date fully closed to booking; HURDLE_RATE = minimum acceptable rate threshold. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: MIN_LOS|MAX_LOS|CTA|CTD|ADVANCE_PURCHASE|BLACKOUT|HURDLE_RATE — promote to reference product]']
  rms_recommendation_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this restriction was system-recommended by the RMS (True) or manually created by a revenue manager (False). Enables analysis of RMS automation adoption rates and comparison of system vs. human yield decisions.']
  source_system_restriction_reference varchar [note: 'The native identifier of this restriction record in the originating operational system (IDeaS G3 RMS, Sabre SynXis CRS, etc.). Enables traceability and reconciliation between the lakehouse Silver Layer and the system of record.']
  updated_by_user varchar [note: 'Username or employee identifier of the revenue manager or system process that last modified this rate restriction record. Supports audit trail and governance of yield management changes.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this rate restriction record was last modified in the source system. Tracks the most recent change for audit and reconciliation purposes. Formatted as yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss.SSSXXX.']

  Note: 'Operational records of rate restrictions applied to rate plans and room types, including minimum LOS (Length of Stay), maximum LOS, closed-to-arrival (CTA), closed-to-departure (CTD), advance purchase requirements, and blackout dates. Managed in IDeaS G3 RMS and distributed via Sabre SynXis CRS. Drives yield optimization by controlling which rates are bookable under specific conditions.'
}

Table revenue.dynamic_rate_rule {
  dynamic_rate_rule_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique surrogate identifier for a Dynamic Rate Rule (DRR) record in the revenue management system. Primary key for this entity.']
  currency_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.currency. Business justification: Dynamic rate rule ceiling/floor amounts (max_rate_ceiling, min_rate_floor) are currency-denominated. currency_code is denormalized; FK to currency entity enforces 3NF and supports multi-currency RMS r']
  demand_forecast_id varchar [note: 'Identifier of the demand forecast record from IDeaS G3 RMS or Infor EzRMS that this forecast-based Dynamic Rate Rule references for its trigger evaluation.']
  distribution_channel_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.channel. Business justification: Dynamic pricing rules target specific channels differently (e.g., OTA rates adjust based on commission costs, direct channel gets best rate). RMS systems apply channel-specific rate optimization strat']
  event_booking_id varchar [note: 'Identifier of the local demand event (e.g., MICE event, conference, festival, sporting event) that triggers this event-based Dynamic Rate Rule. Links to the event master record in Delphi by Amadeus or the events domain.']
  guest_segment_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to guest.segment. Business justification: Dynamic pricing rules target specific guest segments for personalized rate adjustments. Revenue management systems apply segment-specific pricing logic (e.g., loyalty tier discounts, corporate negotia']
  loyalty_tier_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.tier. Business justification: Dynamic pricing rules adjust rates based on member tier for personalized revenue optimization. Business process: applying tier-specific rate adjustments in revenue management systems to reward high-va']
  market_segment_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to revenue.market_segment. Business justification: Dynamic rate rules can be scoped to specific market segments. dynamic_rate_rule has market_segment_code (STRING) which should be normalized to FK. N DRR records → 1 market_segment. Removes redundant m']
  promotion_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.promotion. Business justification: Loyalty promotions can trigger dynamic pricing rules (e.g., a flash-sale promotion activates a dynamic rate adjustment for eligible members). This FK enables promotion-triggered dynamic pricing workfl']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Identifier of the hotel or resort property to which this Dynamic Rate Rule applies. Links to the property master record in Oracle OPERA PMS.']
  revenue_rate_plan_id varchar [note: 'Identifier of the rate plan (e.g., BAR, LRA, NRR) to which this Dynamic Rate Rule applies. A null value indicates the rule applies across all eligible rate plans for the property.']
  room_type_id varchar [note: 'Identifier of the specific room type (e.g., standard king, deluxe suite) to which this Dynamic Rate Rule applies. A null value indicates the rule applies across all room types at the property.']
  target_member_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.member. Business justification: Dynamic rules can target specific high-value members for personalized pricing strategies. Business process: VIP member-specific rate rules for retention and revenue optimization, common in luxury hosp']
  adjustment_direction varchar [note: 'Indicates whether the Dynamic Rate Rule increases or decreases the rate when triggered. Provides explicit directional intent separate from the sign of adjustment_value to prevent ambiguity in RMS configuration.']
  adjustment_type varchar [note: 'Method by which the Dynamic Rate Rule adjusts the published rate when triggered. Percentage applies a relative increase or decrease to the current rate; absolute_amount adds or subtracts a fixed currency value; bar_offset moves the rate a fixed amount above or below the Best Available Rate (BAR); bar_multiplier applies a multiplier to the BAR.']
  adjustment_value decimal(10,4) [note: 'The magnitude of the rate adjustment applied when the Dynamic Rate Rule is triggered. Interpreted according to adjustment_type: a value of 0.10 with type \'percentage\' means a 10% rate increase; a value of 25.00 with type \'absolute_amount\' means a $25 rate increase; a value of -15.00 with type \'bar_offset\' means $15 below BAR.']
  advance_booking_max_days varchar [note: 'Maximum number of days in advance of the arrival date within which a booking must be made for this Dynamic Rate Rule to be eligible to apply. Null indicates no upper advance booking restriction.']
  advance_booking_min_days varchar [note: 'Minimum number of days in advance of the arrival date that a booking must be made for this Dynamic Rate Rule to be eligible to apply. Supports advance purchase pricing strategies.']
  approval_status varchar [note: 'Workflow approval state of the Dynamic Rate Rule indicating whether it has been reviewed and authorized by a revenue manager before activation. Supports SOX-compliant pricing governance controls.']
  approved_by varchar [note: 'Name or employee identifier of the revenue manager or director who approved this Dynamic Rate Rule for activation. Required for SOX financial controls audit trail on pricing decisions.']
  approved_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this Dynamic Rate Rule was approved for activation by the authorized revenue manager. Part of the pricing governance audit trail required under SOX financial controls.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this Dynamic Rate Rule record was first created in the system. Part of the standard audit trail for pricing configuration governance.']
  days_of_week_mask bigint [note: 'Seven-character binary string (positions 1–7 = Mon–Sun) indicating which days of the week this Dynamic Rate Rule is eligible to fire. A value of \'1111100\' means Monday through Friday only. Enables day-of-week yield optimization strategies.']
  effective_from date [note: 'The calendar date from which this Dynamic Rate Rule becomes active and eligible to trigger automated pricing adjustments in the RMS. Aligns with the stay date range for yield optimization.']
  effective_until date [note: 'The calendar date on which this Dynamic Rate Rule expires and ceases to trigger automated pricing adjustments. Null indicates an open-ended rule with no defined expiry.']
  is_stackable boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this Dynamic Rate Rule can be combined (stacked) with other active rules for the same stay date, room type, and rate plan. When False, this rule takes exclusive precedence based on rule_priority and no other rules are applied concurrently.']
  last_triggered_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this Dynamic Rate Rule was most recently evaluated as true and triggered an automated pricing adjustment in the RMS. Used by revenue managers to monitor rule activity and effectiveness.']
  los_max_nights varchar [note: 'Maximum Length of Stay (LOS) restriction in nights beyond which this Dynamic Rate Rule does not apply. Null indicates no upper LOS restriction.']
  los_min_nights varchar [note: 'Minimum Length of Stay (LOS) restriction in nights that must be satisfied for this Dynamic Rate Rule to apply. Used in LOS-based yield optimization to drive longer stays during high-demand periods.']
  max_rate_ceiling decimal(10,2) [note: 'The highest permissible rate (in property currency) that this Dynamic Rate Rule may produce after adjustment. Acts as a pricing guardrail to prevent rates from exceeding the property\'s maximum acceptable rate cap. Sensitive pricing strategy data.']
  min_rate_floor decimal(10,2) [note: 'The lowest permissible rate (in property currency) that this Dynamic Rate Rule may produce after adjustment. Acts as a pricing guardrail to prevent rates from falling below the property\'s minimum acceptable ADR threshold. Sensitive pricing strategy data.']
  pickup_window_days varchar [note: 'Number of days in the booking pickup window used to evaluate pickup velocity for pickup-based Dynamic Rate Rules. For example, a value of 7 means the rule evaluates rooms booked in the last 7 days.']
  rms_rule_reference_code varchar [note: 'Native rule identifier assigned by the source Revenue Management System (IDeaS G3 RMS or Infor EzRMS) for this Dynamic Rate Rule. Used for system-of-record traceability and reconciliation between the lakehouse Silver layer and the operational RMS.']
  rule_code varchar [note: 'Externally-known alphanumeric code uniquely identifying the Dynamic Rate Rule within the Revenue Management System (RMS). Used for cross-system reference between IDeaS G3 RMS, Infor EzRMS, and Sabre SynXis CRS.']
  rule_description varchar [note: 'Detailed narrative description of the Dynamic Rate Rule\'s business purpose, pricing logic, and intended yield optimization outcome.']
  rule_name varchar [note: 'Human-readable name describing the Dynamic Rate Rule, used by revenue managers to identify and manage pricing strategies within the RMS dashboard.']
  rule_priority varchar [note: 'Numeric priority ranking that determines the order of evaluation when multiple Dynamic Rate Rules are eligible to fire simultaneously for the same property, room type, and rate plan. Lower numeric values indicate higher priority (e.g., 1 = highest priority).']
  rule_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle state of the Dynamic Rate Rule governing whether it is eligible to trigger automated pricing adjustments. Active rules are evaluated by the RMS engine; draft rules are under configuration; suspended rules are temporarily disabled; archived rules are retained for historical audit.']
  rule_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the Dynamic Rate Rule by the trigger mechanism driving automated pricing adjustments. Occupancy-based rules fire on OCC thresholds; pickup-based on booking velocity; competitive-based on RGI/ARI/MPI benchmarks from STR STAR Report; event-based on MICE or local demand events; LOS-based on Length of Stay (LOS) restrictions; forecast-based on RMS demand forecasts. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: occupancy_based|pickup_based|competitive_based|event_based|los_based|forecast_based — promote to reference product]']
  trigger_count varchar [note: 'Cumulative number of times this Dynamic Rate Rule has been triggered and applied a pricing adjustment since its activation date. Used to assess rule utilization and yield optimization effectiveness.']
  trigger_threshold_operator varchar [note: 'Comparison operator applied to the trigger threshold value to determine whether the rule condition is met. For example, \'greater_than\' with a threshold of 0.80 means the rule fires when OCC exceeds 80%.']
  trigger_threshold_unit varchar [note: 'Unit of measure for the trigger threshold value. Percentage applies to OCC-based rules; room_count applies to pickup-based rules; index_value applies to competitive benchmarking rules (RGI, MPI, ARI); currency_amount applies to ADR-based triggers; nights applies to LOS-based rules.']
  trigger_threshold_value decimal(10,4) [note: 'The numeric threshold at which this Dynamic Rate Rule fires. For occupancy-based rules, this is the OCC percentage (e.g., 0.80 = 80%). For pickup-based rules, this is the number of rooms picked up within the pickup window. For competitive-based rules, this is the RGI or ARI index value.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this Dynamic Rate Rule record was most recently modified. Used for change data capture (CDC) in the Databricks Lakehouse Silver layer ETL pipeline.']
  version_number varchar [note: 'Incremental version counter tracking the number of times this Dynamic Rate Rule configuration has been modified. Supports audit trail and change management for pricing strategy governance.']

  Note: 'DRR (Dynamic Rate Rule) definitions governing automated pricing adjustments in IDeaS G3 RMS and Infor EzRMS. Captures rule type (occupancy-based, pickup-based, competitive-based, event-based), trigger thresholds, adjustment type (percentage, absolute, BAR offset), applicable room types, applicable rate plans, effective date ranges, and rule priority. Core mechanism for yield optimization and dynamic pricing strategy.'
}

Adding demand_forecast_']

Business justification: Rate/availability snapshots are channel-specific - each channel sees different rates and inventory based on connectivity and contracts. Core distribution management requires tracking what each channel']

  inventory_control_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to revenue.inventory_control. Business justification: Rate availability snapshots are the published output of inventory control decisions — the available_rooms, stop_sell, closed_to_arrival, and closed_to_departure values on rate_availability directly re']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the property (hotel, resort, or vacation property) for which this rate and availability snapshot applies. Sourced from Oracle OPERA PMS property configuration.']

  availability_status varchar [note: 'Current open/closed availability status for this property, room type, rate plan, and date combination as managed in IDeaS G3 RMS and distributed via Sabre SynXis CRS. \'open\' = bookable; \'closed\' = inventory blocked; \'stop_sell\' = yield-driven closure; \'on_request\' = requires manual confirmation; \'min_stay_restriction\' = LOS restriction active; \'closed_to_arrival\' = no new arrivals permitted on this date.']
  available_rooms varchar [note: 'Number of rooms of this room type available for sale on the snapshot date at this property. Represents net sellable inventory after deducting out-of-order, out-of-service, and already-committed rooms. Core input for OCC (Occupancy Rate) and RevPAR calculations.']
  bar_rate decimal(10,2) [note: 'The Best Available Rate (BAR) for this room type, property, and stay date — the lowest publicly available non-restricted rate as determined by IDeaS G3 RMS dynamic pricing engine. BAR is the anchor rate from which other rate plans are derived and is the primary rate distributed via Sabre SynXis CRS and OTA channels.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this rate and availability snapshot record was first created in the Silver layer lakehouse. Serves as the audit creation timestamp for data lineage and ETL pipeline tracking.']
  effective_from_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time from which this rate and availability record became active and was distributed to booking channels. Used for bi-temporal modeling of rate history and supports point-in-time rate reconstruction for revenue audits and dispute resolution.']
  effective_until_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time until which this rate and availability record remains active. Null indicates the record is currently active. Used for bi-temporal modeling and historical rate reconstruction. When a new rate update is received, the prior record\'s effective_until_timestamp is set to the new record\'s effective_from_timestamp.']
  gds_rate_code decimal [note: 'The rate code as published on GDS (Global Distribution System) platforms (Sabre, Amadeus, Travelport) via Sabre SynXis CRS. GDS rate codes follow standardized formats required for travel agent booking systems and corporate travel management programs.']
  group_block_rooms varchar [note: 'Number of rooms on the snapshot date allocated to group blocks (MICE, corporate groups, tour operators) as managed in Oracle OPERA PMS and Delphi by Amadeus. Group block inventory is excluded from transient availability and tracked separately for yield optimization.']
  is_package_rate decimal(9,4) [note: 'Indicates whether this rate plan includes bundled package components (e.g., breakfast, spa credit, parking, airport transfer) beyond the base room charge. Package rates require component-level revenue allocation across USALI departments in Oracle OPERA PMS.']
  last_updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this rate and availability record was last modified in the source system (IDeaS G3 RMS or Sabre SynXis CRS). Represents the business event timestamp of the most recent pricing or availability change. Critical for real-time channel distribution synchronization and SLA monitoring.']
  max_rate decimal(10,2) [note: 'The ceiling rate (maximum sellable rate) for this room type, property, rate plan, and stay date as configured in IDeaS G3 RMS. Caps pricing during peak demand periods to maintain guest trust and brand integrity, and supports rate parity compliance across channels.']
  meal_plan_code varchar [note: 'Code indicating the meal plan inclusion for this rate plan (RO = Room Only; BB = Bed and Breakfast; HB = Half Board; FB = Full Board; AI = All Inclusive). Affects rate composition, F&B revenue allocation, and package pricing in Oracle OPERA PMS and MICROS POS.']
  min_rate decimal(10,2) [note: 'The floor rate (minimum sellable rate) for this room type, property, rate plan, and stay date as configured in IDeaS G3 RMS. Represents the lowest price at which the room may be sold under any circumstance, enforcing revenue floor controls and preventing rate erosion.']
  occupancy_forecast_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Forecasted occupancy rate (OCC%) for the property on the snapshot date as projected by IDeaS G3 RMS or Infor EzRMS at the time of this snapshot. Expressed as a percentage (0.00–100.00). Used to validate pricing decisions and benchmark against STR STAR Report actuals.']
  ota_rate_code decimal [note: 'The rate identifier as assigned by the primary OTA (Online Travel Agency) partner (e.g., Expedia, Booking.com) for this rate plan and property combination. Used for rate parity monitoring, OTA reconciliation, and channel performance reporting.']
  out_of_order_rooms varchar [note: 'Number of rooms of this room type that are out of order (OOO) on the snapshot date due to maintenance, renovation, or damage. Out-of-order rooms are excluded from sellable inventory and impact OCC denominator calculations per USALI standards.']
  pickup_rooms varchar [note: 'Number of rooms booked (picked up) for the snapshot date since the previous snapshot capture. Pickup velocity is a key revenue management signal used in IDeaS G3 RMS and Infor EzRMS to detect demand acceleration and trigger dynamic rate adjustments.']
  pricing_override_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the current rate for this snapshot was manually overridden by a revenue manager, superseding the automated recommendation from IDeaS G3 RMS or Infor EzRMS. Manual overrides are tracked for revenue strategy audit and RMS model calibration.']
  pricing_override_reason varchar [note: 'Free-text or coded reason provided by the revenue manager when manually overriding the RMS-recommended rate. Populated only when pricing_override_flag is True. Used for revenue strategy review, RMS model improvement, and audit trail compliance.']
  rack_rate decimal(10,2) [note: 'The published full undiscounted rate (rack rate) for this room type and stay date. Serves as the reference rate for discount calculations, loyalty redemption valuations, and walk-in pricing. Typically the highest rate tier and the baseline for USALI revenue reporting.']
  rate_parity_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this rate record is subject to rate parity obligations with OTA (Online Travel Agency) partners. When True, the rate must match or be lower than rates published on OTA channels. Critical for OTA contract compliance and channel distribution management.']
  rate_plan_code varchar [note: 'Alphanumeric code identifying the rate plan as distributed via Sabre SynXis CRS and IDeaS G3 RMS (e.g., BAR, CORP01, PKG_BB, NRR_ADV21). Used for channel distribution, GDS mapping, and OTA rate loading.']
  rate_plan_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the rate plan governing this availability record. Determines pricing logic, cancellation policy, and channel eligibility. BAR (Best Available Rate) = dynamic public rate; LRA (Last Room Availability) = guaranteed availability; NRR (Non-Refundable Rate) = prepaid non-cancellable; corporate = negotiated account rate; package = bundled inclusions; group = block rate; loyalty = member rate; promotional = limited-time offer; wholesale = OTA/tour operator net rate. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: bar|lra|nrr|corporate|package|group|loyalty|promotional|wholesale — promote to reference product]']
  record_status varchar
  revenue_management_system decimal(18,2) [note: 'Identifies the Revenue Management System (RMS) that generated or last updated the pricing recommendation for this snapshot record. Supports data lineage tracking and system-of-record attribution for audit and reconciliation purposes.']
  snapshot_date date [note: 'The stay date (arrival night) for which this rate and availability record applies. Represents the business event date — the night a guest would occupy the room at the stated rate. Core dimension for RevPAR and ADR reporting.']
  source_system_record_reference varchar [note: 'The native record identifier from the originating source system (IDeaS G3 RMS or Sabre SynXis CRS) for this rate and availability record. Enables traceability back to the system of record for reconciliation, reprocessing, and audit purposes.']
  stop_sell boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this room type and rate plan combination has been closed to all new bookings on the snapshot date regardless of available inventory. A hard yield management control applied in IDeaS G3 RMS to protect inventory for higher-value bookings or group blocks.']
  total_rooms varchar [note: 'Total physical room count for this room type at the property on the snapshot date. Used as the denominator for occupancy rate (OCC) and RevPAR calculations. Reflects the property\'s sellable capacity before any restrictions.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp indicating when the record was last updated']

  Note: 'Daily rate and availability snapshot per property, room type, and rate plan combination as managed in IDeaS G3 RMS and distributed via Sabre SynXis CRS. Captures open/closed status, available inventory count, current BAR, minimum and maximum rates, and last-updated timestamp. Represents the real-time pricing grid used for reservation fulfillment and channel distribution.'
}

Table revenue.demand_forecast {
  demand_forecast_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique surrogate identifier for each demand forecast record generated by IDeaS G3 RMS or Infor EzRMS. Primary key for the demand_forecast data product in the Databricks Silver Layer.']
  currency_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.currency. Business justification: Projected ADR, RevPAR, and room revenue in demand_forecast are currency-denominated. currency_code is denormalized; FK to currency enforces 3NF and enables accurate multi-currency forecast consolidati']
  event_booking_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to event.event_booking. Business justification: Demand forecasts incorporate known definite event bookings as constrained demand drivers. Critical for pickup forecasting, unconstrained vs constrained demand modeling, and event impact analysis in re']
  forecasted_revenue_center_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to fnb.revenue_center. Business justification: Revenue center-level F&B demand forecasting (covers, revenue, labor hours by bar/restaurant/banquet) is a standard hotel operations process for staffing and procurement planning. demand_forecast links']
  market_segment_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the market segment (e.g., Transient, Group, Corporate, Leisure, OTA) for which the demand forecast is generated. Null when the forecast is at the property or room-type level only.']
  promotion_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.promotion. Business justification: Demand forecasters explicitly adjust unconstrained demand upward when a loyalty promotion (e.g., bonus-points weekend) is active. Without this FK, the forecast model cannot programmatically identify w']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the hotel or resort property for which this demand forecast was generated. Aligns with the Oracle OPERA PMS property master.']
  room_type_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the specific room type (e.g., King Deluxe, Double Standard, Suite) for which the demand forecast is generated. Null when the forecast is at the property or market-segment level only.']
  seasonal_calendar_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.seasonal_calendar. Business justification: demand_forecast has is_holiday, is_special_event, special_event_name flags that duplicate seasonal_calendar data. Linking to seasonal_calendar enables RMS to automatically apply holiday/event demand u']
  ari_forecast decimal(8,4) [note: 'Forecasted Average Rate Index (ARI), representing the property\'s projected ADR relative to the competitive set\'s projected ADR. An ARI above 1.0 indicates the property is expected to achieve a rate premium over its competitive set.']
  booking_pace_index decimal(8,4) [note: 'Ratio of current bookings on-hand for the forecast date compared to the same point in time in the prior year or baseline period. A value above 1.0 indicates ahead-of-pace demand; below 1.0 indicates behind-pace. Used by revenue managers to assess demand trajectory.']
  confidence_interval_lower decimal(10,2) [note: 'Lower bound of the statistical confidence interval for the unconstrained demand forecast. Represents the pessimistic demand scenario used for risk-adjusted pricing and inventory control decisions in IDeaS G3 RMS.']
  confidence_interval_upper decimal(10,2) [note: 'Upper bound of the statistical confidence interval for the unconstrained demand forecast. Represents the optimistic demand scenario used for overbooking strategy and group evaluation in IDeaS G3 RMS.']
  confidence_level_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Statistical confidence level (e.g., 90.00, 95.00) associated with the forecast confidence interval. Indicates the probability that actual demand will fall within the lower and upper confidence bounds.']
  constrained_demand decimal(10,2) [note: 'The forecasted room demand (in room-nights) after applying available inventory capacity constraints. Represents the demand the property can actually accommodate. Used for occupancy projection and revenue optimization.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this demand forecast record was first captured and written to the Silver Layer data product. Used for audit trail and data lineage tracking.']
  day_of_week bigint [note: 'Day of the week corresponding to the forecast date. Used for day-of-week demand pattern analysis, weekend vs. weekday segmentation, and pricing strategy differentiation. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: Monday|Tuesday|Wednesday|Thursday|Friday|Saturday|Sunday — 7 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  demand_segment_mix_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Forecasted percentage share of total demand attributed to the specific market segment in this record. For example, if the Transient segment is expected to represent 65% of total demand on the forecast date, this field holds 65.00. Populated only for market-segment-level forecasts.']
  forecast_accuracy_mape decimal(8,4) [note: 'Mean Absolute Percentage Error (MAPE) of the forecast model for this property-segment-horizon combination, based on historical back-testing. Lower values indicate higher model accuracy. Used to weight forecast confidence and flag low-accuracy forecasts for revenue manager review.']
  forecast_date date [note: 'The stay date (arrival date) for which the demand forecast values apply. Represents the future date being predicted, formatted as yyyy-MM-dd.']
  forecast_granularity varchar [note: 'The dimensional level at which this forecast record is generated. \'property\' is the highest level; \'room_type_segment\' is the most granular, combining room type and market segment dimensions as supported by IDeaS G3 RMS.']
  forecast_horizon_days varchar [note: 'Number of days from the forecast run date to the forecast date, representing how far into the future this forecast projects. For example, a forecast run on 2024-01-01 for a stay date of 2024-04-01 has a horizon of 90 days. Used to assess forecast accuracy by horizon bucket.']
  forecast_model_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the algorithmic approach used to generate the forecast. \'time_series\' uses historical booking patterns; \'regression\' uses demand drivers; \'machine_learning\' uses ML-based models; \'hybrid\' combines multiple approaches; \'manual_override\' indicates a revenue manager manually adjusted the system forecast.']
  forecast_model_version varchar [note: 'Version identifier of the demand forecasting model or algorithm used to generate this forecast record (e.g., \'IDeaS-G3-v8.2\', \'EzRMS-v5.1\'). Enables model performance tracking, A/B comparison, and audit of forecast methodology changes.']
  forecast_run_reference varchar [note: 'Externally-known unique identifier assigned by the Revenue Management System (RMS) to the specific forecast generation run that produced this record. Enables traceability back to the originating RMS batch or on-demand run.']
  forecast_run_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this forecast record was generated by the Revenue Management System. Represents the principal business event timestamp for this transaction, formatted as yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss.SSSXXX.']
  forecast_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle state of this forecast record. \'active\' indicates the current operative forecast; \'superseded\' indicates a newer run has replaced it; \'draft\' indicates a preliminary run not yet published to pricing decisions; \'published\' indicates the forecast has been released to the Revenue Management System for pricing action; \'archived\' indicates historical retention only.']
  forecast_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the forecast methodology or purpose. \'unconstrained\' reflects true market demand without inventory limits; \'constrained\' reflects demand limited by available inventory; \'group_evaluation\' is used for group block assessment in IDeaS G3 RMS; \'pickup\' reflects incremental booking pace; \'budget\' reflects the annual budget forecast baseline.']
  is_holiday boolean [note: 'Flag indicating whether the forecast date falls on a public or national holiday in the property\'s market. Used to apply holiday demand adjustment factors in the forecasting model.']
  is_override boolean [note: 'Flag indicating whether a revenue manager manually overrode the system-generated forecast values for this record. When true, the forecast reflects human judgment rather than pure algorithmic output. Used to track override frequency and assess model trust.']
  is_special_event boolean [note: 'Flag indicating whether the forecast date coincides with a special event (e.g., conference, concert, sporting event, public holiday) that is expected to materially impact demand. When true, the forecast may incorporate event-specific demand uplift factors.']
  mpi_forecast decimal(8,4) [note: 'Forecasted Market Penetration Index (MPI), representing the property\'s projected occupancy share relative to the competitive set\'s projected occupancy. An MPI above 1.0 indicates the property is expected to capture more than its fair share of market demand.']
  projected_adr decimal(18,2) [note: 'Forecasted Average Daily Rate (ADR) in the property\'s local currency for the forecast date. Represents the expected average revenue per occupied room. Core revenue management KPI used to drive pricing strategy.']
  projected_cancellations decimal(10,2) [note: 'Forecasted number of room-nights expected to cancel from the current on-books position before the forecast date. Used to calculate net demand and inform overbooking strategy.']
  projected_no_shows decimal(10,2) [note: 'Forecasted number of room-nights expected to result in no-show arrivals on the forecast date. Used alongside cancellation forecasts to calibrate overbooking levels and protect revenue.']
  projected_occupancy_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Forecasted occupancy rate expressed as a percentage of available rooms expected to be sold on the forecast date. Calculated as constrained demand divided by total available rooms. Key input to RevPAR and yield optimization decisions.']
  projected_pickup decimal(10,2) [note: 'Forecasted incremental room-nights expected to be booked between the forecast run date and the forecast date. Represents the additional demand the RMS expects to materialize beyond rooms already on books.']
  projected_revpar decimal(18,2) [note: 'Forecasted Revenue Per Available Room (RevPAR) in the property\'s local currency for the forecast date. Derived as projected ADR multiplied by projected occupancy rate. Primary yield optimization metric used by Revenue Management.']
  projected_room_revenue decimal(18,2) [note: 'Forecasted total room revenue in the property\'s local currency for the forecast date. Calculated as projected rooms sold multiplied by projected ADR. Used for budget variance analysis and revenue strategy.']
  projected_rooms_available varchar [note: 'Forecasted number of rooms available for sale on the forecast date after accounting for out-of-order, out-of-service, and maintenance blocks. Denominator for occupancy and RevPAR calculations.']
  projected_rooms_sold varchar [note: 'Forecasted number of rooms expected to be sold (occupied) on the forecast date. Used for housekeeping scheduling, staffing planning, and inventory control decisions.']
  record_status varchar
  rgi_forecast decimal(8,4) [note: 'Forecasted Revenue Generation Index (RGI), representing the property\'s projected RevPAR relative to the competitive set\'s projected RevPAR. An RGI above 1.0 indicates the property is expected to outperform its competitive set. Sourced from STR STAR Report benchmarking data integrated into Infor EzRMS.']
  rooms_on_books varchar [note: 'Number of rooms already confirmed (on books) for the forecast date at the time the forecast was generated. Represents the definite demand component; the RMS adds pickup forecast to arrive at total projected demand.']
  special_event_name varchar [note: 'Name or description of the special event influencing demand on the forecast date (e.g., \'Super Bowl LIX\', \'New Year Eve\', \'City Marathon\'). Populated only when is_special_event is true.']
  unconstrained_demand decimal(10,2) [note: 'The total forecasted room demand (in room-nights) without any inventory capacity constraints applied. Represents true market demand as estimated by the RMS model. Used to identify demand compression and inform inventory control decisions.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this demand forecast record was last modified in the Silver Layer, such as when a revised forecast supersedes a prior run for the same forecast date and segment.']

  Note: 'Forward-looking demand forecast records generated by IDeaS G3 RMS and Infor EzRMS at the property, room type, and market segment level. Captures forecast date, forecast horizon, unconstrained demand, constrained demand, projected occupancy, projected ADR, projected RevPAR, forecast confidence interval, and forecast model version. Used to drive pricing decisions, inventory controls, and group evaluation.'
}
