  inventory_control_id varchar [pk, note: 'Primary key for inventory_control']
  currency_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.currency. Business justification: Inventory control hurdle rates and current BAR values are currency-denominated. currency_code is denormalized; FK to currency enforces 3NF and ensures correct currency context for sell-limit and overb']
  demand_forecast_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to revenue.demand_forecast. Business justification: Inventory control records in IDeaS G3 RMS and Infor EzRMS are governed by demand forecasts — the hurdle rate, sell limit, and overbooking parameters are set based on forecasted demand. Adding demand_f']
  distribution_channel_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.channel. Business justification: Inventory controls (sell limits, hurdles, stop-sells) vary by channel. Revenue managers allocate inventory differently across direct, OTA, GDS channels based on profitability and strategy. Fundamental']
  dynamic_rate_rule_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the Dynamic Rate Rule (DRR) applied to derive the current_bar for this room type and stay date. Links to the pricing strategy configuration governing automated rate adjustments in IDeaS G3 RMS.']
  event_booking_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to event.event_booking. Business justification: Inventory controls (sell limits, hurdle rates, overbooking caps) are adjusted based on event booking displacement analysis. Essential for inventory optimization around events and group block allocatio']
  primary_inventory_property_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the property (hotel, resort, or vacation property) to which this inventory control record applies. Aligns with Oracle OPERA PMS property configuration and IDeaS G3 RMS property setup.']
  revenue_rate_plan_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the rate plan (e.g., BAR, LRA, NRR, corporate, package) associated with this inventory control record. Determines the pricing tier and restrictions applied to the available inventory.']
  room_type_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the specific room type (e.g., King Deluxe, Double Standard, Suite) for which this inventory control record is defined. Aligns with Oracle OPERA PMS room type configuration and IDeaS G3 RMS room class setup.']
  allotment_rooms varchar [note: 'Number of rooms of this room type on the stay date allocated to contracted allotments (OTA allotments, wholesale, tour operator contracts). Managed via Sabre SynXis CRS channel management and reduces the freely-sellable transient inventory.']
  approval_authority varchar [note: 'Designates the level of authority required to approve the overbooking level for this inventory control record. Ensures governance and accountability for overbooking decisions per property SOPs and SOX internal control requirements.']
  available_room_count varchar [note: 'Real-time count of rooms available for sale for this property, room type, stay date, and rate plan combination at the time of last update. Reflects physical inventory minus confirmed reservations, group blocks, and out-of-order rooms. Distributed via Sabre SynXis CRS for reservation fulfillment.']
  control_record_code varchar [note: 'Externally-known alphanumeric business identifier for this inventory control record as referenced in IDeaS G3 RMS and Sabre SynXis CRS. Used for cross-system reconciliation and audit traceability.']
  control_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle state of this inventory control record indicating whether the room type/rate plan combination is open for sale, closed, restricted, pending review, or subject to a manual override. This is the real-time availability state distributed via Sabre SynXis CRS.']
  control_type varchar [note: 'Classifies the category of inventory control applied to this record. Determines how the control_value is interpreted and enforced by the Revenue Management System. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: hurdle_rate|sell_limit|overbooking_level|los_restriction|cta_restriction|ctd_restriction|allotment|group_block — promote to reference product]']
  control_value decimal(18,4) [note: 'The operative value for this control record as applied by the Revenue Management System. Interpretation depends on control_type: for hurdle_rate it is the minimum acceptable rate in local currency; for sell_limit it is the maximum rooms to sell; for overbooking_level it is the number of rooms above physical capacity authorized to sell.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this inventory control record was first created in the source Revenue Management System (IDeaS G3 RMS or Infor EzRMS). Provides the audit trail creation anchor for data lineage and SOX compliance.']
  current_bar decimal(10,2) [note: 'The current Best Available Rate (BAR) in local currency for this room type and stay date as published via Sabre SynXis CRS and channel distribution. Represents the lowest publicly available non-restricted rate and is the primary pricing signal for transient demand.']
  effective_from_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time from which this inventory control record\'s control_value and restrictions became operative in the Revenue Management System. Supports temporal validity tracking and historical rate/availability grid reconstruction.']
  effective_until_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time at which this inventory control record\'s control_value and restrictions ceased to be operative. Null for currently active records. Enables point-in-time historical analysis of the rate/availability grid.']
  group_block_rooms varchar [note: 'Number of rooms of this room type on the stay date allocated to group blocks (MICE, tour groups, corporate groups). Reduces the transient sell limit and is managed via Delphi by Amadeus group block management and IDeaS G3 RMS group evaluation.']
  hurdle_rate decimal(10,2) [note: 'Minimum acceptable rate (in local currency) below which a reservation for this room type on the stay date should not be accepted, as determined by the Revenue Management System. Used in displacement analysis and group evaluation in IDeaS G3 RMS.']
  is_closed_to_arrival boolean [note: 'Indicates whether arrivals are blocked for this room type and rate plan on the stay date (Closed to Arrival / CTA restriction). When True, guests may not check in on this date but may stay through it as part of a longer booking.']
  is_closed_to_departure boolean [note: 'Indicates whether departures are blocked for this room type and rate plan on the stay date (Closed to Departure / CTD restriction). When True, guests may not check out on this date, requiring stays to extend beyond it.']
  is_override boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the applied control_value represents a manual override of the system_recommended_value. True when a revenue manager has manually intervened; False when the system recommendation was accepted as-is. Critical for RMS model performance auditing.']
  last_distributed_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this inventory control record\'s rate and availability state was last successfully distributed to Sabre SynXis CRS and downstream channels (OTA, GDS). Critical for SLA monitoring and channel distribution reconciliation.']
  max_los varchar [note: 'Maximum number of nights a guest may stay when booking this room type at this rate plan on the stay date. Used to prevent long-stay displacement of higher-value transient demand during peak periods.']
  max_rate decimal(10,2) [note: 'The ceiling rate in local currency above which no rate plan for this room type and stay date may be sold. Used to enforce rate integrity, prevent rate gouging, and comply with local pricing regulations during high-demand periods.']
  min_los varchar [note: 'Minimum number of nights a guest must stay to be eligible to book this room type at this rate plan on the stay date. A Length of Stay (LOS) restriction used to optimize revenue during high-demand periods by requiring longer stays.']
  min_rate decimal(10,2) [note: 'The absolute floor rate in local currency below which no rate plan for this room type and stay date may be sold, regardless of channel or negotiated agreement. Enforced as a hard constraint in the Revenue Management System and CRS.']
  occupancy_on_books decimal(5,2) [note: 'Current confirmed occupancy rate (OCC) percentage for this room type on the stay date at the time of last update, calculated as confirmed reservations divided by physical_room_count. Key input to dynamic pricing and sell limit decisions in the Revenue Management System.']
  out_of_order_rooms varchar [note: 'Number of rooms of this room type on the stay date designated as out of order (OOO) due to maintenance, renovation, or FF&E replacement. These rooms are excluded from sellable inventory and occupancy calculations per USALI standards.']
  overbooking_absolute_cap varchar [note: 'Hard ceiling on the absolute number of rooms that may be overbooked above physical capacity for this room type on the stay date, regardless of the overbooking_pct calculation. Prevents excessive walk exposure during high-demand periods.']
  overbooking_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Maximum authorized overbooking level expressed as a percentage above physical room capacity for this room type on the stay date. Defined in the overbooking policy and used by IDeaS G3 RMS to set the sell limit above physical_room_count.']
  override_reason varchar [note: 'Free-text or coded justification provided by the revenue manager when is_override is True. Documents the business rationale for deviating from the system recommendation (e.g., local event, competitive action, group displacement). Required for audit and RMS calibration.']
  physical_room_count varchar [note: 'Total number of physical rooms of this room type at the property, representing the hard capacity ceiling before overbooking allowances are applied. Used as the denominator for occupancy rate (OCC) calculations.']
  rate_availability_source varchar [note: 'Identifies the originating system or process that set the current rate and availability state for this control record. Supports data lineage, audit, and reconciliation between IDeaS G3 RMS, Sabre SynXis CRS, and Oracle OPERA PMS.']
  record_status varchar
  sell_limit varchar [note: 'Maximum number of rooms authorized to be sold for this room type on the stay date, inclusive of overbooking allowance. Set by the Revenue Management System and may exceed physical_room_count when overbooking is authorized. Enforced at the CRS and PMS booking engine.']
  stay_date date [note: 'The specific calendar date (night of stay) for which this inventory control record applies. Represents the primary dimension of the rate/availability grid alongside property, room type, and rate plan.']
  system_recommended_value decimal(18,4) [note: 'The value recommended by the Revenue Management System (IDeaS G3 RMS or Infor EzRMS) prior to any manual override. Enables comparison between algorithmic recommendation and the applied control_value for yield optimization analysis and RMS model performance tracking.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this inventory control record was most recently modified in the source system. Used for incremental ETL processing, change detection, and audit trail maintenance in the Databricks Silver Layer.']
  walk_compensation_type varchar [note: 'Type of compensation offered to a walked guest when the walk_policy requires compensation. Governs the financial and loyalty implications of overbooking execution and is tracked for Guest Recovery Rate (GRR) and CPOR reporting.']
  walk_policy varchar [note: 'Defines the operational procedure to follow when a guest with a confirmed reservation cannot be accommodated due to overbooking (a \'walk\'). Determines whether the guest is walked to a partner hotel, upgraded, or compensated per AHLA guest relocation standards.']

  Note: 'Inventory control records managing the complete room availability and pricing grid as applied in IDeaS G3 RMS. Encompasses hurdle rates, sell limits, overbooking levels, room type allotments, group blocks, and the resulting daily rate availability state per property, room type, and rate plan combination. Captures control type, room type, stay date, control value, system-recommended value, override indicator, overbooking policy parameters (max overbooking percentage, absolute cap, walk policy, compensation type, partner hotel agreements, approval authority), and real-time availability state (open/closed status, available inventory count, current BAR, minimum/maximum rates, last-updated timestamp). This is the SSOT for all inventory control decisions, overbooking policy configuration, and the rate/availability grid distributed via Sabre SynXis CRS for reservation fulfillment and channel distribution.'
}

Table revenue.performance_actuals {
  performance_actuals_id varchar [pk, note: 'Primary key for performance_actuals']
  budget_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to revenue.revenue_budget. Business justification: Performance actuals carry denormalized budget targets (budget_adr, budget_occupancy_rate, budget_room_revenue, budget_total_revenue) for variance computation. Adding revenue_budget_id normalizes these']
  currency_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.currency. Business justification: All performance_actuals monetary KPIs (ADR, RevPAR, GOP, EBITDA) are currency-denominated. currency_code is denormalized; FK to currency enforces 3NF and is required for STR benchmarking, owner report']
  demand_forecast_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to revenue.demand_forecast. Business justification: Performance actuals are compared against demand forecasts for MAPE (forecast accuracy) and variance analysis — a core function of IDeaS G3 RMS and STR STAR reporting. Adding demand_forecast_id links e']
  event_booking_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to event.event_booking. Business justification: Daily actuals track which room nights and revenue came from specific event bookings for segment reporting. Required for event contribution analysis, MICE segment performance reporting, and group vs tr']
  franchise_agreement_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.franchise_agreement. Business justification: Franchise fee calculations (royalty, marketing, loyalty fees) are computed from performance actuals revenue figures. Linking performance_actuals to franchise_agreement enables automated franchise fee ']
  hierarchy_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.hierarchy. Business justification: Performance actuals are reported and benchmarked at hierarchy node levels (brand, region, cluster) for executive dashboards and STR market reporting. Linking to hierarchy enables hierarchical KPI roll']
  primary_fnb_outlet_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to fnb.fnb_outlet. Business justification: Daily actuals track outlet-level F&B revenue for TRevPAR calculation and USALI reporting. Required for total property revenue reporting, GOP analysis, outlet performance attribution in consolidated fi']
  promotion_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.promotion. Business justification: Promotion ROI / lift analysis is a named loyalty reporting process: did the double-points weekend actually lift RevPAR? Linking performance_actuals to the active promotion enables incremental revenue ']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the property for which this daily revenue performance record is captured. Links to the property master entity in the Property domain.']
  revenue_center_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to fnb.revenue_center. Business justification: USALI mandates F&B performance reporting by revenue center (restaurant, bar, banquet). performance_actuals tracks fb_revenue but has no revenue_center FK. This link enables department-level P&L report']
  seasonal_calendar_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.seasonal_calendar. Business justification: Performance actuals must be contextualized by season for meaningful YoY variance analysis (prior_year_revpar exists as a plain attr). Linking to seasonal_calendar enables season-adjusted STR benchmark']
  adr decimal(18,2) [note: 'Average Daily Rate in the property\'s operating currency, calculated as total room revenue divided by rooms sold (excluding complimentary). Core KPI for STR STAR Report benchmarking, RGI, ARI, and MPI calculations.']
  ancillary_revenue decimal(18,2) [note: 'Total ancillary revenue on the performance date from upsells, packages, resort fees, and add-on services not captured in departmental revenue lines. Supports total revenue and TRevPAR reporting.']
  ari decimal(6,4) [note: 'Average Rate Index representing the property\'s ADR performance relative to its competitive set, sourced from STR STAR Report. ARI > 1.0 indicates the property is achieving a rate premium over its comp set.']
  channel_direct_rooms varchar [note: 'Number of rooms sold through direct channels (brand website, call center, walk-in) on the performance date. Supports direct vs. indirect channel mix analysis and cost-of-acquisition reporting.']
  channel_ota_rooms varchar [note: 'Number of rooms sold through Online Travel Agency (OTA) channels (e.g., Expedia, Booking.com) on the performance date. Supports channel distribution mix analysis and OTA commission cost management.']
  cpor decimal(10,2) [note: 'Cost Per Occupied Room on the performance date, calculated as total rooms department operating expenses divided by rooms sold. Measures operational efficiency of the rooms department per USALI.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this performance actual record was first created in the data lakehouse Silver layer. Supports audit trail and data lineage requirements.']
  ebitda_contribution decimal(14,2) [note: 'Property-level EBITDA contribution on the performance date, representing operating earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation, and amortization. Used for ownership reporting, asset valuation, and management contract performance measurement.']
  fb_revenue decimal(18,2) [note: 'Total Food and Beverage revenue generated on the performance date across all F&B outlets (restaurants, bars, banquets, in-room dining). Sourced from Oracle Hospitality MICROS POS and reconciled against SAP S/4HANA. Included in TRevPAR calculation per USALI.']
  gop decimal(14,2) [note: 'Gross Operating Profit on the performance date, calculated as total operated department revenue minus total operated department expenses per USALI. Key profitability metric for ownership reporting and management contracts.']
  goppar decimal(10,2) [note: 'Gross Operating Profit Per Available Room in the property\'s operating currency, calculated as GOP divided by rooms available. Measures overall property profitability efficiency. Core KPI for ownership reporting and management fee calculations.']
  is_reconciled boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this daily performance actual record has been reconciled between Oracle OPERA PMS and SAP S/4HANA General Ledger. True = reconciled and approved for reporting; False = pending reconciliation. Supports financial close and SOX controls.']
  miscellaneous_income decimal(14,2) [note: 'Total miscellaneous and rental income on the performance date including rentals, commissions, and other non-departmental income per USALI non-operating income classification.']
  mpi decimal(6,4) [note: 'Market Penetration Index representing the property\'s occupancy performance relative to its competitive set, sourced from STR STAR Report. MPI > 1.0 indicates the property is capturing more than its fair share of market occupancy.']
  occupancy_rate decimal(5,4) [note: 'Daily occupancy rate expressed as a decimal (e.g., 0.8250 = 82.50%), calculated as rooms sold divided by rooms available. Core KPI for the STR STAR Report, DOR, and ownership reporting. Stored as a raw ratio; display layer applies percentage formatting.']
  parking_revenue decimal(18,2) [note: 'Total parking revenue generated on the performance date from valet, self-park, and garage operations. Classified under other operated departments per USALI and included in TRevPAR.']
  performance_date date [note: 'The calendar date (business date) for which this revenue performance actual record applies. Represents the stay date or operating day used in the Daily Operations Report (DOR) and all KPI calculations.']
  prior_year_revpar decimal(18,2) [note: 'RevPAR for the same calendar date in the prior year. Used for year-over-year (YOY) variance analysis in the DOR, STR STAR Report benchmarking, and ownership reporting.']
  record_status varchar [note: 'Lifecycle status of this performance actual record indicating whether figures are preliminary (intra-day), final (end-of-day close), adjusted (post-close correction), or closed (period-locked). Supports audit and reconciliation workflows.']
  revpar decimal(18,2) [note: 'Revenue Per Available Room in the property\'s operating currency, calculated as ADR multiplied by occupancy rate (or total room revenue divided by rooms available). Primary rooms revenue KPI for ownership reporting, STR STAR Report, and RGI benchmarking.']
  rgi decimal(6,4) [note: 'Revenue Generation Index representing the property\'s RevPAR performance relative to its competitive set, sourced from STR STAR Report. RGI > 1.0 indicates the property is outperforming its comp set. Core competitive benchmarking KPI.']
  rooms_available varchar [note: 'Total number of rooms available for sale on the performance date after deducting out-of-order (OOO) and out-of-service (OOS) rooms. Denominator for Occupancy Rate (OCC) and RevPAR calculations per USALI and STR STAR Report standards.']
  rooms_complimentary varchar [note: 'Number of rooms occupied on a complimentary (no-charge) basis on the performance date. Tracked separately per USALI for accurate ADR and revenue reporting, as complimentary rooms are excluded from ADR calculation.']
  rooms_out_of_order varchar [note: 'Number of rooms designated as out-of-order (OOO) on the performance date due to maintenance, renovation, or damage. Excluded from rooms available per USALI inventory standards.']
  rooms_sold varchar [note: 'Total number of rooms occupied (sold) on the performance date, including complimentary rooms. Used to calculate Occupancy Rate (OCC) and Average Daily Rate (ADR) per USALI standards.']
  segment_contract_rooms varchar [note: 'Number of rooms sold under negotiated contract rates (airline crew, long-stay corporate contracts) on the performance date. Supports contract segment revenue analysis and channel mix reporting.']
  segment_group_rooms varchar [note: 'Number of rooms sold to group accounts (MICE, corporate groups, tour groups) on the performance date. Supports group vs. transient mix analysis and group revenue contribution reporting per USALI.']
  segment_transient_rooms varchar [note: 'Number of rooms sold to transient (individual/FIT) guests on the performance date. Supports segment-level revenue analysis and channel mix reporting per USALI market segmentation standards.']
  source_system_code varchar [note: 'Identifies the operational system of record from which this performance actual record was sourced or reconciled (e.g., Oracle OPERA PMS for rooms data, SAP S/4HANA for financial totals). Supports data lineage and reconciliation audits.']
  spa_revenue decimal(18,2) [note: 'Total spa and wellness revenue generated on the performance date. Included in total property revenue and TRevPAR calculation per USALI other operated departments classification.']
  total_property_revenue decimal(18,2) [note: 'Total gross revenue across all operated departments and income streams on the performance date (rooms + F&B + spa + parking + other operated departments + miscellaneous + ancillary). Denominator basis for TRevPAR. Reconciled against SAP S/4HANA GL per USALI.']
  total_room_revenue decimal(18,2) [note: 'Total gross room revenue generated on the performance date across all rate plans and channels, before deductions. Sourced from Oracle OPERA PMS and reconciled against SAP S/4HANA GL. Numerator for ADR and RevPAR calculations per USALI.']
  trevpar decimal(18,2) [note: 'Total Revenue Per Available Room in the property\'s operating currency, calculated as total property revenue divided by rooms available. Measures total revenue productivity of the property beyond rooms. Core KPI for ownership and management reporting.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this performance actual record was last modified, including post-close adjustments or reconciliation corrections. Supports audit trail and change tracking.']

  Note: 'Daily revenue performance actuals at the property level capturing all revenue streams aligned to USALI departmental reporting. Includes room revenue metrics (ADR, OCC, RevPAR, rooms sold, rooms available, total room revenue) and total property revenue metrics (F&B revenue, spa revenue, parking, other operated departments, miscellaneous income, ancillary revenue, TRevPAR, GOPPAR, CPOR, GOP, EBITDA contribution). Sourced from Oracle OPERA PMS and SAP S/4HANA, reconciled against USALI standards. This is the single authoritative record for all daily revenue performance — both rooms and total revenue — used for the Daily Operations Report (DOR), ownership reporting, TRevPAR/GOPPAR calculation, and variance analysis against budget.'
}

Table revenue.market_segment {
  market_segment_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique surrogate identifier for the market segment record. Primary key for the market_segment data product in the revenue domain. Role classification: MASTER_RESOURCE — this entity represents a classification resource used across revenue, reservation, and channel domains.']
  currency_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.currency. Business justification: Market segment commission rates and contribution margin tiers are currency-context-dependent. currency_code is denormalized; FK to currency enforces 3NF and supports multi-currency segment profitabili']
  ada_accommodation_typical boolean [note: 'Indicates whether guests in this market segment typically require ADA (Americans with Disabilities Act) accessible accommodations. Relevant for government, medical, and certain group segments. Informs room inventory allocation and accessibility compliance reporting.']
  avg_lead_time_days varchar [note: 'Average number of days between booking date and arrival date for this market segment. Key input for demand forecasting in IDeaS G3 RMS and Infor EzRMS. Segments with short lead times (e.g., OTA last-minute) require different yield strategies than long-lead corporate or group segments. Represents the MEASUREMENT_OR_VALUE for this resource.']
  avg_length_of_stay_nights decimal(5,2) [note: 'Average number of nights guests in this segment stay per booking (ALOS — Average Length of Stay). Used in revenue management for LOS (Length of Stay) restriction optimization, demand forecasting, and RevPAR (Revenue Per Available Room) modeling in IDeaS G3 RMS.']
  cancellation_propensity decimal(9,4) [note: 'Qualitative classification of the historical cancellation rate tendency for this market segment. Informs overbooking strategy, no-show reserve calculations, and revenue protection policies in IDeaS G3 RMS. High-propensity segments (e.g., OTA flexible rate) require higher overbooking buffers.']
  channel_affinity varchar [note: 'Primary distribution channel through which this market segment predominantly books. Drives channel strategy, OTA (Online Travel Agency) commission management, and GDS (Global Distribution System) rate loading decisions in Sabre SynXis CRS. Used for channel mix analysis and cost-of-acquisition reporting. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: direct|ota|gds|voice|group|wholesale|other — 7 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  commission_eligible decimal(18,2) [note: 'Indicates whether bookings in this segment are subject to travel agent or OTA commission payments. Direct corporate and government segments are typically non-commissionable; OTA and GDS segments carry commission obligations. Drives accounts payable commission processing in SAP S/4HANA.']
  commission_rate_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Standard commission rate percentage applicable to bookings in this segment when commission_eligible is true. Expressed as a percentage of room revenue (e.g., 10.00 for 10%). Used for cost-of-acquisition analysis, OTA contract management, and CPOR (Cost Per Occupied Room) calculations. Confidential as it reflects contracted commercial terms.']
  contribution_margin_tier varchar [note: 'Classification of the segment\'s typical contribution margin profile relative to other segments. Reflects net revenue after channel commissions, OTA fees, GDS fees, and loyalty redemption costs. Premium tiers (e.g., direct corporate) yield higher GOP (Gross Operating Profit) than low-margin OTA or wholesale segments. Used in GOPPAR analysis.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this market segment record was first created in the enterprise data lakehouse. Supports data lineage, audit trail, and record provenance tracking. Aligns with RECORD_AUDIT_CREATED requirement for MASTER_RESOURCE entities.']
  crs_segment_code varchar [note: 'The segment code as configured in Sabre SynXis CRS for central reservations and channel distribution. Used for rate plan distribution, availability controls, and channel-level segment reporting. Enables cross-system segment reconciliation.']
  demand_pattern varchar [note: 'Classification of the temporal demand pattern exhibited by this market segment. Corporate transient segments typically show weekday concentration; leisure segments show weekend and seasonal peaks; event-driven segments spike around MICE (Meetings Incentives Conferences Exhibitions) events. Used in Infor EzRMS demand forecasting.']
  description varchar [note: 'Detailed narrative description of the market segment, including its defining characteristics, typical guest profile, booking behavior, and applicable rate strategies. Used for training, documentation, and business glossary alignment across revenue management, reservations, and sales teams.']
  effective_from date [note: 'Date from which this market segment definition becomes active and available for use in reservations, rate plans, and revenue reporting. Supports temporal validity management for segment taxonomy changes aligned with fiscal year or STR reporting period updates.']
  effective_until date [note: 'Date after which this market segment definition is no longer active. Null indicates an open-ended segment with no planned expiry. Supports segment lifecycle management and historical reporting continuity when segment taxonomies are revised.']
  gdpr_data_subject_applicable boolean [note: 'Indicates whether guest data associated with bookings in this market segment is subject to GDPR data subject rights (right to erasure, portability, access). Relevant for segments involving EU/EEA guests. Drives data retention and anonymization policies in the data lakehouse.']
  gds_eligible boolean [note: 'Indicates whether rates for this market segment are distributed through GDS (Global Distribution System) channels such as Amadeus, Sabre, and Travelport. Controls rate loading and availability display in Sabre SynXis CRS for GDS-connected travel agencies.']
  group_block_eligible boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this market segment supports group room block reservations. Group-eligible segments (e.g., MICE, sports groups, tour groups) require group block management in Oracle OPERA PMS and Delphi by Amadeus for BEO (Banquet Event Order) coordination.']
  hierarchy_level varchar [note: 'Numeric level of this segment within the market segment hierarchy. Level 1 represents top-level categories (e.g., Transient, Group); Level 2 represents sub-categories (e.g., Corporate, Leisure); Level 3 represents granular segments (e.g., Corporate Negotiated, Leisure OTA). Used for hierarchical roll-up in revenue reporting.']
  is_internal_use_only boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this market segment is for internal reporting and analytics purposes only and should not be exposed to guests, OTA partners, or external distribution channels. Internal segments (e.g., complimentary, house use, employee rate) are excluded from external rate distribution in Sabre SynXis CRS.']
  loyalty_eligible boolean [note: 'Indicates whether bookings under this market segment are eligible to earn loyalty program points and benefits. Wholesale, crew, and certain contracted segments may be excluded from loyalty accrual per program rules. Drives loyalty point calculation logic in Salesforce CRM loyalty management.']
  market_segment_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the market segment record. Active segments are available for rate plan assignment, reservation coding, and revenue reporting. Inactive or deprecated segments are retained for historical analysis but excluded from new bookings. Aligns with MASTER_RESOURCE LIFECYCLE_STATUS requirement.']
  min_rate_override_allowed boolean [note: 'Indicates whether revenue managers are permitted to override the minimum rate floor for this segment. Restricting overrides for high-value segments (e.g., LRA corporate) protects rate integrity. Configurable in IDeaS G3 RMS inventory controls and Oracle OPERA PMS rate management.']
  negotiated_rate_required boolean [note: 'Indicates whether bookings in this segment require a pre-negotiated rate agreement (e.g., corporate account rate, government per diem, airline crew contract). When true, a valid rate agreement must exist before reservations can be accepted at segment rates in Oracle OPERA PMS.']
  no_show_propensity decimal(9,4) [note: 'Qualitative classification of the historical no-show rate tendency for this market segment. Distinct from cancellation propensity — no-shows occur without prior cancellation and have different revenue recovery implications. Used in overbooking model calibration within IDeaS G3 RMS.']
  ota_eligible boolean [note: 'Indicates whether rates for this market segment are distributed through OTA (Online Travel Agency) channels such as Expedia, Booking.com, and Hotels.com. Controls channel availability in Sabre SynXis CRS and impacts OTA commission cost tracking.']
  pci_scope boolean [note: 'Indicates whether payment card data associated with bookings in this segment falls within PCI DSS scope. Segments with direct card-present or card-not-present transactions require PCI-compliant data handling. Drives data masking and tokenization requirements in the lakehouse.']
  pms_segment_code varchar [note: 'The segment code as configured in Oracle OPERA PMS. Used for reservation coding, folio routing, and rate plan assignment at the property level. Enables reconciliation between the enterprise data lakehouse and the operational PMS source system.']
  price_sensitivity decimal(18,2) [note: 'Classification of the segment\'s sensitivity to rate changes. Inelastic segments (e.g., airline crew, government contracted) book regardless of rate fluctuations. Highly elastic segments (e.g., leisure OTA) respond strongly to price changes. Drives DRR (Dynamic Rate Rule) configuration in IDeaS G3 RMS.']
  rate_plan_category varchar [note: 'Classification of the rate plan type typically associated with this segment. BAR (Best Available Rate) for transient leisure, negotiated for corporate accounts, LRA (Last Room Availability) for top-tier corporate, NRR (Non-Refundable Rate) for advance purchase segments. Drives rate loading in Oracle OPERA PMS and Sabre SynXis CRS. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: bar|negotiated|lra|nrr|wholesale|package|complimentary — 7 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  record_status varchar
  revenue_bucket decimal(18,2) [note: 'Primary revenue category associated with this market segment for TRevPAR (Total Revenue Per Available Room) and USALI departmental reporting. Rooms-focused segments contribute primarily to rooms revenue; MICE segments contribute across rooms, F&B (Food and Beverage), and events revenue buckets.']
  rms_segment_code varchar [note: 'The segment code as configured in IDeaS G3 RMS or Infor EzRMS. Used for demand forecasting, pricing optimization, and inventory control at the segment level. May differ from PMS segment code due to system-specific taxonomy requirements.']
  segment_category varchar [note: 'High-level classification grouping the segment into a primary demand category. Drives pricing strategy, channel allocation, and revenue reporting roll-ups. Aligns with STR segment category definitions used in STAR Report benchmarking. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: transient|group|contract|wholesale|ota|corporate|government|leisure|crew|airline — promote to reference product]']
  segment_code varchar [note: 'Short alphanumeric code uniquely identifying the market segment, used as the externally-known business identifier across Oracle OPERA PMS, IDeaS G3 RMS, Sabre SynXis CRS, and Infor EzRMS. Examples: CORP, TRANS, LEIS, OTA, GRP, GOVT, CREW. Aligns with STR segment code taxonomy for benchmarking and STAR Report mapping.']
  segment_name varchar [note: 'Full descriptive name of the market segment as displayed in reporting, dashboards, and revenue management systems. Examples: Corporate Negotiated, Leisure Transient, Online Travel Agency, Government/Military, Group Meetings. Used as the IDENTITY_LABEL for this resource entity.']
  segment_type varchar [note: 'Secondary classification distinguishing whether the segment represents individual (FIT — Free Independent Traveler) bookings, group blocks, negotiated corporate accounts, wholesale/tour operator contracts, or consortia arrangements. Used in IDeaS G3 RMS for demand segmentation and pricing strategy.']
  sort_order varchar [note: 'Numeric value controlling the display sequence of market segments in reports, dashboards, and system configuration screens. Ensures consistent ordering in Oracle OPERA PMS segment lists, IDeaS G3 RMS segment configuration, and BI reporting tools.']
  str_segment_code varchar [note: 'The official STR (Smith Travel Research) segment code used for competitive benchmarking and STAR Report alignment. Enables mapping of internal segment definitions to the industry-standard STR taxonomy for RGI (Revenue Generation Index), MPI (Market Penetration Index), and ARI (Average Rate Index) calculations.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this market segment record was last modified. Tracks configuration changes to segment definitions, status updates, and taxonomy revisions. Essential for change data capture (CDC) in ETL pipelines feeding IDeaS G3 RMS and Infor EzRMS.']
  usali_segment_code varchar [note: 'The USALI (Uniform System of Accounts for the Lodging Industry) standardized segment code used for financial reporting and departmental P&L allocation. Ensures consistency in GOP (Gross Operating Profit), NOI (Net Operating Income), and EBITDA reporting across properties and for external financial audits under GAAP/IFRS.']

  Note: 'Master classification of revenue market segments used for demand analysis, pricing strategy, and performance reporting. Defines segment code, segment name, segment category (transient, group, contract, wholesale, OTA, corporate, government, leisure, crew, airline), contribution margin profile, booking behavior characteristics, average lead time, and cancellation propensity. SSOT for market segment taxonomy aligned to STR segment definitions and used across revenue, reservation, and channel domains.'
}

  budgeted_fnb_outlet_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to fnb.fnb_outlet. Business justification: Revenue budgets include outlet-level F&B targets for total property budget planning.   demand_forecast_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to revenue.demand_forecast. Business justification: Revenue budgets and strategic plans in hospitality are built on top of demand forecasts — the target_occupancy_rate, target_adr, and target_revpar in revenue_budget are derived from demand forecast pr']

Linking revenue_budget to hierarchy enables hierarchical budget rollup for regional VP review, brand portfol']
  market_segment_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the market segment (e.g., transient leisure, transient corporate, group, wholesale, OTA) for which this budget is defined. Enables segment-level revenue planning and variance analysis.']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the property for which this revenue budget applies. Links to the property master record in the Property domain.']
  revenue_center_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to fnb.revenue_center. Business justification: USALI standard hotel budgeting sets F&B targets at the revenue center level (e.g., restaurant vs. bar vs. banquet). revenue_budget has budgeted_fb_revenue but no revenue_center FK. This link supports ']
  seasonal_calendar_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.seasonal_calendar. Business justification: Revenue budgets are planned by season (peak, shoulder, off-peak). Linking revenue_budget to seasonal_calendar enables season-based budget variance reporting, supports annual planning cycles aligned to']
  approval_date date [note: 'The date on which the revenue director formally approved this budget version. Marks the transition from \'draft\' to \'approved\' strategy status.']
  budgeted_available_rooms varchar [note: 'Total number of room-nights planned to be available for sale during the planning period (capacity baseline). Used as the denominator for RevPAR, TRevPAR, and GOPPAR calculations and STR STAR Report benchmarking.']
  budgeted_cpor decimal(10,2) [note: 'Budgeted Cost Per Occupied Room (CPOR) in the property\'s operating currency, representing the planned direct operating cost per occupied room night. Used for profitability planning and variance analysis against actuals.']
  budgeted_events_revenue decimal(18,2) [note: 'Total budgeted revenue from Meetings, Incentives, Conferences, and Exhibitions (MICE) and event spaces for the planning period. Supports TRevPAR planning and event sales governance in Delphi by Amadeus.']
  budgeted_fb_revenue decimal(18,2) [note: 'Total budgeted Food and Beverage (F&B) revenue in the property\'s operating currency for the planning period. Supports TRevPAR planning and USALI departmental revenue reporting.']
  budgeted_gop decimal(15,2) [note: 'Budgeted Gross Operating Profit (GOP) in the property\'s operating currency for the planning period, per USALI departmental and undistributed expense structure. Used for GOPPAR derivation and owner NOI reporting.']
  budgeted_occupied_rooms varchar [note: 'Total number of room-nights planned to be occupied (sold) during the planning period. Derived from budgeted available rooms × target OCC, stored as a planning target for demand forecasting and group block management.']
  budgeted_other_revenue decimal(18,2) [note: 'Total budgeted ancillary revenue (spa, parking, resort fees, retail, etc.) in the property\'s operating currency for the planning period. Completes the TRevPAR revenue stack beyond rooms, F&B, and events.']
  budgeted_room_revenue decimal(18,2) [note: 'Total budgeted room revenue (in operating currency) for the planning period and market segment. The primary monetary commitment in the revenue budget, used for variance analysis against actuals in the DOR and management reporting. Classified confidential as a strategic financial target.']
  budgeted_total_revenue decimal(18,2) [note: 'Aggregate budgeted total revenue across all revenue streams (rooms + F&B + events + other) in the property\'s operating currency for the planning period. The top-line financial commitment used in owner presentations and EBITDA planning.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this revenue budget record was first created in the lakehouse Silver Layer. Supports audit trail, data lineage, and SOX financial controls compliance.']
  fiscal_period varchar [note: 'The fiscal month or period number (1–12) within the fiscal year for monthly budget granularity. Supports period-level variance analysis in the DOR and management reporting.']
  fiscal_year varchar [note: 'The fiscal year to which this revenue budget belongs (e.g., 2025). Aligns with the property\'s USALI-compliant financial reporting calendar and SAP S/4HANA GL fiscal periods.']
  is_owner_approved boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this budget has received formal approval from the property owner or ownership group (True = owner-approved; False = pending or not required). Relevant for managed properties where owner sign-off is contractually required.']
  key_tactical_actions varchar [note: 'Free-text description of the near-term tactical revenue actions planned for this budget period (e.g., BAR adjustments, LRA controls, OTA channel mix shifts, promotional rate activations). Captured from the revenue strategy narrative in IDeaS G3 RMS and Infor EzRMS.']
  notes varchar [note: 'Free-text field for additional context, assumptions, or commentary associated with this revenue budget record (e.g., macro-economic assumptions, renovation impact adjustments, force majeure notes). Supports management reporting and audit documentation.']
  planning_horizon_type varchar [note: 'Granularity of the planning horizon for this budget record: \'annual\' (full-year plan), \'quarterly\' (90-day rolling), \'monthly\' (period-level), or \'weekly\' (short-term tactical). Determines the reporting cadence for variance analysis.']
  planning_period_end_date date [note: 'The last date of the planning horizon covered by this revenue budget (e.g., 2025-12-31 for an annual plan). Defines the effective end of the budget period.']
  planning_period_start_date date [note: 'The first date of the planning horizon covered by this revenue budget (e.g., 2025-01-01 for an annual plan). Defines the effective start of the budget period for variance tracking against actuals.']
  property_segment varchar [note: 'Brand/service tier of the property for which this budget applies: \'luxury\', \'premium\', \'select_service\', or \'extended_stay\'. Enables cross-segment benchmarking and portfolio-level revenue governance.']
  record_status varchar
  reference_number bigint [note: 'Externally-known alphanumeric identifier for this budget record, used in management reports, owner presentations, and cross-system references (e.g., SAP S/4HANA GL budget entries). Format: RB-{PropertyCode}-{Year}.']
  strategic_initiatives varchar [note: 'Free-text description of longer-horizon strategic revenue initiatives included in this budget (e.g., loyalty program rate strategy, new OTA partnership, dynamic pricing rule (DRR) rollout, group business development targets). Supports owner presentations and management reporting.']
  strategy_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle state of this revenue budget and strategy record. \'draft\' = under preparation; \'approved\' = signed off by revenue director; \'active\' = in-period execution; \'superseded\' = replaced by a newer version; \'archived\' = closed period record.']
  strategy_type varchar [note: 'Classifies the revenue strategy scope covered by this budget: \'transient\' (FIT/BAR-driven room revenue), \'group\' (MICE and group block revenue), \'total_revenue\' (TRevPAR-level all-revenue planning), \'food_and_beverage\' (F&B revenue plan), \'events\' (event/conference revenue), or \'other\'. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: transient|group|total_revenue|food_and_beverage|events|other — promote to reference product]']
  submission_date date [note: 'The date on which this budget version was formally submitted for review and approval. Used for governance tracking and audit trail in owner presentations and management reporting.']
  target_adr decimal(18,2) [note: 'Budgeted Average Daily Rate (ADR) in the property\'s operating currency for the planning period. Represents the planned average revenue earned per occupied room per night. Core revenue KPI used in STR STAR Report, RGI, and MPI benchmarking.']
  target_alos decimal(5,2) [note: 'Budgeted Average Length of Stay (ALOS) in nights for the planning period and market segment. Supports LOS-based pricing strategy, minimum stay restrictions, and demand pattern planning in IDeaS G3 RMS.']
  target_ari decimal(6,4) [note: 'Budgeted Average Rate Index (ARI) target, representing the property\'s planned ADR performance relative to its STR competitive set (property ADR / comp set ADR). Supports rate strategy and competitive positioning planning.']
  target_goppar decimal(10,2) [note: 'Budgeted Gross Operating Profit Per Available Room (GOPPAR) in the property\'s operating currency. Represents the profitability target per available room after operating expenses, used in owner presentations and GOP governance.']
  target_mpi decimal(6,4) [note: 'Budgeted Market Penetration Index (MPI) target, representing the property\'s planned occupancy performance relative to its STR competitive set (property OCC / comp set OCC). Supports competitive benchmarking strategy.']
  target_occupancy_rate decimal(5,2) [note: 'Budgeted occupancy rate (OCC) expressed as a percentage (0.00–100.00) for the planning period. Represents the planned proportion of available rooms expected to be sold. Core KPI input for RevPAR calculation and STR STAR Report benchmarking.']
  target_revpar decimal(18,2) [note: 'Budgeted Revenue Per Available Room (RevPAR) in the property\'s operating currency for the planning period. Calculated as ADR × OCC but stored as a strategic target for direct comparison against actuals and STR competitive set benchmarks (RGI).']
  target_rgi decimal(6,4) [note: 'Budgeted Revenue Generation Index (RGI) target, representing the property\'s planned RevPAR performance relative to its STR competitive set (property RevPAR / comp set RevPAR). RGI > 1.0 indicates planned market share gain.']
  target_trevpar decimal(18,2) [note: 'Budgeted Total Revenue Per Available Room (TRevPAR) in the property\'s operating currency, encompassing all revenue streams (rooms, F&B, events, spa, parking, etc.) per available room. Supports total revenue strategy planning beyond rooms-only RevPAR.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this revenue budget record was most recently modified. Tracks version changes, reforecast updates, and approval workflow transitions for audit and governance purposes.']
  version varchar [note: 'Indicates the iteration of this budget record: \'original\' (initial annual plan), \'revised\' (mid-year adjustment), or \'reforecast\' (rolling forecast update). Supports version-controlled variance analysis in the Daily Operations Report (DOR) and management reporting.']

  Note: 'Revenue planning, strategy, and budget records combining strategic revenue targets with financial budget commitments at the property and market segment level, aligned to USALI standards. Captures planning period, property, strategy type (transient, group, total revenue), target and budgeted ADR/occupancy/RevPAR/TRevPAR, budgeted room revenue, key tactical actions and strategic initiatives, budget version (original, revised, reforecast), strategy status (draft, approved, active), planning horizon, and approving revenue director. This is the SSOT for all revenue planning governance — both strategic direction and financial targets — used for variance analysis against actuals in the DOR, management reporting, owner presentations, and strategic revenue governance.'
}
