  is_lra boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this negotiated rate carries a Last Room Availability (LRA) obligation, requiring the property to honor the contracted rate as long as any room of the applicable type remains available, regardless of demand or yield management controls.']
  is_non_refundable boolean [note: 'Indicates whether reservations booked under this negotiated rate are non-refundable (NRR). Affects cancellation policy enforcement and revenue recognition timing.']
  max_los varchar [note: 'Maximum number of consecutive nights allowed per reservation under this negotiated rate. Null if no upper limit is imposed.']
  min_los varchar [note: 'Minimum number of consecutive nights required per reservation to qualify for this negotiated rate. Enforced at booking in Sabre SynXis CRS and Oracle OPERA PMS.']
  min_night_commitment varchar [note: 'Minimum number of room nights the account is contractually committed to consume during the contract period. Used for volume tracking and contract compliance reporting.']
  negotiation_owner varchar [note: 'Name or employee identifier of the revenue manager or sales manager responsible for negotiating and managing this rate agreement. Used for accountability and performance tracking.']
  rate_bar_variance_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'The percentage discount or premium of this negotiated rate relative to the Best Available Rate (BAR) at time of contract negotiation. Used by revenue management to assess rate competitiveness and yield impact.']
  rate_code varchar [note: 'Alphanumeric rate code used to identify and load this negotiated rate in Sabre SynXis CRS and Oracle OPERA PMS. This is the externally-known business identifier referenced in GDS/CRS rate loading and reservation transactions.']
  rate_includes_tax decimal(18,2) [note: 'Indicates whether the negotiated rate amount is inclusive of applicable taxes. Critical for revenue recognition, financial reporting, and guest billing accuracy.']
  rate_loaded_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when the negotiated rate was successfully loaded into Sabre SynXis CRS and/or Oracle OPERA PMS for distribution. Null if loading has not yet occurred.']
  rate_loading_status varchar [note: 'Current status of the rate loading process in Sabre SynXis CRS and Oracle OPERA PMS. Indicates whether the negotiated rate has been successfully distributed to all applicable booking channels.']
  rate_name varchar [note: 'Human-readable name describing the negotiated rate agreement, typically referencing the account or program name (e.g., \'Acme Corp 2025 Corporate Rate\'). Used in reporting and rate management dashboards.']
  rate_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the negotiated rate agreement. Controls whether the rate is bookable and distributed through CRS/GDS channels.']
  rate_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the pricing structure for this negotiated rate. Fixed rates are static for the contract period; dynamic rates may fluctuate within agreed bounds; tiered rates vary by volume; per diem rates are government-mandated ceiling rates.']
  record_status varchar
  source_system_rate_reference decimal [note: 'Native identifier of this negotiated rate record in the originating operational system (Oracle OPERA PMS, Sabre SynXis CRS, or Salesforce CRM). Enables traceability and reconciliation between the lakehouse and source systems.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this negotiated rate record was last modified in the source system. Supports change tracking, audit compliance, and incremental ETL processing.']

  Note: 'Corporate and wholesale negotiated rate agreements defining contracted pricing for specific accounts, travel management companies (TMCs), and consortia. Captures account identifier, rate code, negotiated rate amount, LRA (Last Room Availability) obligation, blackout dates, minimum night commitment, contract period, and rate loading status in Sabre SynXis CRS and Oracle OPERA PMS. Distinct from public rate plans — these are account-specific contracted rates.'
}

Table revenue.restriction_application {
  restriction_application_id varchar [pk, note: 'Primary key for the restriction_application association']
  rate_availability_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to the specific daily rate and availability snapshot to which this restriction is applied.']
  rate_restriction_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to the rate restriction rule being applied to the availability record.']
  advance_purchase_days varchar [note: 'Minimum number of days in advance a booking must be made to qualify for this rate plan on the snapshot date (e.g., 7-day advance purchase, 21-day advance purchase for NRR rates). A key rate restriction parameter managed in IDeaS G3 RMS and Sabre SynXis CRS. [Moved from rate_availability: Advance purchase requirement is a restriction rule attribute defined on rate_restriction. Its presence on rate_availability is a denormalized snapshot of the active restriction. The restriction_application association provides the proper operational link between the restriction definition and the availability record.]']
  applied_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this specific restriction was activated and applied to the linked rate availability record. Sourced from detection phase relationship data.']
  closed_to_arrival boolean [note: 'Indicates whether new arrivals are blocked on the snapshot date for this room type and rate plan. When True, guests cannot check in on this date but may continue an existing stay through it. A yield management restriction used to optimize multi-night booking patterns. [Moved from rate_availability: CTA is a restriction type managed in rate_restriction. Its presence on rate_availability is a denormalized snapshot. The restriction_application association captures which specific CTA restriction record is applied to which availability record, with its own status and override state.]']
  closed_to_departure boolean [note: 'Indicates whether departures are blocked on the snapshot date for this room type and rate plan. When True, guests cannot check out on this date, forcing stays to extend through it. Used in conjunction with CTA restrictions to shape booking patterns during peak periods. [Moved from rate_availability: CTD is a restriction type managed in rate_restriction. Same reasoning as closed_to_arrival — the denormalized boolean on rate_availability should be derived from the active restriction_application records rather than stored redundantly.]']
  distribution_status varchar [note: 'Indicates whether this specific restriction application has been successfully distributed to connected channel systems (GDS, OTA, CRS) for this availability record. Distinct from the restriction-level distribution_status on rate_restriction. Sourced from detection phase relationship data.']
  los_maximum varchar [note: 'Maximum number of nights permitted under this rate plan for the snapshot date. Used to prevent long-stay bookings at promotional rates during high-demand periods. Managed in IDeaS G3 RMS as an upper LOS (Length of Stay) restriction. [Moved from rate_availability: Same reasoning as los_minimum — maximum LOS is a restriction rule attribute. Its denormalization on rate_availability collapses multiple simultaneous restriction applications into a single value, losing the operational detail that restriction_application captures.]']
  los_minimum varchar [note: 'Minimum number of nights a guest must stay to qualify for this rate plan on the snapshot date. A key yield optimization restriction managed in IDeaS G3 RMS. LOS (Length of Stay) restrictions are used to maximize revenue during high-demand periods by requiring multi-night commitments. [Moved from rate_availability: Minimum LOS is a restriction attribute that belongs to the restriction_application pairing. Its presence on rate_availability represents a denormalized snapshot of the currently active restriction. When multiple restrictions with different LOS rules apply simultaneously, a single los_minimum on rate_availability cannot represent the full picture. The authoritative value lives on rate_restriction and the effective application state lives on restriction_application.]']
  override_allowed boolean [note: 'Indicates whether a revenue manager or authorized staff member is permitted to manually override this specific restriction application for the linked availability record. Sourced from detection phase relationship data.']
  priority_rank varchar [note: 'Numeric priority rank used to resolve conflicts when multiple restrictions are simultaneously applied to the same rate availability record. Determines which restriction takes precedence when rules conflict. Sourced from detection phase relationship data.']
  restriction_status varchar [note: 'Current operational status of this specific restriction-to-availability pairing. Tracks whether the restriction is actively enforced, has expired, or has been overridden for this availability record. Sourced from detection phase relationship data.']

  Note: 'This association product represents the operational application of a rate restriction to a specific rate availability record in the revenue management system. It captures the active state of each restriction-to-availability pairing as managed in IDeaS G3 RMS and distributed via Sabre SynXis CRS. Each record links one rate_availability snapshot to one rate_restriction rule with attributes that exist only in the context of this specific application — including activation timestamp, distribution status, priority rank for conflict resolution, and override authorization state.. Existence Justification: In IDeaS G3 RMS and Sabre SynXis CRS, revenue managers explicitly apply multiple rate restrictions (min LOS, CTA, CTD, advance purchase, blackout) simultaneously to a single rate availability record, and a single restriction definition (e.g., a 2-night minimum LOS rule) covers many availability records across its date range, room type scope, and rate plan scope. This is an actively managed operational concept — revenue managers create, activate, override, and expire these restriction-to-availability pairings as a core yield optimization workflow. The relationship is a first-class operational entity called \'restriction_application\' in RMS terminology, carrying its own status, priority, and override metadata.'
}

Table loyalty.member {
  member_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the loyalty program member. Primary key.']
  enrollment_channel_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.channel. Business justification: Loyalty enrollment attribution reporting requires linking each member to the channel through which they enrolled. The plain-text enrollment_channel attribute is a denormalization of channel.channel. M']
  primary_member_enrollment_hotel_property_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key reference to the property where the member enrolled in the loyalty program, if enrollment occurred at a physical location.']
  primary_member_guest_profile_id varchar [note: 'FK to guest.profile.profile_id — MUST-HAVE: Loyalty member must resolve to guest identity for personalization, stay history correlation, and profile merge operations. Without this FK, loyalty benefits cannot be applied at check-in.']
  tier_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key reference to the loyalty tier product. Represents the current tier assignment (e.g., Silver, Gold, Platinum, Elite).']
  account_closure_date date [note: 'Date when the membership account was closed or terminated. Null for active accounts.']
  account_closure_reason varchar [note: 'Reason for membership account closure. Used for churn analysis and program improvement.']
  communication_opt_in boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the member has opted in to receive marketing communications and promotional offers from the loyalty program.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when the member record was first created in the system. Used for audit trail and data lineage.']
  currency_preference varchar [note: 'Member\'s preferred currency for displaying points value and pricing. Three-letter ISO 4217 currency code.']
  current_points_balance decimal(18,2) [note: 'Current available points balance that can be redeemed by the member. Reflects earned points minus redeemed and expired points.']
  email_opt_in boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the member has consented to receive email communications. Separate from general communication opt-in for channel-specific consent.']
  enrollment_date date [note: 'Date when the guest enrolled in the loyalty program. Marks the beginning of the member lifecycle.']
  language_preference varchar [note: 'Member\'s preferred language for communications and service delivery. Three-letter ISO 639-2 language code.']
  last_stay_date date [note: 'Date of the member\'s most recent completed stay. Used for recency analysis and churn prediction.']
  lifetime_nights varchar [note: 'Total number of room nights stayed by the member since enrollment. Used for tier qualification and LTV (Lifetime Value) calculation.']
  lifetime_points_earned varchar [note: 'Total cumulative points earned by the member since enrollment. Used for tier qualification and lifetime value tracking.']
  lifetime_revenue decimal(18,2) [note: 'Total revenue generated by the member across all stays, F&B (Food and Beverage), and ancillary services since enrollment. Key LTV (Lifetime Value) metric.']
  lifetime_stays varchar [note: 'Total number of completed stays by the member since enrollment. Key metric for member engagement and tier qualification.']
  membership_number bigint [note: 'Externally-known unique membership identifier assigned to the loyalty program member. Used for member recognition and program transactions.']
  membership_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the loyalty membership account. Active members can accrue and redeem points; suspended or closed accounts have restricted access.']
  next_stay_date date [note: 'Date of the member\'s next confirmed reservation. Used for engagement tracking and personalized offers.']
  nps_score varchar [note: 'Most recent NPS (Net Promoter Score) rating provided by the member. Scale of -100 to 100, measuring likelihood to recommend the brand.']
  partner_sharing_consent boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the member has consented to share their data with loyalty program partners (airlines, car rentals, etc.) for cross-program benefits.']
  points_expired varchar [note: 'Total cumulative points that have expired due to inactivity or program rules.']
  points_redeemed varchar [note: 'Total cumulative points redeemed by the member for rewards, upgrades, or benefits since enrollment.']
  salt_score decimal(5,2) [note: 'SALT (Satisfaction and Loyalty Tracking) composite score measuring member satisfaction and loyalty. Proprietary metric combining multiple engagement and satisfaction indicators.']
  sms_opt_in boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the member has consented to receive SMS/text message communications.']
  tier_expiration_date date [note: 'Date when the member\'s current tier status expires. Used for tier renewal campaigns and retention efforts.']
  tier_qualification_date date [note: 'Date when the member qualified for their current tier. Used for tier anniversary tracking and benefit eligibility.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when the member record was last modified. Used for audit trail and change tracking.']
  vip_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the member is designated as a VIP for special recognition and service. May be based on tier, LTV (Lifetime Value), or manual assignment.']
  ytd_nights varchar [note: 'Number of room nights stayed by the member in the current calendar year. Used for annual tier qualification.']
  ytd_revenue decimal(18,2) [note: 'Total revenue generated by the member in the current calendar year. Used for tier qualification and annual performance tracking.']
  ytd_stays varchar [note: 'Number of completed stays by the member in the current calendar year. Used for annual tier qualification.']

  Note: 'Core master entity representing a guest enrolled in the loyalty program. Captures membership identity, enrollment date, current tier assignment (FK to tier), lifetime points balance, LTV metrics (total revenue, stays, nights), SALT scores, program opt-in preferences, communication consent, membership number, and account status (active, suspended, closed). This is the SSOT for loyalty membership identity and current member state — distinct from the guest profile in the guest domain, which owns PII and stay history. References guest_id as a foreign key to the guest domain. Also serves as the anchor for member segment assignments (segment memberships tracked temporally within member_segment).'
}

Table loyalty.tier {
  tier_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the loyalty program tier. Primary key.']
  bonus_points_on_enrollment varchar [note: 'Number of bonus loyalty points awarded to a member upon first achieving this tier status.']
  breakfast_benefit_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether members at this tier receive complimentary breakfast during their stays.']
  code varchar [note: 'Short alphanumeric code uniquely identifying the tier (e.g., SILVER, GOLD, PLATINUM, DIAMOND). Used for system integration and display.']
  color_code varchar [note: 'Hexadecimal color code used for visual representation of the tier in digital interfaces and marketing materials (e.g., #C0C0C0 for Silver, #FFD700 for Gold).']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this tier record was first created in the system.']
  dedicated_support_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether members at this tier have access to a dedicated customer service line or concierge team.']
  description varchar [note: 'Detailed description of the tier, including benefits summary and value proposition, used for member communications and marketing.']
  display_order varchar [note: 'Numeric sort order for displaying tiers in user interfaces and reports. Lower numbers appear first.']
  downgrade_grace_period_months varchar [note: 'Number of months of grace period provided before downgrading a member who no longer meets qualification thresholds.']
  early_checkin_hours varchar [note: 'Number of hours before standard check-in time that members at this tier are entitled to for early check-in (e.g., 2 for 1pm check-in when standard is 3pm).']
  effective_end_date date [note: 'Date when this tier definition expires or was discontinued. Null for currently active tiers with no planned end date.']
  effective_start_date date [note: 'Date when this tier definition became or will become active and available for member assignment.']
  guaranteed_availability_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether members at this tier have guaranteed room availability when booking within specified advance notice periods.']
  icon_url varchar [note: 'URL or path to the icon or badge image representing this tier in digital channels.']
  last_modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this tier record was last updated.']
  late_checkout_hours varchar [note: 'Number of hours past standard checkout time that members at this tier are entitled to for late checkout (e.g., 2 for 2pm checkout when standard is 12pm).']
  level varchar [note: 'Numeric ranking of the tier within the program hierarchy. Lower numbers indicate entry-level tiers, higher numbers indicate elite status. Used for tier comparison and upgrade logic.']
  lounge_access_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether members at this tier have complimentary access to executive lounges or club floors at participating properties.']
  name varchar [note: 'Full display name of the loyalty tier (e.g., Silver Elite, Gold Premier, Platinum Honors, Diamond Ambassador).']
  points_earning_multiplier decimal(5,2) [note: 'Multiplier applied to base points earning for members at this tier (e.g., 1.5 means 50% bonus points, 2.0 means double points).']
  priority_reservation_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether members at this tier receive priority handling for reservations and waitlist requests.']
  qualification_currency_code varchar [note: 'ISO 4217 three-letter currency code for the qualification spend threshold (e.g., USD, EUR, GBP).']
  qualification_nights_threshold varchar [note: 'Minimum number of qualifying nights required to achieve or maintain this tier status within the qualification period.']
  qualification_period_months varchar [note: 'Number of months over which qualification activity is measured (e.g., 12 for annual qualification, 24 for rolling two-year window).']
  qualification_points_threshold varchar [note: 'Minimum number of loyalty points required to achieve or maintain this tier status within the qualification period.']
  qualification_spend_threshold decimal(18,2) [note: 'Minimum monetary spend amount required to achieve or maintain this tier status within the qualification period. Typically measured in the program\'s base currency.']
  qualification_stays_threshold varchar [note: 'Minimum number of qualifying stays required to achieve or maintain this tier status within the qualification period.']
  room_upgrade_eligible_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether members at this tier are eligible for complimentary room upgrades at check-in (subject to availability).']
  tier_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the tier. Active tiers are available for member assignment; inactive tiers are temporarily suspended; discontinued tiers are retired but may have legacy members.']
  validity_months varchar [note: 'Number of months that tier status remains valid once achieved, before re-qualification is required (e.g., 12 for annual renewal, 24 for two-year validity).']
  welcome_amenity_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether members at this tier receive a welcome amenity (e.g., fruit basket, beverage credit) upon arrival.']

  Note: 'Reference master defining the loyalty program tier hierarchy (e.g., Silver, Gold, Platinum, Diamond). Captures tier name, tier code, qualification thresholds (nights, stays, points, spend), benefit entitlements, upgrade/downgrade rules, tier validity period, and display order. Governs tier assignment logic and benefit eligibility across the program.'
}

Table loyalty.points_ledger {
  points_ledger_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for each points ledger transaction entry. Primary key for the points ledger.']
  accrual_rule_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.accrual_rule. Business justification: Points accrual transactions should reference the rule that governed the earning calculation. Currently points_ledger has earn_multiplier (DECIMAL) but no FK to the rule. Adding accrual_rule_id enables']
  event_booking_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to event.event_booking. Business justification: MICE/group loyalty programs award points for event bookings separately from hotel stays. Points_ledger already has reservation_booking_id for stays; a parallel event_booking_id FK is needed to record ']
  member_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the loyalty program member who owns this points transaction.']
  points_channel_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.channel. Business justification: Points ledger transactions must link to distribution channel for analyzing points accrual patterns by booking channel, understanding channel-specific earning behavior, and calculating true channel pro']
  promotion_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.promotion. Business justification: points_ledger has promotion_code (STRING) for bonus points earned via promotions. Adding promotion_id FK formalizes this relationship, enabling promotion-level points tracking and ROI analysis. Nullab']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.property. Business justification: Loyalty finance reconciliation requires linking points accrual/redemption transactions to specific properties for revenue allocation and inter-company settlements. Currently property_code is text; FK ']
  redemption_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.redemption. Business justification: Points ledger entries of transaction_type \'redemption\' should link to the redemption transaction that caused the points burn. Creates bidirectional navigation between ledger and redemption. Nullable (']
  redemption_rule_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.redemption_rule. Business justification: Points redemption/burn transactions should reference the rule that governed the redemption calculation. Enables rule-level reporting and ensures redemptions can be traced to their governing rules. Nul']
  revenue_center_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to fnb.revenue_center. Business justification: Points ledger entries from F&B transactions must reference the originating revenue center for F&B-level loyalty reporting (points earned per outlet), USALI reconciliation, and revenue center profitabi']
  reversal_reference_points_ledger_id varchar [note: 'Points ledger ID of the original transaction that this entry reverses. Null for original transactions. Creates audit trail for cancelled transactions.']
  stay_history_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to guest.stay_history. Business justification: Loyalty audit and points dispute resolution require direct reconciliation of points ledger entries against stay history records. Points posting teams and member services agents use this link to valida']
  activity_date date [note: 'Date when the underlying business activity occurred (e.g., stay checkout date, F&B transaction date, partner purchase date). This is the business event date, distinct from posting date.']
  adjustment_notes varchar [note: 'Free-text explanation for manual adjustments or reversals, providing context for audit and member service. Null for standard transactions.']
  adjustment_reason_code varchar [note: 'Standardized code explaining why a manual adjustment or reversal was made (e.g., service recovery, system error correction, duplicate posting). Null for standard transactions.']
  balance_after_transaction decimal(18,2) [note: 'Member\'s total points balance immediately after this transaction was posted. Provides running balance for audit and reconciliation.']
  base_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Monetary amount in base currency that generated the points accrual (e.g., room revenue, F&B spend). Used to calculate points earned. Null for non-monetary transactions.']
  base_currency_code varchar [note: 'ISO 4217 three-letter currency code of the underlying monetary transaction that generated points (e.g., USD, EUR, GBP). Null for non-monetary point awards.']
  conversion_rate decimal(10,4) [note: 'Exchange rate applied when converting points between hotel program and partner program (e.g., 1.5 means 1 hotel point = 1.5 partner points). Null for non-transfer transactions.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'System timestamp when this ledger entry was first created in the database. Used for audit trail and data lineage.']
  expiry_date date [note: 'Date when these points will expire if not redeemed. Null for non-expiring points or debit transactions. Used to enforce points expiration policies.']
  is_qualifying boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this transaction counts toward tier qualification or elite status progression. True for qualifying stays and spend, false for bonus points and transfers.']
  modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'System timestamp when this ledger entry was last updated. Used for audit trail and change tracking.']
  partner_confirmation_number bigint [note: 'Confirmation or reference number provided by partner program for transfer transactions. Used for reconciliation and dispute resolution. Null for non-transfer transactions.']
  partner_program_code varchar [note: 'Code identifying the external partner loyalty program involved in transfer transactions (e.g., airline frequent flyer program, credit card rewards program). Null for internal transactions.']
  points_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Quantity of points involved in this transaction. Positive for accruals (earn, transfer_in, bonus), negative for debits (redeem, transfer_out, expire, adjust).']
  posting_date date [note: 'Date when the points transaction was posted to the member\'s account and became effective in their balance. May differ from activity_date due to processing lag.']
  source_activity_type varchar [note: 'Category of business activity that generated this points transaction: stay (room revenue), fnb (Food and Beverage spend), spa (spa/wellness services), partner_purchase (external partner transaction), promotion (marketing campaign), manual (staff adjustment), transfer (partner program exchange). [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: stay|fnb|spa|partner_purchase|promotion|manual|transfer — 7 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  tier_at_transaction varchar [note: 'Member\'s loyalty tier status at the time this transaction was posted (e.g., Silver, Gold, Platinum). Captures tier for historical analysis of earning patterns.']
  transaction_number bigint [note: 'Business-facing unique identifier for this points transaction, used for member inquiries and reconciliation.']
  transaction_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the points transaction: pending (awaiting posting), posted (finalized and reflected in balance), reversed (cancelled), failed (rejected due to validation error).']
  transaction_type varchar [note: 'Type of points movement: earn (accrual from activity), redeem (points spent), expire (time-based expiration), adjust (manual correction), transfer_out (sent to partner), transfer_in (received from partner), bonus (promotional award), reversal (cancellation of prior transaction). [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: earn|redeem|expire|adjust|transfer_out|transfer_in|bonus|reversal — 8 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  transfer_direction varchar [note: 'Direction of partner transfer: inbound (points received from partner into hotel program), outbound (points sent from hotel program to partner). Null for non-transfer transactions.']
  transfer_fee_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Fee charged to member for partner transfer transaction, expressed in points. Null if no fee applies or for non-transfer transactions.']

  Note: 'Authoritative transactional ledger recording every points movement for a loyalty member — including accruals, redemptions, expirations, adjustments, and partner transfers. Each row is an immutable debit or credit entry capturing transaction type (earn, redeem, expire, adjust, transfer_out, transfer_in, bonus), points amount, balance after transaction, source activity (stay, F&B spend, partner purchase, promotion), activity date, posting date, expiry date, originating system reference. For transfer-type entries: partner program reference, transfer direction, conversion rate applied, partner confirmation number, transfer status, and fee charged. This is the SSOT for points balance, movement history, and partner transfer activity.'
}

Table loyalty.accrual_rule {
  accrual_rule_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the loyalty points accrual rule. Primary key for the accrual rule configuration entity.']
  booking_source_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.booking_source. Business justification: Accrual rules are frequently restricted to specific booking sources (e.g., OTA bookings earn fewer points than direct). The plain-text booking_channel_restriction attribute is a denormalization of cha']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.property. Business justification: Property revenue managers need to forecast loyalty liability by analyzing which accrual rules apply to their property. Currently applicable_property_ids is a text list; FK enables property-specific ea']
  revenue_center_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to fnb.revenue_center. Business justification: Loyalty accrual rules are scoped to specific F&B revenue centers in hotel operations (e.g., 2x points at signature restaurant vs. bar). This FK enables revenue-center-specific points earning configura']
  segment_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to guest.segment. Business justification: Loyalty program configuration includes segment-targeted accrual rules (e.g., corporate segment earns 3x points). Revenue and loyalty managers configure and report on segment-specific earning rules. A ']
  applicable_brands varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of brand codes where this rule applies (e.g., luxury, premium, select-service). Used when property_applicability is \'brand_specific\'. Null indicates all brands.']
  applicable_property_ids varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of property identifiers where this rule applies. Used when property_applicability is \'property_list\'. Null indicates rule applies per property_applicability setting.']
  applicable_regions varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of geographic region codes where this rule applies (e.g., NORAM, EMEA, APAC, LATAM). Used when property_applicability is \'region_specific\'. Null indicates all regions.']
  approval_status varchar [note: 'Workflow approval status for the accrual rule configuration. Used for governance and change control before rules are activated in production.']
  approved_by varchar [note: 'User ID or name of the business owner or system administrator who approved this accrual rule for production use. Used for audit trail and accountability.']
  approved_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this accrual rule was approved for production use. Part of the governance audit trail.']
  blackout_dates varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of date ranges (YYYY-MM-DD:YYYY-MM-DD) during which this accrual rule does not apply. Used for promotional exclusions or high-demand periods. Null indicates no blackouts.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this accrual rule record was first created in the system. Part of the standard audit trail.']
  currency_code varchar [note: 'Three-letter ISO 4217 currency code for the earning basis (e.g., USD, EUR, GBP). Defines the currency in which the points-per-currency-unit rate applies.']
  day_of_week_restriction bigint [note: 'Comma-separated list of days of week (MON, TUE, WED, THU, FRI, SAT, SUN) when this rule applies. Used for promotional rules targeting specific days. Null indicates all days are eligible.']
  earning_basis varchar [note: 'The transaction component or activity on which points accrual is calculated: room_revenue (ADR-based), fnb_spend (Food and Beverage), spa_spend, ancillary_spend (parking, resort fees), partner_spend (co-branded partners), nights_stayed (per-night basis), qualifying_stays (per-stay basis). [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: room_revenue|fnb_spend|spa_spend|ancillary_spend|partner_spend|nights_stayed|qualifying_stays — 7 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  effective_end_date date [note: 'Date when this accrual rule expires and stops applying to transactions. Null indicates the rule is open-ended with no expiration. Part of the rule\'s temporal validity window.']
  effective_start_date date [note: 'Date when this accrual rule becomes active and begins applying to qualifying transactions. Part of the rule\'s temporal validity window.']
  eligible_rate_codes decimal [note: 'Comma-separated list of rate codes (BAR, corporate, government, promotional) that qualify for points earning under this rule. Null or empty indicates all rate codes are eligible.']
  estimated_annual_points_volume varchar [note: 'Projected total number of loyalty points expected to be issued annually under this accrual rule. Used for program economics forecasting and liability planning.']
  excluded_rate_codes decimal [note: 'Comma-separated list of rate codes explicitly excluded from earning points under this rule (e.g., employee rates, complimentary stays, distressed inventory). Takes precedence over eligible_rate_codes.']
  external_rule_code varchar [note: 'Unique identifier for this accrual rule in the source operational system. Used for cross-system reconciliation and integration mapping.']
  is_stackable boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this accrual rule can be combined with other rules for the same transaction (True) or is mutually exclusive (False). Used to control promotional stacking and program economics.']
  last_modified_by varchar [note: 'User ID or name of the person who last modified this accrual rule configuration. Used for audit trail and change tracking.']
  last_modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this accrual rule record was last updated. Part of the standard audit trail for configuration change management.']
  marketing_message varchar [note: 'Member-facing promotional message describing the earning opportunity (e.g., \'Earn 2X points on weekend stays!\'). Used in marketing campaigns and member communications.']
  maximum_points_per_transaction varchar [note: 'Cap on the number of points that can be earned in a single transaction under this rule. Used to prevent abuse and manage program liability. Null indicates no cap.']
  member_segment_restriction varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of member segment codes (corporate, leisure, group, FIT) eligible for this accrual rule. Used for segment-targeted promotions. Null indicates all segments are eligible.']
  member_tier_restriction varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of loyalty tier codes (base, silver, gold, platinum, diamond) eligible for this accrual rule. Used for tier-specific promotional rules. Null indicates all tiers are eligible.']
  minimum_transaction_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Minimum spend threshold required for the accrual rule to apply. Transactions below this amount do not earn points under this rule. Null indicates no minimum.']
  points_per_currency_unit decimal(10,4) [note: 'Base rate of loyalty points earned per unit of currency spent (e.g., 10.0000 points per USD, 5.0000 points per EUR). Used as the multiplier in the points calculation engine.']
  program_liability_impact varchar [note: 'Assessment of the financial liability impact this accrual rule has on the loyalty program\'s balance sheet: low (minimal incremental liability), medium (moderate impact), high (significant liability increase). Used for program economics monitoring.']
  property_applicability varchar [note: 'Scope of properties where this accrual rule applies: all (entire portfolio), brand_specific (luxury/premium/select-service), property_list (specific property IDs), region_specific (geographic regions).']
  rule_code varchar [note: 'Short alphanumeric code used as a unique business identifier for the accrual rule in operational systems and reporting (e.g., \'ROOM_BASE\', \'FNB_ELITE\', \'SPA_PROMO\').']
  rule_description varchar [note: 'Detailed business description of the accrual rule, including its purpose, earning mechanics, eligibility criteria, and any special conditions. Used for documentation and business user reference.']
  rule_name varchar [note: 'Business-friendly name of the accrual rule for identification and reporting purposes (e.g., \'Base Room Revenue Earn\', \'Elite Tier Bonus\', \'F&B Spend Multiplier\').']
  rule_priority varchar [note: 'Numeric priority ranking used to resolve conflicts when multiple accrual rules apply to the same transaction. Lower numbers indicate higher priority. The points calculation engine applies the highest-priority matching rule.']
  rule_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the accrual rule: draft (under development), active (in production), suspended (temporarily disabled), expired (past effective_end_date), retired (permanently deactivated).']
  rule_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the accrual rule by its business purpose: base (standard earning), bonus (additional points), promotional (limited-time campaign), tier_multiplier (elite status boost), partner (third-party earn), seasonal (time-bound recurring).']
  segment_multiplier decimal(5,2) [note: 'Additional multiplier applied based on member segment or customer classification (e.g., corporate, leisure, group). Used for targeted earning incentives.']
  terms_and_conditions varchar [note: 'Legal terms and conditions text associated with this accrual rule, including disclaimers, exclusions, and member obligations. Used for regulatory compliance and member communication.']
  tier_multiplier decimal(5,2) [note: 'Additional multiplier applied based on member loyalty tier or elite status (e.g., 1.00 for base, 1.25 for silver, 1.50 for gold, 2.00 for platinum). Multiplies the base points calculation.']
  version_number varchar [note: 'Sequential version number for this accrual rule configuration. Incremented with each modification to support change history and rollback capabilities.']
  created_by varchar [note: 'User ID or name of the person who created this accrual rule configuration. Used for audit trail and accountability.']

  Note: 'Master configuration entity defining the rules by which loyalty points are earned. Captures rule name, earning basis (room revenue, F&B spend, spa spend, partner spend), points-per-currency-unit rate, multiplier for tier or segment, eligible rate codes, blackout conditions, effective date range, property applicability, and rule priority. Drives the points calculation engine for all earn transactions.'
}

Business justification: Redemption rules in hotel loyalty programs are scoped to specific F&B revenue centers (e.g., points redeemable only at the signature restaurant). This FK enables outlet-specific redemption configurati']
  seasonal_calendar_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.seasonal_calendar. Business justification: Redemption blackout dates align with peak seasonal demand periods. Linking redemption_rule to seasonal_calendar replaces the unstructured blackout_dates text field with a structured FK, enabling autom']
  advance_booking_days varchar [note: 'Minimum number of days in advance a reservation must be made for this rule to apply. Used for early booking incentives.']
  blackout_dates varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of date ranges (YYYY-MM-DD:YYYY-MM-DD) when this rule is not applicable. Used for peak season restrictions.']
  calculation_basis varchar [note: 'Defines the monetary or transactional basis for points calculation. Determines which revenue component is used for earn rate application.']
  combinable_with_promotions boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this redemption rule can be combined with other promotional offers. False means this rule is exclusive.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this redemption rule record was first created in the system. Audit trail for rule configuration.']
  currency_code varchar [note: 'Three-letter ISO 4217 currency code for monetary earn rules. Defines the currency basis for points calculation.']
  description varchar [note: 'Detailed business description of the redemption rule including terms, conditions, and member-facing explanation.']
  effective_end_date date [note: 'Date when this redemption rule expires and is no longer applied. Nullable for open-ended rules.']
  effective_start_date date [note: 'Date when this redemption rule becomes active and eligible for application. Part of the rule validity window.']
  eligible_property_codes varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of property codes where this redemption rule is applicable. Defines geographic or brand scope.']
  eligible_rate_codes decimal [note: 'Comma-separated list of rate codes eligible for this redemption rule. Defines which booking rate plans qualify for points earning or redemption.']
  excluded_property_codes varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of property codes explicitly excluded from this redemption rule. Takes precedence over eligible properties.']
  excluded_rate_codes decimal [note: 'Comma-separated list of rate codes explicitly excluded from this redemption rule. Takes precedence over eligible rate codes.']
  lra_applicable boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this redemption rule applies under Last Room Availability conditions. True means members can redeem even when standard inventory is sold out.']
  maximum_earn_per_stay varchar [note: 'Maximum number of points that can be earned per stay under this rule. Cap for earn rules to prevent abuse.']
  maximum_los varchar [note: 'Maximum number of nights allowed for this redemption rule to apply. Used to cap extended stay benefits.']
  maximum_redemption_per_transaction varchar [note: 'Maximum number of points that can be redeemed in a single transaction under this rule. Cap for burn rules.']
  minimum_los varchar [note: 'Minimum number of nights required for this redemption rule to apply. Used for stay-based earn or burn rules.']
  minimum_points_balance decimal(18,2) [note: 'Minimum loyalty points balance required in member account to be eligible for this redemption rule. Applies to burn rules only.']
  modified_by varchar [note: 'User identifier or system account that last modified this redemption rule. Audit trail for accountability.']
  modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this redemption rule record was last modified. Audit trail for rule configuration changes.']
  partner_code varchar [note: 'External partner identifier for partner-based earn or burn rules (e.g., airline, car rental, credit card partner). Nullable for non-partner rules.']
  points_rate decimal(10,2) [note: 'For earn rules: points earned per currency unit spent (e.g., 10 points per USD). For burn rules: points required per unit of benefit (e.g., 25000 points for free night).']
  redemption_rule_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the redemption rule. Only active rules are applied by the points calculation engine.']
  rounding_method varchar [note: 'Method used to round calculated points values. Ensures consistent points calculation across the loyalty program.']
  rule_code varchar [note: 'Unique business identifier code for the redemption rule used across systems and reporting. Externally-known identifier for rule configuration.']
  rule_direction varchar [note: 'Indicates whether this rule governs points earning (earn) or points redemption (burn). Core classification for the rule engine.']
  rule_name varchar [note: 'Human-readable name of the redemption rule for display and reporting purposes.']
  rule_priority varchar [note: 'Numeric priority for rule application when multiple rules are eligible. Lower numbers indicate higher priority. Used by the rules engine for conflict resolution.']
  rule_type varchar [note: 'Categorical classification of the rule basis. For earn rules: room_revenue, fnb_spend, partner_spend. For burn rules: free_night, upgrade, statement_credit, merchandise, experience. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: room_revenue|fnb_spend|partner_spend|free_night|upgrade|statement_credit|merchandise|experience — 8 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  terms_and_conditions varchar [note: 'Legal terms and conditions text associated with this redemption rule. Displayed to members during redemption flow.']
  tier_multiplier_base decimal(5,2) [note: 'Base tier multiplier applied to the points rate for base-tier members. Default is 1.0.']
  tier_multiplier_gold decimal(5,2) [note: 'Tier multiplier applied to the points rate for gold-tier members. Typically 1.5 to 2.0.']
  tier_multiplier_platinum decimal(5,2) [note: 'Tier multiplier applied to the points rate for platinum-tier members. Typically 2.0 to 3.0.']
  tier_multiplier_silver decimal(5,2) [note: 'Tier multiplier applied to the points rate for silver-tier members. Typically 1.25 to 1.5.']
  created_by varchar [note: 'User identifier or system account that created this redemption rule. Audit trail for accountability.']

  Note: 'Unified master configuration entity defining all rules governing how loyalty points are earned and redeemed (earn/burn rules engine). Captures rule direction (earn or burn), rule name, basis (room revenue, F&B spend, partner spend for earn; free night, upgrade, credit for burn), rate or points cost, tier multipliers, eligible rate codes and properties, blackout conditions, minimum balance requirements, LRA applicability, caps, effective date range, and rule priority. Single source of truth for the points calculation and redemption eligibility engines.'
}

Table loyalty.redemption {
  redemption_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the loyalty points redemption transaction. Primary key.']
  channel_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.channel. Business justification: Redemptions must link to distribution channel for channel-specific redemption performance analysis, understanding which channels drive points burn vs. cash bookings, and calculating true channel profi']
  event_booking_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to event.event_booking. Business justification: Members redeem points against event bookings (meeting room rental, AV packages, catering). Redemption already has reservation_booking_id for hotel stays; a distinct event_booking_id FK tracks MICE red']
  member_id varchar [note: 'Identifier of the loyalty program member who initiated the redemption.']
  outlet_property_outlet_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.property_outlet. Business justification: When members redeem points for F&B rewards (complimentary dining, F&B credits), the redemption must reference the specific outlet for outlet-level loyalty redemption reporting, revenue offset accounti']
  pos_check_id varchar [note: 'Identifier of the POS transaction associated with this redemption, if applicable (e.g., F&B voucher redemption). Nullable for non-POS redemptions.']
  redemption_rule_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.redemption_rule. Business justification: Redemptions should reference the rule that governed the redemption calculation and eligibility. Enables rule-level redemption reporting and ensures redemptions can be audited against their governing r']
  revenue_rate_plan_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to revenue.revenue_rate_plan. Business justification: Loyalty redemptions for free night awards or discounted stays must link to the specific rate plan used for the redemption. This FK enables revenue displacement analysis, rate plan performance tracking']
  reward_catalog_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to loyalty.reward_catalog. Business justification: Redemptions of type \'reward\' should reference the catalog item being redeemed. Currently redemption has reward_description and reward_category (STRING) but no FK. Adding reward_catalog_id formalizes t']
  cancellation_reason varchar [note: 'Reason for redemption cancellation (e.g., member request, system error, fraud detection, reward unavailable). Nullable if not cancelled.']
  cancellation_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when the redemption was cancelled. Nullable if not cancelled.']
  cash_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Cash component paid by the member for cash-and-points redemptions. Zero for pure points redemptions.']
  confirmation_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when the redemption was confirmed and points were deducted from the member account. Nullable if still pending.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this redemption record was first created in the source system.']
  currency_code varchar [note: 'Three-letter ISO 4217 currency code for the cash component (e.g., USD, EUR, GBP).']
  expiration_date date [note: 'Date by which the redemption must be fulfilled or the reward will expire. Nullable for redemptions without expiration.']
  fulfillment_channel varchar [note: 'Channel through which the reward was delivered: at property, physical mail, email, partner fulfillment, digital delivery, or in-app delivery.']
  fulfillment_date date [note: 'Date when the reward was delivered or service was rendered to the member. Nullable if not yet fulfilled.']
  fulfillment_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Precise timestamp when the reward was fulfilled. Nullable if not yet fulfilled.']
  last_modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this redemption record was last updated in the source system.']
  monetary_equivalent_value decimal(15,2) [note: 'Estimated monetary value of the redeemed reward in the currency specified, used for program economics and LTV (Lifetime Value) analysis.']
  notes varchar [note: 'Free-text notes captured during redemption processing, including special requests, service recovery actions, or fulfillment instructions.']
  partner_code varchar [note: 'Code of the partner organization fulfilling the reward (e.g., airline, car rental, merchandise vendor). Nullable for internal redemptions.']
  points_redeemed varchar [note: 'Total number of loyalty points deducted from the member account for this redemption.']
  points_refunded varchar [note: 'Number of points returned to the member account due to cancellation or reversal. Zero if no refund occurred.']
  property_code varchar [note: 'Code of the property where the redemption was fulfilled, if applicable. Nullable for non-property redemptions (e.g., partner rewards, merchandise).']
  redemption_number bigint [note: 'Externally-visible unique business identifier for the redemption transaction, used for guest communication and service recovery.']
  redemption_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the redemption: pending approval, confirmed and awaiting fulfillment, fulfilled and completed, cancelled by member or system, expired before fulfillment, or reversed due to service recovery or fraud.']
  redemption_type varchar [note: 'Category of reward being redeemed: free night award, room upgrade, F&B voucher, partner airline/car rental reward, merchandise, curated experience, points transfer to another member, cash plus points combination, or gift certificate. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: free_night|room_upgrade|fnb_voucher|partner_reward|merchandise|experience|points_transfer|cash_and_points|gift_certificate — 9 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  refund_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when points were refunded to the member account. Nullable if no refund occurred.']
  request_date date [note: 'Date when the member submitted the redemption request. Business event date for analytics and reporting.']
  request_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Precise timestamp when the redemption request was initiated by the member, including time zone offset.']
  source_system_code varchar [note: 'Unique identifier of this redemption in the source operational system, used for data lineage and reconciliation.']
  tier_at_redemption varchar [note: 'Loyalty program tier of the member at the time of redemption (e.g., Silver, Gold, Platinum, Diamond). Used for tier-specific redemption analysis.']

  Note: 'Transactional record of a loyalty member redeeming points for a reward. Captures redemption request date, fulfillment date, redemption type (free night, upgrade, F&B voucher, partner reward, merchandise), points deducted, monetary equivalent value, redemption status (pending, confirmed, fulfilled, cancelled, expired), associated reservation or POS transaction reference, and fulfillment channel. SSOT for all reward redemption activity.'
}

  points_cost_gold decimal(18,2) [note: 'Loyalty points required for redemption by Gold tier members, reflecting enhanced tier benefits and discounts.']
  points_cost_platinum decimal(18,2) [note: 'Loyalty points required for redemption by Platinum tier members, offering maximum tier discount benefits.']
  points_cost_silver decimal(18,2) [note: 'Loyalty points required for redemption by Silver tier members, typically discounted from base tier pricing.']
  property_restriction varchar [note: 'Defines which properties or property segments are eligible for redemption of hotel-related rewards.']
  redemption_validity_days varchar [note: 'Number of days from issuance that a redeemed reward certificate or voucher remains valid for use before expiration.']
  reward_category varchar [note: 'Primary classification of the reward type determining redemption process and fulfillment workflow. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: hotel_stay|room_upgrade|dining|spa|experience|merchandise|partner|travel — 8 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  reward_code varchar [note: 'Unique business identifier code for the reward item used across systems and member communications.']
  reward_description varchar [note: 'Detailed description of the reward including benefits, usage instructions, and any special features or limitations.']
  reward_name varchar [note: 'Display name of the reward as presented to loyalty program members in catalogs and redemption interfaces.']
  reward_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the reward in the catalog determining visibility and redemption availability.']
  reward_subcategory varchar [note: 'Secondary classification providing granular categorization within the primary reward category for enhanced filtering and reporting.']
  terms_and_conditions varchar [note: 'Legal terms, restrictions, blackout dates, usage limitations, and other conditions governing reward redemption and usage.']
  total_redemptions varchar [note: 'Cumulative count of all redemptions of this reward since its introduction, used for popularity analytics and program economics.']
  created_by varchar [note: 'User identifier or system account that created the reward catalog entry.']

  Note: 'Master catalog of all rewards available for redemption within the loyalty program, including issued reward instances (certificates and vouchers). Captures reward name, category (hotel stay, upgrade, dining, spa, experiences, merchandise, partner), points cost by tier, monetary value, availability type (always-on, limited, seasonal), inventory count, eligible member tiers, redemption channel, terms and conditions, supplier/partner reference, and active status. For issued instances: certificate type, face value, issue date, expiry date, redemption status (issued, redeemed, expired, voided), associated reservation, and issuing channel. SSOT for both what rewards are available and what reward instruments have been issued to members.'
}

  reservation_booking_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to reservation.reservation_booking. Business justification: When a loyalty benefit (free breakfast, room upgrade, late checkout) is consumed on a specific stay, the entitlement must reference the booking where it was applied. This enables benefit utilization r']
  stay_history_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to guest.stay_history. Business justification: Benefit fulfillment tracking requires knowing which stay consumed a benefit entitlement (e.g., complimentary breakfast, room upgrade). Loyalty operations and audit teams report on benefit utilization ']
  tier_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the loyalty tier that grants this benefit as a standard entitlement. Null if the benefit is individually granted outside of tier benefits.']

The role-prefix \'upgrade_\' disambiguates the target room type the member is entitled ']
  advance_booking_required_days varchar [note: 'The minimum number of days in advance that a reservation must be made to redeem this benefit. Null if no advance booking requirement exists.']
  auto_apply_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this benefit is automatically applied to eligible reservations or requires manual member selection. True if auto-applied, False if opt-in required.']
  benefit_description varchar [note: 'Detailed description of the benefit, including terms, conditions, and any restrictions or exclusions.']
  benefit_name varchar [note: 'Human-readable name of the benefit entitlement for display and communication purposes.']

  blackout_dates varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of date ranges during which this benefit cannot be redeemed, typically during peak demand periods or special events.']
  brand_restriction varchar [note: 'The brand code if this benefit is restricted to properties within a specific brand. Null if no brand restriction applies.']

Tier standard benefits are automatic based on member tier; status match benefits are granted when matching status from another program; manual grants are discretionary; promotion benefits are campaign-driven; compensation benefits are service recovery; partner benefits come from co-branded or partner integrations.']
  entitlement_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the benefit entitlement. Active entitlements can be redeemed; suspended entitlements are temporarily unavailable; expired entitlements have passed their validity period; revoked entitlements have been withdrawn; pending entitlements are awaiting activation.']
  expiry_date date [note: 'The date on which this benefit entitlement expires and can no longer be redeemed. Null for benefits with no expiration.']
