  minimum_stay_nights varchar [note: 'The minimum length of stay (LOS) in nights required to redeem this benefit. Null if no minimum stay requirement exists.']
  monetary_value decimal(10,2) [note: 'The estimated monetary value of this benefit in the property\'s base currency, used for program economics tracking and liability calculation.']
  notes varchar [note: 'Free-text field for additional comments, special instructions, or contextual information about this benefit entitlement.']
  points_multiplier decimal(5,2) [note: 'The bonus points multiplier applied to eligible stays when this benefit is active. For example, 1.5 means the member earns 50% bonus points. Null if this benefit does not include a points multiplier.']
  priority_rank varchar [note: 'The priority order for applying this benefit when multiple benefits are available. Lower numbers indicate higher priority. Used to resolve conflicts when benefits cannot be combined.']
  property_restriction varchar [note: 'Indicates whether this benefit can be redeemed at all properties, only at specific properties, within a specific brand, or within a specific geographic region.']
  region_restriction varchar [note: 'The geographic region code if this benefit is restricted to properties within a specific region. Null if no region restriction applies.']
  remaining_usage varchar [note: 'The number of redemptions remaining for this benefit. Calculated as usage_limit minus usage_count. Null if usage is unlimited.']
  revocation_reason varchar [note: 'The business reason or justification for revoking this benefit entitlement. Null if the benefit has not been revoked.']
  revoked_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this benefit entitlement was revoked. Null if the benefit has not been revoked.']
  source_system_code varchar [note: 'The unique identifier of this benefit entitlement in the source operational system.']
  transferable_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this benefit can be transferred to another loyalty member. True if transferable, False if non-transferable.']
  usage_count varchar [note: 'The number of times this benefit has been redeemed to date. Used to track remaining usage against the usage limit.']
  usage_limit varchar [note: 'The maximum number of times this benefit can be redeemed during its validity period. Null indicates unlimited usage.']

  Note: 'Master record of the specific benefits a loyalty member is entitled to based on their current tier and any individually granted benefits. Captures benefit type (complimentary breakfast, room upgrade, late checkout, lounge access, welcome amenity, bonus points multiplier), entitlement source (tier standard, status match, manual grant, promotion), effective date, expiry date, usage limit, and remaining usage count. Enables benefit delivery and tracking at the property level.'
}

Table loyalty.promotion {
  promotion_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the loyalty promotion. Primary key.']
  marketing_channel_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.channel. Business justification: Loyalty promotions are distributed through specific channels (OTA, direct, GDS). The plain-text marketing_channel attribute is a denormalization of channel.channel. Channel-level promotion performance']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.property. Business justification: Property marketing teams analyze which promotions drive enrollment and stays at their property for campaign ROI measurement. Currently qualifying_property_list is text; FK enables property-level promo']
  seasonal_calendar_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.seasonal_calendar. Business justification: Loyalty promotions (double points, bonus nights) are coordinated with seasonal demand periods. Linking promotion to seasonal_calendar enables revenue management teams to align loyalty incentives with ']
  tier_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the loyalty tier required to participate in this promotion. Null if promotion is open to all tiers. Used to restrict offers to specific membership levels (e.g., Gold, Platinum, Diamond).']
  approval_date date [note: 'Date when this promotion was formally approved for launch. Null if promotion is still in draft or pending approval. Used for campaign governance and audit trail.']
  approved_by varchar [note: 'Username or employee ID of the manager or director who approved this promotion for launch. Null if promotion is still in draft status. Used for governance and approval workflow tracking.']
  award_fulfillment_date date [note: 'Target date by which bonus points or nights will be posted to qualifying members\' accounts after promotion completion. Used for member communication and fulfillment SLA (Service Level Agreement) tracking.']
  bonus_nights_credit varchar [note: 'Number of bonus elite-qualifying nights awarded upon promotion completion. Used for tier progression acceleration. Null if promotion does not award night credits.']
  bonus_points_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Fixed number of bonus loyalty points awarded upon successful completion of promotion criteria. Null if bonus is not a fixed point amount (e.g., multiplier-based).']
  bonus_points_multiplier decimal(5,2) [note: 'Multiplier applied to base points earned during the promotion period. Example: 2.0 for double points, 1.5 for 50% bonus. Null if promotion awards fixed points rather than a multiplier.']
  budget_cap_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Maximum financial budget allocated for this promotion (total cost of all bonuses awarded). Promotion may be paused or closed early if budget is exhausted. Measured in base currency (typically USD).']
  budget_consumed_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Cumulative financial cost of bonuses awarded to date under this promotion. Updated as members complete qualifying activity and bonuses are posted. Used for budget tracking and ROI (Return on Investment) analysis.']
  cancellation_reason varchar [note: 'Explanation for why the promotion was cancelled or terminated early. Null if promotion completed normally or is still active. Examples: \'Budget exhausted\', \'Low engagement\', \'Business priority change\', \'Legal compliance issue\'.']
  code varchar [note: 'Externally-known unique alphanumeric code for the promotion, used in marketing materials and member enrollment. Example: BONUS2024, WELCOME500.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this promotion record was first created in the system. Used for audit trail and data lineage.']
  end_date date [note: 'Date when the promotion expires. Qualifying activity after this date does not count toward the promotion. Null for open-ended promotions.']
  minimum_nights varchar [note: 'Minimum number of qualifying nights required to earn the promotion bonus. Null if nights are not a qualifying criterion.']
  minimum_spend_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Minimum total spend (in base currency) required to qualify for the promotion. Null if spend is not a qualifying criterion. Typically measured in USD or property local currency.']
  name varchar [note: 'Human-readable name of the promotion displayed to members and in marketing channels. Example: \'Double Points Summer Getaway\', \'Elite Status Fast Track\'.']
  promotion_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle state of the promotion. Values: draft (being designed), scheduled (approved, not yet live), active (currently running), paused (temporarily suspended), completed (ended successfully), cancelled (terminated early).']
  promotion_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the promotion mechanism. Values: bonus_points_multiplier (earn extra points per dollar), double_nights (accelerate tier qualification), targeted_offer (personalized to segment), welcome_back (re-engagement), birthday_bonus (member birthday reward), spend_challenge (gamified spending goal).']
  qualifying_criteria_description varchar [note: 'Detailed narrative of the requirements a member must meet to earn the promotion bonus. Examples: \'Complete 3 stays between June 1 and August 31\', \'Spend minimum $500 on F&B (Food and Beverage) during stay\', \'Book via mobile app using rate code MOBILE2024\'.']
  qualifying_property_list varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of property IDs or property codes where stays qualify for this promotion. Null or \'ALL\' if promotion applies to all properties. Example: \'PROP001,PROP045,PROP102\' or \'ALL\'.']
  qualifying_rate_codes decimal [note: 'Comma-separated list of rate codes (BAR - Best Available Rate, corporate codes, promotional codes) that qualify for this promotion. Null or \'ALL\' if all rate codes qualify. Example: \'BAR,CORP,PROMO2024\'.']
  registration_required_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether members must explicitly register or opt-in to participate in this promotion. True = registration required before qualifying activity counts; False = automatic enrollment for eligible members.']
  stackable_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this promotion can be combined with other active promotions. True = member can earn bonuses from multiple promotions simultaneously; False = this promotion cannot be stacked with others.']
  start_date date [note: 'Date when the promotion becomes active and members can begin earning toward the bonus. Qualifying activity before this date does not count.']
  terms_and_conditions_url varchar [note: 'Web link to the full legal terms and conditions document for this promotion. Displayed to members during enrollment and in promotional materials.']
  total_completions varchar [note: 'Count of members who have successfully completed all qualifying criteria and earned the promotion bonus. Used for conversion rate and campaign effectiveness analysis.']
  total_enrollments varchar [note: 'Count of unique members who have enrolled or been auto-enrolled in this promotion. Used for campaign reach and engagement metrics.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this promotion record was last modified. Updated whenever any attribute changes. Used for change tracking and audit trail.']
  created_by varchar [note: 'Username or employee ID of the marketing or loyalty team member who created this promotion record. Used for audit trail and accountability.']

  Note: 'Master entity defining loyalty program promotions and bonus offers, including member participation tracking. Captures promotion name, type (bonus points multiplier, double nights, targeted offer, welcome back, birthday bonus, spend challenge), target segment or tier, qualifying criteria (minimum nights, minimum spend, specific properties, specific rate codes), bonus awarded, registration requirement, start/end dates, and budget cap. For member participation: enrollment date, enrollment channel, member promotion status (enrolled, in-progress, completed, expired, awarded), qualifying activity progress, bonus awarded flag, award date, and opt-out date. Drives personalized offer delivery, campaign economics, and promotion fulfillment tracking.'
}

Table loyalty.member_preference {
  member_preference_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the member preference record. Primary key.']
  member_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the loyalty member who holds this preference. Links to the loyalty member master record.']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.property. Business justification: Property guest services teams honor member preferences (e.g., \'never book me at this property\', \'preferred property for business travel\') during reservation and check-in. Currently restricted_property']
  room_type_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to inventory.room_type. Business justification: Member Preference Management — Room Type: member_preference records room-type preferences (preference_category=\'room_type\') with preference_value as a denormalized string. A proper FK to inventory.roo']
  brand_restriction varchar [note: 'The brand code if this preference is restricted to a specific brand within the portfolio. Nullable if preference applies across all brands.']
  confidence_level bigint [note: 'The confidence or reliability level of this preference. Stated preferences have highest confidence; inferred preferences are scored based on frequency and recency of observed behavior.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this preference record was first created in the loyalty system. Audit trail for record creation.']
  effective_date date [note: 'The date from which this preference becomes active and should be applied to member experiences.']
  expiration_date date [note: 'The date after which this preference is no longer valid or should no longer be applied. Nullable for preferences with no expiration.']
  last_confirmed_date date [note: 'The date when the member explicitly confirmed or reaffirmed this preference. Distinct from last_updated_date which may include system-inferred updates.']
  last_observed_date date [note: 'The most recent date when this preference was observed in a stay or interaction. Used for recency scoring in confidence calculations.']
  last_updated_date date [note: 'The date when this preference was last modified or confirmed by the member or system. Used to track recency for confidence scoring.']
  notes varchar [note: 'Free-text notes or additional context about this preference. May include special instructions, member comments, or operational guidance.']
  observation_count varchar [note: 'The number of times this preference has been observed in the member\'s stay history or interactions. Used to calculate confidence level for inferred preferences.']
  override_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this preference can be overridden by operational constraints or property-level decisions. True if override is allowed; false if preference must be honored.']
  preference_category varchar [note: 'The category or domain of the preference (e.g., room type, pillow type, floor preference, amenity preferences, dietary restrictions, communication channel, language, newspaper, housekeeping schedule). Classifies the type of personalization being captured. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: room_type|pillow_type|floor_preference|amenity|dietary_restriction|communication_channel|language|newspaper|housekeeping_schedule — promote to reference product]']
  preference_source varchar [note: 'The origin or channel through which this preference was captured (e.g., stated at enrollment, updated via mobile app, updated via website, captured by call center, inferred from stay history, imported from PMS profile).']
  preference_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of this preference record. Active preferences are used for personalization; inactive or expired preferences are retained for historical analysis.']
  preference_value decimal(18,2) [note: 'The specific value or selection for this preference (e.g., \'King Bed\', \'Hypoallergenic Pillow\', \'High Floor\', \'Vegetarian\', \'Email\'). Free-text or structured value depending on category.']
  priority_rank varchar [note: 'The priority or importance ranking of this preference relative to other preferences for the same member. Lower numbers indicate higher priority. Used when preferences conflict.']
  property_restriction varchar [note: 'Indicates whether this preference applies to all properties, a specific property, a brand, or a region. Supports property-specific personalization.']
  source_system_code varchar [note: 'The unique identifier for this preference record in the source system. Used for data lineage and reconciliation.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this preference record was last modified. Audit trail for record updates.']

  Note: 'Master record of a loyalty member\'s stated and inferred preferences used to personalize the hospitality experience. Captures preference category (room type, pillow type, floor preference, amenity preferences, dietary restrictions, communication channel, language, newspaper, housekeeping schedule), preference source (stated at enrollment, updated via app, inferred from stay history), confidence level, and last updated date. Distinct from guest domain preferences as this is loyalty-program-managed personalization data.'
}

Table loyalty.promotion_enrollment {
  promotion_enrollment_id varchar [pk, note: 'Primary key for the promotion_enrollment association']
  member_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking this enrollment record to the enrolled loyalty member.']
  promotion_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking this enrollment record to the parent loyalty promotion.']
  award_date date [note: 'Date when the bonus points or nights were posted to the member\'s account for this promotion enrollment. Used for fulfillment tracking and reconciliation.']
  completion_date date [note: 'Date when the member successfully completed all qualifying criteria for this promotion. Null if not yet completed. Source for promotion.total_completions aggregate.']
  enrollment_channel varchar [note: 'Channel through which the member enrolled in the promotion (e.g., web, mobile_app, front_desk, email_link, auto_enrolled). Belongs to the enrollment event, not to the member or promotion.']
  enrollment_date date [note: 'Date when the member enrolled or was auto-enrolled in the promotion. Belongs to the enrollment relationship, not to the member or promotion alone. Source for promotion.total_enrollments aggregate.']
  exclusion_list varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of member IDs or segments explicitly excluded from this promotion (e.g., employees, test accounts, members who opted out). Null if no exclusions apply. [Moved from promotion: The exclusion_list on promotion is an anti-pattern (comma-separated member IDs stored as STRING). Member-level exclusion state belongs in the enrollment association as a status value (e.g., status = \'excluded\') or as a separate exclusion flag on the enrollment record. This attribute should be removed from promotion and replaced by querying enrollment records with excluded status.]']
  opt_out_date date [note: 'Date when the member opted out of this specific promotion enrollment. Null if still active or completed. Belongs to the enrollment lifecycle.']
  points_awarded decimal(18,2) [note: 'Actual bonus points awarded to this member upon completion of this promotion. May differ from promotion.bonus_points_amount if pro-rated or adjusted. Belongs to the enrollment outcome, not to the member\'s lifetime balance or the promotion\'s budget.']
  promotion_enrollment_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle state of this member\'s participation in the promotion. Tracks progress from enrollment through completion or expiry.']
  qualifying_spend_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Cumulative qualifying spend the member has accumulated toward this promotion\'s minimum_spend_amount requirement. Belongs to the enrollment relationship.']
  qualifying_stays_count varchar [note: 'Number of qualifying stays the member has accumulated toward this promotion\'s minimum_nights requirement. Belongs to the enrollment relationship as it tracks progress specific to this member-promotion pair.']
  registration_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Precise timestamp of the enrollment event, capturing the exact moment the member registered. Used for audit trail and channel attribution.']

  Note: 'This association product represents the Enrollment event between a loyalty promotion and a loyalty member. It captures the full lifecycle of a member\'s participation in a specific promotion — from registration through qualifying activity progress to bonus award or expiry. Each record links one promotion to one member and carries attributes that exist only in the context of that specific member-promotion participation: enrollment channel, status, qualifying progress, and award outcome. This is the operational source of truth for promotion fulfillment tracking and the source for the aggregate counters (total_enrollments, total_completions) on the promotion entity.. Existence Justification: In loyalty program operations, a member can enroll in multiple promotions simultaneously (e.g., a birthday bonus AND a spend challenge AND a double nights offer), and each promotion is designed to attract and track hundreds or thousands of members. The business actively manages each member-promotion enrollment as a distinct operational record — tracking enrollment date, progress toward qualifying criteria, completion status, and bonus award. This is a textbook operational M:N: the enrollment itself is a named business concept with rich lifecycle data that belongs to neither the promotion nor the member alone.'
}

Table channel.channel {
  channel_id varchar [pk, note: 'Primary key for channel']
  ota_partner_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.ota_partner. Business justification: Many distribution channels are operated by OTA partners (e.g., Expedia operates multiple channels/brands). This FK establishes the ownership relationship. Removes redundant platform_name which can be ']
  activation_date date [note: 'Date on which this distribution channel was first activated and began accepting live bookings. Distinct from contract_start_date which reflects the commercial agreement date. Used for channel onboarding tracking and performance benchmarking from go-live.']
  bar_eligible boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this channel is eligible to display and sell the Best Available Rate (BAR) — the lowest publicly available rate at the time of booking. True = BAR rates are distributed to this channel; False = channel receives only specific contracted or negotiated rates. Drives rate distribution strategy in IDeaS G3 RMS and Sabre SynXis CRS.']
  booking_fee_usd decimal(18,2) [note: 'Per-transaction booking fee charged by the channel in addition to or instead of a commission percentage, expressed in USD. Common in GDS channels (e.g., GDS segment fee per booking). Used in cost-of-acquisition and channel profitability analysis.']
  cancellation_policy_code varchar [note: 'Code referencing the default cancellation policy applied to bookings made through this channel (e.g., \'24H_FREE\', \'48H_PENALTY\', \'NON_REFUNDABLE\'). Cancellation policies may differ by channel based on contractual agreements. Managed in Oracle OPERA PMS and Sabre SynXis CRS.']
  category varchar [note: 'High-level grouping of the channel by booking relationship: DIRECT = guest books directly with the property (web, mobile, voice, corporate direct); INDIRECT = third-party intermediary involved (OTA, GDS, wholesaler, metasearch); OPAQUE = rate and property identity concealed until after booking (e.g., Hotwire, Priceline opaque). Drives cost-of-acquisition analysis and channel mix strategy.']
  channel_status varchar [note: 'Current operational lifecycle status of the distribution channel. active = channel is live and accepting bookings; inactive = channel is configured but not currently selling; suspended = channel temporarily halted (e.g., rate parity violation, connectivity issue); pending_activation = channel onboarded but not yet live; decommissioned = channel permanently retired.']
  channel_type varchar [note: 'Categorical classification of the distribution channel by its market segment and technology interface. OTA = Online Travel Agency (e.g., Expedia, Booking.com); GDS = Global Distribution System (e.g., Sabre, Amadeus, Galileo); DIRECT_WEB = brand.com web booking; DIRECT_MOBILE = brand mobile app; VOICE = call center reservations; CORPORATE_DIRECT = negotiated corporate accounts; WHOLESALER = tour operators and bed banks; METASEARCH = Google Hotel Ads, Trivago. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: OTA|GDS|DIRECT_WEB|DIRECT_MOBILE|VOICE|CORPORATE_DIRECT|WHOLESALER|METASEARCH — promote to reference product]']
  code varchar [note: 'Externally-known alphanumeric code uniquely identifying the distribution channel across enterprise systems including Sabre SynXis CRS, Oracle OPERA PMS, and IDeaS G3 RMS. Used for channel mapping and cross-system reconciliation.']
  commission_basis varchar [note: 'The commercial model under which commission is calculated for this channel. NET_RATE = channel marks up a net rate provided by the property; GROSS_RATE = commission deducted from the gross rate charged to the guest; MARKUP = channel applies a markup over the property\'s net rate; FLAT_FEE = fixed fee per booking regardless of rate. Critical for accurate revenue and cost-of-acquisition reporting.']
  commission_rate_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Standard commission percentage charged by this distribution channel on each booking, expressed as a percentage of the room revenue (e.g., 15.00 for 15%). Drives cost-of-acquisition calculations and net revenue reporting per USALI standards. Confidential as it reflects negotiated commercial terms.']
  connectivity_fee_usd decimal(18,2) [note: 'Annual or periodic connectivity/subscription fee charged by the channel or switch provider for maintaining the technical integration, expressed in USD. Included in total cost-of-acquisition analysis alongside commission. Confidential as it reflects negotiated commercial terms.']
  connectivity_method varchar [note: 'Technical integration method used to connect the property management system or CRS to this distribution channel. API = RESTful or SOAP API integration; XML = XML-based messaging (e.g., OTA XML); SFTP = file-based batch transfer; DIRECT_CONNECT = proprietary direct connection; SWITCH = via a channel manager switch (e.g., SiteMinder, Channex); MANUAL = manually managed extranet updates. Impacts SLA and rate update latency.']
  content_distribution_enabled boolean [note: 'Indicates whether property content (room descriptions, images, amenities, policies) is actively distributed to this channel via a content API or content management system. True = content is pushed/synced to this channel; False = content is managed manually or not distributed. Relevant for OTA and metasearch channels.']
  contract_end_date date [note: 'Date on which the commercial agreement with this distribution channel expires or is scheduled to terminate. Null for evergreen/open-ended agreements. Used for contract renewal management and channel lifecycle planning. Stored in yyyy-MM-dd format.']
  contract_start_date date [note: 'Date on which the commercial agreement with this distribution channel became effective. Used for contract lifecycle management, commission audit trails, and regulatory compliance. Stored in yyyy-MM-dd format.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this distribution channel record was first created in the enterprise data platform. Stored in yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss.SSSXXX format. Used for audit trail, data lineage, and record lifecycle management.']
  crs_channel_code varchar [note: 'Channel identifier as configured in the Sabre SynXis Central Reservation System (CRS). Used for cross-system reconciliation between the enterprise data lakehouse and the CRS source of record. Enables traceability of bookings back to the originating CRS channel configuration.']
  deactivation_date date [note: 'Date on which this distribution channel was deactivated or decommissioned. Null for currently active channels. Used for channel lifecycle management, historical reporting, and audit trails. Stored in yyyy-MM-dd format.']
  description varchar [note: 'Free-text description of the distribution channel, including its market positioning, target guest segment, special contractual terms, or operational notes. Used for channel management documentation and onboarding reference.']
  gdpr_data_processor boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this distribution channel acts as a GDPR data processor for guest personal data collected during the booking process. True = a Data Processing Agreement (DPA) is in place with this channel; False = channel does not process personal data on behalf of the property. Required for GDPR compliance and data governance.']
  gds_chain_code varchar [note: 'Two-letter GDS chain code assigned to the hotel brand or property group within Global Distribution Systems (Sabre, Amadeus, Galileo/Travelport, Worldspan). Required for GDS-type channels to route availability and rate requests correctly. Null for non-GDS channels.']
  geographic_scope varchar [note: 'Geographic reach of this distribution channel. GLOBAL = channel operates worldwide; REGIONAL = channel serves a specific geographic region (e.g., Asia-Pacific, Europe); DOMESTIC = channel serves a single country; LOCAL = channel serves a specific city or metro area. Used for channel mix strategy and market segmentation analysis.']
  inventory_allocation_method varchar [note: 'Method by which room inventory is allocated to this distribution channel. POOLED = channel draws from the shared central inventory pool (real-time); ALLOTMENT = a fixed block of rooms is pre-allocated to the channel; FREE_SALE = channel can sell without prior allocation up to a defined limit; ON_REQUEST = bookings require manual confirmation. Managed in IDeaS G3 RMS and Sabre SynXis CRS.']
  last_room_availability boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this channel has Last Room Availability (LRA) rights — meaning the property must make the last available room accessible through this channel at the contracted rate. LRA is a common contractual obligation in corporate and GDS agreements. True = LRA applies; False = LRA does not apply.']
  last_updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this distribution channel record was most recently modified in the enterprise data platform. Stored in yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss.SSSXXX format. Used for change tracking, data freshness monitoring, and audit compliance.']
  loyalty_bookings_eligible boolean [note: 'Indicates whether bookings made through this channel are eligible for loyalty program points accrual and redemption. True = loyalty points are awarded and redeemable; False = bookings through this channel do not qualify for loyalty benefits (common for opaque OTA channels). Managed in Salesforce CRM Loyalty Management.']
  mice_bookings_supported boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this distribution channel supports group and MICE (Meetings, Incentives, Conferences, Exhibitions) bookings in addition to transient reservations. True = MICE/group bookings can be sourced through this channel; False = transient bookings only. Relevant for event sales and Delphi by Amadeus integration.']
  name varchar [note: 'Human-readable name of the distribution channel (e.g., \'Expedia Partner Central\', \'Booking.com Extranet\', \'Sabre GDS\', \'Direct Web\', \'Voice Reservations\'). Used in reporting, dashboards, and channel mix analysis.']
  nrr_eligible boolean [note: 'Indicates whether Non-Refundable Rate (NRR) products are distributed through this channel. True = NRR fences are available on this channel; False = only flexible/refundable rates are distributed. Impacts revenue management yield strategy and cancellation policy enforcement.']
  payment_model decimal(18,2) [note: 'Defines who collects payment from the guest for bookings made through this channel. HOTEL_COLLECT = property collects payment directly at check-in/check-out; CHANNEL_COLLECT = the OTA or intermediary collects payment and remits net to the property; SPLIT = partial payment collected by each party. Impacts accounts receivable and revenue recognition per USALI and GAAP/IFRS.']
  pci_compliant boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this distribution channel is certified as compliant with PCI DSS (Payment Card Industry Data Security Standard) for handling cardholder data. True = channel holds current PCI DSS certification; False = channel is not PCI compliant or certification has lapsed. Required for risk management and payment security governance.']
  primary_market_country_code bigint [note: 'ISO 3166-1 alpha-3 country code of the primary market served by this distribution channel (e.g., \'USA\', \'GBR\', \'DEU\'). Used for geographic channel mix analysis, market penetration reporting, and regulatory compliance (e.g., GDPR for EU-based channels).']
  priority_rank varchar [note: 'Numeric rank indicating the strategic priority of this channel in the distribution mix, where lower numbers indicate higher priority (e.g., 1 = highest priority, typically direct web). Used by revenue management to determine inventory release sequencing and rate strategy. Configured in IDeaS G3 RMS and Sabre SynXis CRS.']
  rate_parity_required boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this distribution channel contractually requires rate parity — i.e., the property must offer the same or lower rates on this channel as on any other channel. True = rate parity clause is active in the channel agreement; False = no rate parity obligation. Critical for revenue management compliance and rate strategy.']
  rate_parity_type varchar [note: 'Specifies the scope of the rate parity obligation for this channel. BROAD = property must match rates across all channels including direct; NARROW = property must match rates on other OTAs but may offer lower rates on direct channels (common post-EU regulatory changes); NONE = no rate parity obligation. Drives revenue management and direct booking strategy.']
  remittance_frequency varchar [note: 'Frequency at which the channel remits collected payments to the property for CHANNEL_COLLECT payment model bookings. Applicable only when payment_model is CHANNEL_COLLECT or SPLIT. Drives accounts receivable forecasting and cash flow management in SAP S/4HANA.']
  sla_response_time_seconds varchar [note: 'Maximum allowable response time in seconds for availability and rate queries from this channel, as defined in the channel\'s Service Level Agreement (SLA). Used to monitor channel connectivity performance and enforce SLA compliance. Typical values: 3 seconds for OTA/GDS, 5 seconds for XML channels.']
  sla_uptime_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Contractually committed uptime percentage for this channel\'s connectivity, expressed as a percentage (e.g., 99.90 for 99.9% uptime). Used to monitor channel reliability and enforce SLA penalties. Managed against actual uptime metrics in channel performance reporting.']
  supported_currencies varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of ISO 4217 three-letter currency codes supported by this distribution channel for booking and payment (e.g., \'USD,EUR,GBP,JPY\'). Relevant for multi-currency rate distribution and foreign exchange management. Managed in Sabre SynXis CRS.']
  supported_languages varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of ISO 639-1 two-letter language codes supported by this channel for content display and guest communication (e.g., \'en,fr,de,zh,ja\'). Relevant for content localization strategy and international market reach.']

  Note: 'Master registry of all distribution channels through which Travel Hospitality properties sell inventory, including OTA platforms (Expedia, Booking.com), GDS networks (Sabre, Amadeus, Galileo), direct web/mobile, voice/call center, corporate direct, wholesalers, and metasearch engines. Captures channel type, connectivity method, commission tier, rate parity obligations, and channel-level SLA parameters. This is the SSOT for channel identity across the enterprise.'
}

Table channel.ota_partner {
  ota_partner_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique surrogate identifier for the OTA partner record in the silver layer lakehouse. Primary key for the ota_partner master data product.']
  affiliate_network boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the OTA partner operates an affiliate or sub-distribution network through which third-party websites or agents can book on behalf of the OTA. True = affiliate network active; False = direct OTA platform only. Relevant for booking source attribution accuracy.']
  base_commission_rate_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Standard commission percentage charged by the OTA partner on each confirmed booking, expressed as a percentage of the gross booking value (e.g., 15.00 = 15%). Foundational input for cost-of-acquisition (COA) and channel profitability analysis.']
  cancellation_policy_type varchar [note: 'Default cancellation policy type applied to bookings made through this OTA channel. Flexible = free cancellation up to 24-48 hours; Moderate = partial penalty; Strict = high penalty; Non_Refundable = NRR (Non-Refundable Rate) — no refund on cancellation. Impacts revenue management and guest experience.']
  channel_manager_platform varchar [note: 'Name of the channel manager or switch platform used to manage the technical connectivity to this OTA partner (e.g., Sabre SynXis, Siteminder, Amadeus iHotelier, RateGain). Relevant when connectivity is not direct API-to-API.']
  commission_model varchar [note: 'Commercial model governing how the OTA partner earns revenue. Net Rate = hotel sells at net, OTA marks up; Merchant = OTA collects full payment and remits net; Agency = OTA collects commission on hotel-collected payment; Retail = standard published rate with commission; Opaque = rate hidden from consumer until post-booking (e.g., Hotwire).']
  connectivity_fee_frequency decimal(18,2) [note: 'Frequency at which the connectivity fee is billed by the OTA partner or channel manager. Annual = yearly flat fee; Monthly = recurring monthly; Per_Booking = transactional fee per confirmed booking; One_Time = setup/onboarding fee only.']
  connectivity_fee_usd decimal(18,2) [note: 'Annual or per-transaction connectivity fee charged by the OTA partner or channel manager for maintaining the technical integration (API/XML/GDS switch). Expressed in USD. Used for total cost-of-acquisition (COA) calculation and channel profitability reporting per USALI.']
  connectivity_protocol varchar [note: 'Technical protocol used for two-way inventory, rate, and availability (IRA) connectivity between the hotel\'s CRS/PMS and the OTA partner. XML = legacy XML push/pull; REST_API = modern RESTful API; GDS = Global Distribution System switch; SFTP = file-based batch; OTA_XML = OpenTravel Alliance XML standard; HTNG = HTNG web services.']
  content_score decimal(5,2) [note: 'Numeric score (typically 0–100) representing the completeness and quality of the hotel\'s content (photos, descriptions, amenities) on the OTA partner\'s platform. Higher scores correlate with improved search ranking and conversion rates. Sourced from OTA partner reporting APIs.']
  contract_effective_date date [note: 'Date on which the master distribution agreement with the OTA partner becomes legally binding and operational. Governs the start of commission obligations and rate parity clauses.']
  contract_expiry_date date [note: 'Date on which the master distribution agreement with the OTA partner expires or is scheduled for renewal. Null indicates an evergreen/open-ended contract. Used for contract renewal management and risk monitoring.']
  contract_reference varchar [note: 'Unique reference number of the master distribution agreement or contract executed with the OTA partner. Links to the contract management repository in SAP S/4HANA for financial and legal audit purposes.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when the OTA partner record was first created in the data platform. Supports data lineage, audit trail, and silver layer ingestion tracking. Format: yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss.SSSXXX.']
  data_sharing_agreement boolean [note: 'Indicates whether a formal data sharing agreement (DSA) is in place with the OTA partner governing the exchange of guest booking data, anonymised analytics, and performance reporting. Required for GDPR and CCPA compliance when guest PII is transmitted.']
  gdpr_data_processor boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the OTA partner is formally designated as a GDPR Data Processor under Article 28, processing guest personal data on behalf of the hotel as Data Controller. True = Data Processing Agreement (DPA) executed; False = not designated as processor.']
  gds_chain_code varchar [note: 'Two-letter chain code assigned by the Global Distribution System (GDS) to identify the hotel brand/chain within GDS networks (Sabre, Amadeus, Travelport). Applicable only when connectivity_protocol is GDS. Null for non-GDS OTA partners.']
  hq_country_code bigint [note: 'ISO 3166-1 alpha-3 country code of the country where the OTA partner\'s legal headquarters is registered. Used for tax treaty application, withholding tax determination, and regulatory jurisdiction identification.']
  inventory_allocation_model varchar [note: 'Model governing how room inventory is made available to the OTA partner. Free_Sell = real-time availability from CRS with no pre-allocated block; Allotment = pre-contracted room block allocated to the OTA; On_Request = bookings require manual confirmation. Managed in IDeaS G3 RMS and Sabre SynXis.']
  last_room_availability boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the OTA partner contract includes a Last Room Availability (LRA) clause, requiring the hotel to make its last available room accessible to this channel. LRA clauses impact revenue management inventory controls and are tracked in IDeaS G3 RMS.']
  legal_entity_name varchar [note: 'Full registered legal name of the OTA partner organisation as it appears on the master distribution agreement (e.g., Expedia, Inc.; Booking Holdings B.V.). Used for contract management, AP reconciliation, and regulatory filings.']
  market_coverage varchar [note: 'Description of the primary geographic markets or regions where the OTA partner has significant consumer reach and booking volume (e.g., \'North America, Western Europe\'; \'Asia-Pacific\'; \'Global\'). Used for channel mix optimisation and market-specific distribution strategy.']
  mobile_app_channel boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the OTA partner operates a dedicated mobile application channel through which bookings are made. True = mobile app channel is active and tracked separately for attribution; False = desktop/web only. Supports channel mix and mobile booking trend analysis.']
  ota_account_manager_email varchar [note: 'Business email address of the OTA partner\'s designated account manager. Used for commercial communications, promotional campaign coordination, and escalation. Classified as confidential PII per GDPR Article 4.']
  ota_account_manager_name varchar [note: 'Full name of the OTA partner\'s designated account manager or market manager assigned to the hotel account. Primary point of contact for commercial negotiations, promotional campaigns, and issue resolution.']
  ota_account_manager_phone varchar [note: 'Business phone number of the OTA partner\'s designated account manager. Used for urgent escalations and commercial negotiations. Classified as confidential PII per GDPR Article 4.']
  partner_code varchar [note: 'Short alphanumeric code uniquely identifying the OTA partner within the Central Reservation System (CRS) and Property Management System (PMS). Used for channel mapping, rate distribution, and booking source attribution in Sabre SynXis and Oracle OPERA.']
  partner_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the OTA partner relationship. Active = live and distributing inventory; Pending = contract under negotiation or connectivity setup in progress; Suspended = temporarily halted (e.g., rate parity breach); Terminated = contract ended.']
  partner_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the distribution partner by channel category. OTA = Online Travel Agency (Expedia, Booking.com); GDS = Global Distribution System (Sabre, Amadeus); METASEARCH = price comparison engine (Google Hotel Ads, Trivago); DIRECT = brand.com or call centre; WHOLESALE = tour operator/bed bank; AFFILIATE = sub-affiliate network. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: OTA|GDS|METASEARCH|DIRECT|WHOLESALE|AFFILIATE — promote to reference product if additional types emerge]']
  payment_collection_party decimal(18,2) [note: 'Identifies which party collects payment from the guest. Hotel = property collects at check-in/check-out (agency model); OTA = OTA collects full payment and remits net to hotel (merchant model); Split = partial payment collected by each party.']
  preferred_commission_rate_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Negotiated commission rate applicable when the property holds preferred partner or sponsored placement status with the OTA. Typically lower than the base rate in exchange for enhanced visibility or placement. Null if preferred status is not applicable.']
  preferred_partner boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the hotel or brand holds preferred partner or sponsored placement status with this OTA, typically in exchange for a higher commission rate or marketing investment. Preferred partners receive enhanced search ranking and visibility on the OTA platform.']
  primary_market_country_code bigint [note: 'ISO 3166-1 alpha-3 country code representing the OTA partner\'s primary consumer market or country of dominant booking volume (e.g., USA, GBR, SGP). Used for geographic channel attribution and market penetration analysis.']
  rate_parity_clause boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the OTA partner contract includes a rate parity clause requiring the hotel to offer rates no lower on other channels than those offered on this OTA. True = rate parity clause is active; False = no rate parity obligation. Critical for revenue management and legal compliance monitoring.']
  rate_parity_type varchar [note: 'Specifies the scope of the rate parity obligation. Broad = hotel cannot offer lower rates on ANY channel including its own website; Narrow = hotel cannot offer lower rates on OTHER OTAs but may offer lower rates on its own direct channels; None = no parity obligation. Relevant for EU regulatory compliance following rate parity investigations.']
  remittance_cycle_days varchar [note: 'Number of days after the guest check-out date within which the OTA partner remits commission payments or net booking proceeds to the hotel. Used for cash flow forecasting and AP/AR reconciliation in SAP S/4HANA (e.g., 30 = net-30 terms).']
  review_count varchar [note: 'Total number of guest reviews published on the OTA partner\'s platform for the hotel. Used alongside review_score to assess statistical significance and platform engagement. Sourced from OTA partner reporting APIs.']
  review_score decimal(4,2) [note: 'Average guest review score for the hotel as published on the OTA partner\'s platform (e.g., Booking.com score out of 10, Expedia score out of 5). Used for reputation management, competitive benchmarking, and NPS/GSS correlation analysis via Medallia.']
  tax_registration_number bigint [note: 'VAT, GST, or equivalent tax registration number of the OTA partner\'s legal entity. Required for tax invoice processing, withholding tax compliance, and AP reconciliation in SAP S/4HANA.']
  trade_name varchar [note: 'Consumer-facing brand name under which the OTA partner operates (e.g., Hotels.com, Agoda). May differ from the legal entity name when the OTA operates multiple consumer brands under one legal umbrella.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when the OTA partner record was most recently modified in the data platform. Used for change data capture (CDC), incremental ETL processing, and audit compliance. Format: yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss.SSSXXX.']

  Note: 'Master data for Online Travel Agency partners including Expedia, Booking.com, Agoda, Hotels.com, Airbnb, and regional OTAs. Captures partner legal entity, contract reference, commission rate tiers, connectivity protocol (XML/API/GDS), rate parity clause status, preferred partner designation, market coverage, and account management contacts. Distinct from the channel record — an OTA partner may operate multiple channels (desktop, mobile app, affiliate).'
}

Table channel.gds_connection {
  gds_connection_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique surrogate identifier for each GDS connection configuration record in the silver layer lakehouse. Primary key for this master configuration entity.']
  booking_source_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.booking_source. Business justification: GDS connections are associated with specific booking source codes for attribution when reservations come through GDS channels. Many GDS connections per booking source. Removes redundant booking_source']
  channel_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the parent distribution channel record associated with this GDS connection, enabling channel mix analysis and cost-of-acquisition reporting.']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the property for which this GDS connection is configured. Links the GDS connectivity record to the specific hotel or resort property.']
  activation_date date [note: 'Date on which this GDS connection was first activated and made live for bookings. Used for contract term tracking, connectivity health history, and channel distribution reporting.']
  availability_sync_method varchar [note: 'Method by which room availability is synchronized between the property management system and the GDS. Real-time provides instant updates; batch updates on a scheduled interval; on_request queries availability at booking time; seamless provides live two-way availability.']
  chain_code varchar [note: 'Two- to four-character hotel chain code registered with the GDS network, identifying the hotel brand or management company within the GDS. Assigned by the GDS provider and used for inventory and rate loading.']
  commission_rate_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Percentage commission payable to travel agents or GDS intermediaries on bookings made through this GDS connection. Used for commission accrual, accounts payable processing, and channel cost analysis per USALI standards.']
  connection_status varchar [note: 'Current operational lifecycle status of the GDS connection. Active indicates live booking capability; suspended indicates temporary halt; pending_activation indicates setup in progress; decommissioned indicates permanently retired.']
  connectivity_fee_monthly_usd decimal(18,2) [note: 'Fixed monthly fee charged by the GDS provider or switch vendor for maintaining the technical connectivity of this GDS connection. Distinct from per-segment fees; used for OpEx budgeting and channel cost allocation.']
  connectivity_type varchar [note: 'Technical connectivity model used for this GDS connection. Direct connect provides real-time two-way communication; switch connect routes through a switch provider; seamless provides full availability and rate transparency; standard uses batch updates.']
  contract_end_date date [note: 'Expiration date of the GDS connectivity contract. Null for evergreen contracts. Used for renewal alerts, contract renegotiation planning, and channel distribution continuity management.']
  contract_start_date date [note: 'Effective start date of the GDS connectivity contract governing this connection. Used for contract lifecycle management, renewal planning, and financial obligation tracking.']
  corporate_rate_enabled boolean [note: 'Indicates whether negotiated corporate rates are loaded and accessible through this GDS connection. Corporate rates are a primary revenue stream for GDS channels and require specific rate plan configuration in the CRS.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this GDS connection configuration record was first created in the system. Used for audit trail, data lineage, and record lifecycle tracking in the silver layer lakehouse.']
  crs_interface_code varchar [note: 'Identifier for the CRS-to-GDS interface configuration within Sabre SynXis CRS. Links the GDS connection to the specific CRS interface instance managing rate distribution and availability synchronization.']
  currency_code varchar [note: 'ISO 4217 three-letter currency code in which rates are loaded and displayed to travel agents in this GDS connection. Ensures rate accuracy and currency consistency for international GDS distribution.']
  deactivation_date date [note: 'Date on which this GDS connection was or is scheduled to be deactivated. Null for currently active connections. Used for contract lifecycle management and channel distribution planning.']
  display_priority varchar [note: 'Numeric priority ranking that determines the property\'s display order in GDS search results for travel agents. Lower values indicate higher priority. Influenced by GDS tier, participation level, and performance metrics.']
  gds_name varchar [note: 'Human-readable name of the GDS provider (Sabre, Amadeus, Galileo, Worldspan, Travelport). Used for reporting, dashboards, and channel mix analysis.']
  gds_network_code varchar [note: 'Industry-standard two-character GDS network identifier assigned by IATA/ARC. 1S=Sabre, 1A=Amadeus, 1G=Galileo/Travelport, 1P=Worldspan. Used for routing and segment fee attribution.']
  gds_tier varchar [note: 'Participation tier level for this GDS connection, reflecting the level of GDS merchandising, display priority, and content features contracted. Preferred tier provides enhanced display and content capabilities; standard is base participation; basic is minimal listing.']
  health_check_status varchar [note: 'Result of the most recent automated health check for this GDS connection. Healthy indicates full two-way connectivity; degraded indicates partial functionality; failed indicates connectivity loss; unknown indicates health check has not been performed.']
  last_health_check_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp of the most recent automated connectivity health check performed for this GDS connection. Used for SLA monitoring, connectivity uptime reporting, and proactive issue detection.']
  lra_enabled boolean [note: 'Indicates whether Last Room Availability (LRA) is enabled for this GDS connection, requiring the property to make the last available room accessible to GDS bookers. LRA is a contractual obligation with some GDS providers and corporate accounts.']
  max_advance_booking_days varchar [note: 'Maximum number of days in advance that reservations can be booked through this GDS connection. Controls the booking window loaded to the GDS and aligns with the Revenue Management System (RMS) inventory control horizon.']
  min_advance_booking_days varchar [note: 'Minimum number of days in advance that reservations must be booked through this GDS connection. Supports Last Room Availability (LRA) and advance purchase rate controls managed by the Revenue Management System.']
  notes varchar [note: 'Free-text operational notes regarding this GDS connection, including special configuration requirements, known issues, contractual exceptions, or migration history. Used by channel distribution and revenue management teams.']
  nrr_supported boolean [note: 'Indicates whether Non-Refundable Rates (NRR) can be loaded and booked through this GDS connection. NRR support is a key revenue management capability enabling advance purchase rate strategies via GDS.']
  property_code_gds varchar [note: 'The unique property identifier as registered within the specific GDS network. May differ from the internal PMS property code. Used for inventory display and booking routing within the GDS.']
  pseudo_city_code varchar [note: 'GDS-assigned Pseudo City Code (PCC) that identifies the travel agency or booking office within the GDS network. Used for commission tracking, segment attribution, and agency relationship management.']
  rate_loading_protocol varchar [note: 'The technical protocol or standard used to load and update rate plans into the GDS. HTNG and OTA are XML-based standards; DHISCO is a switch-based protocol; manual indicates rates are loaded via GDS terminal; API indicates direct programmatic loading.']
  rate_parity_enforced boolean [note: 'Indicates whether rate parity is contractually enforced for this GDS connection, requiring that rates loaded to the GDS match the Best Available Rate (BAR) offered on direct channels. Critical for OTA and GDS contract compliance monitoring.']
  rate_plan_count varchar [note: 'Number of distinct rate plans currently loaded and active for this GDS connection. Used to monitor rate plan coverage, identify gaps in GDS rate distribution, and support rate parity audits.']
  rate_update_frequency varchar [note: 'Frequency at which rate updates are pushed from the Revenue Management System (RMS) or CRS to this GDS connection. Real-time supports dynamic pricing; scheduled frequencies reflect batch update configurations.']
  segment_fee_currency decimal(18,2) [note: 'ISO 4217 three-letter currency code for the GDS segment fee. Enables multi-currency cost-of-acquisition reporting for properties operating in non-USD markets.']
  segment_fee_usd decimal(18,2) [note: 'Per-booking segment fee charged by the GDS provider in US dollars for each reservation booked through this GDS connection. A GDS segment is one hotel booking transaction. Used for cost-of-acquisition analysis and channel profitability reporting.']
  support_contact_email varchar [note: 'Email address for the GDS provider\'s technical support team for this connection. Used for connectivity issue escalation, health check alerts, and SLA breach notifications.']
  switch_provider varchar [note: 'Name of the third-party switch provider (e.g., DHISCO, TravelClick, Pegasus) used to route availability and rate data between the CRS and the GDS, when connectivity_type is switch_connect. Null for direct connect configurations.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this GDS connection configuration record was most recently modified. Used for change tracking, incremental ETL processing, and audit compliance in the silver layer lakehouse.']
  uptime_sla_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Contractually agreed minimum uptime percentage for this GDS connection as specified in the GDS connectivity SLA. Used for vendor performance monitoring and contract compliance reporting.']

  Note: 'Master configuration record for each Global Distribution System connection (Sabre, Amadeus, Galileo/Travelport, Worldspan). Captures GDS network identifier, property chain code, pseudo city code (PCC), connectivity status, rate loading protocol, availability sync method, segment fee structure, and GDS-specific rate plan mappings. Supports GDS segment fee tracking and connectivity health monitoring.'
}

Table channel.crs_channel_mapping {

Removes redundant booking_source_code which can be retrieved via F']

The crs_channel_mapping table has crs_rate_plan_code and channel_rate_plan_code (STRING). Adding chan']
  gds_connection_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.gds_connection. Business justification: CRS channel mappings can be specific to GDS connections when the channel is a GDS. Adding nullable gds_connection_id FK allows linking CRS mappings to specific GDS connection configurations (Sabre, Am']
  inventory_room_type_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to inventory.room_type. Business justification: CRS channel mappings must link channel room type codes to physical inventory room types for rate loading, availability synchronization, and booking fulfillment. Essential for channel manager operation']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the hotel or resort property for which this CRS channel mapping is configured. Links the mapping to the specific property in the property master.']
  cancellation_policy_code varchar [note: 'Code identifying the cancellation policy applied to bookings made through this channel mapping (e.g., \'FLEX24H\' for 24-hour free cancellation, \'NRR\' for non-refundable). Determines the terms communicated to guests at the point of booking on the channel.']
  channel_contract_reference varchar [note: 'Reference number or identifier of the commercial contract governing the distribution relationship with this channel (e.g., OTA master agreement number, GDS connectivity contract ID). Used for contract management, commission dispute resolution, and audit compliance.']
  channel_property_code varchar [note: 'The property identifier code as recognized by the distribution channel (e.g., Booking.com hotel ID, Expedia property ID, GDS chain/property code). Used to match the CRS property to the channel\'s own property record during rate and availability pushes.']
  channel_type varchar [note: 'Categorical classification of the distribution channel type. Determines the connectivity protocol, commission structure, and rate parity rules applicable to this mapping. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: ota|gds|direct_web|voice|mobile|wholesaler|corporate|metasearch — promote to reference product]']
  commission_rate_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'The commission percentage charged by the distribution channel on bookings made through this mapping (e.g., 15.00 for 15%). Used for cost-of-acquisition analysis, channel profitability reporting, and USALI-compliant distribution cost accounting. Classified as confidential due to contractual sensitivity.']
  connectivity_fee_usd decimal(18,2) [note: 'Fixed or per-booking connectivity fee charged by the channel or GDS switch for maintaining the distribution connection, expressed in USD. Used in total cost-of-acquisition calculations and channel ROI analysis per USALI standards.']
  connectivity_protocol varchar [note: 'The technical messaging protocol used for rate and availability distribution between Sabre SynXis CRS and the channel (e.g., OTA XML, HTNG, OpenTravel Alliance ARI). Determines the message format and integration method. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: OTA_XML|HTNG|OpenTravel|ARI|TravelPort|Amadeus|direct_API — promote to reference product]']
