Relevant for OTA and metasearch channels that require content distribution alongside rate/inventory feeds.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this CRS channel mapping configuration record was first created in the system. Used for audit trail, data lineage tracking, and compliance with GDPR data processing records requirements.']
  crs_property_code varchar [note: 'The property identifier code as registered in Sabre SynXis CRS. This is the CRS-side property reference used in all rate and availability distribution messages to channels. Distinct from the internal property_id.']
  crs_rate_plan_code decimal [note: 'The rate plan code as defined in Sabre SynXis CRS (e.g., BAR, LRA, NRR, corporate rate codes). This is the source-side rate plan identifier that is translated and mapped to the channel-specific rate plan code for distribution.']
  currency_code varchar [note: 'ISO 4217 three-letter currency code in which rates are distributed to this channel (e.g., USD, EUR, GBP). Determines the currency of rate publication and commission calculation for this channel mapping.']
  effective_from date [note: 'The date from which this CRS channel mapping configuration becomes active and rates/availability begin distributing to the channel. Used to schedule future mapping activations and track the start of channel distribution periods.']
  effective_until date [note: 'The date on which this CRS channel mapping configuration expires and distribution to the channel ceases. Null indicates the mapping is open-ended with no scheduled end date. Used for contract-aligned channel distribution management.']
  guarantee_policy_code varchar [note: 'Code identifying the payment guarantee policy required for bookings through this channel mapping (e.g., \'CC_REQUIRED\' for credit card guarantee, \'DEPOSIT\' for advance deposit). Ensures PCI DSS-compliant payment handling requirements are communicated to the channel.']
  inventory_allocation_type varchar [note: 'Defines how room inventory is allocated to this channel. \'pooled\' means the channel draws from the shared inventory pool; \'allotment\' means a fixed block is reserved for the channel; \'free_sell\' means unlimited sell without allocation; \'on_request\' means availability must be confirmed manually.']
  is_mobile_optimized boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this channel mapping is configured to distribute mobile-specific rates or content optimized for mobile booking platforms. Supports mobile channel performance analytics and targeted mobile rate strategy.']
  last_sync_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp of the most recent successful rate and availability synchronization push from Sabre SynXis CRS to the distribution channel for this mapping. Used to monitor channel connectivity health, detect stale distributions, and support SLA compliance reporting.']
  lra_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this channel mapping is configured with Last Room Availability (LRA), meaning the channel has access to the last available room in the property\'s inventory. LRA is typically granted to GDS corporate accounts and preferred OTA partners under contractual obligation.']
  mapping_code varchar [note: 'Externally-known unique alphanumeric code identifying this CRS-to-channel mapping configuration within Sabre SynXis. Used as the business identifier for cross-system reference and audit. Serves as the BUSINESS_IDENTIFIER for this MASTER_RESOURCE entity.']
  mapping_name varchar [note: 'Human-readable descriptive name for this CRS channel mapping configuration (e.g., \'Booking.com Standard Rate Mapping - NYC Midtown\'). Serves as the IDENTITY_LABEL for this MASTER_RESOURCE entity.']
  mapping_status varchar [note: 'Current operational lifecycle status of this CRS channel mapping. \'active\' means the mapping is live and distributing rates/availability; \'suspended\' means temporarily halted; \'testing\' means in QA validation. Serves as the LIFECYCLE_STATUS for this MASTER_RESOURCE entity.']
  mapping_type varchar [note: 'Classification of what this mapping configuration governs — whether it maps rate plans, room types, inventory controls, packages, or promotional offers to the channel. Serves as the CLASSIFICATION_OR_TYPE for this MASTER_RESOURCE entity.']
  market_segment_code varchar [note: 'The market segment code assigned to bookings originating from this channel mapping (e.g., \'LEISURE\', \'CORPORATE\', \'WHOLESALE\', \'OTA\'). Used for USALI-compliant revenue segmentation, STR benchmarking, and RevPAR analysis by channel.']
  max_advance_booking_days varchar [note: 'Maximum number of days in advance that a booking can be made through this channel mapping (booking window). Controls how far into the future availability is published to the channel. Null indicates no maximum booking window restriction.']
  max_los varchar [note: 'Maximum number of nights allowed for a booking through this channel mapping. Null indicates no maximum stay restriction. Used to control long-stay bookings on specific channels as part of yield optimization strategy.']
  min_advance_booking_days varchar [note: 'Minimum number of days in advance that a booking must be made through this channel mapping. Used to enforce advance purchase restrictions (e.g., NRR non-refundable rates requiring 7-day advance booking) as distributed via the CRS.']
  min_los varchar [note: 'Minimum number of nights required for a booking to be accepted through this channel mapping. A value of 1 means no minimum stay restriction. Used to enforce LOS (Length of Stay) controls as part of revenue management strategy distributed via the CRS.']
  rate_category varchar [note: 'Classification of the rate type distributed through this channel mapping. Indicates whether the channel receives Best Available Rate (BAR), Last Room Availability (LRA) rates, Non-Refundable Rates (NRR), corporate negotiated rates, packages, promotional rates, or wholesale rates. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: bar|lra|nrr|corporate|package|promotional|wholesale — promote to reference product]']
  rate_offset_type varchar [note: 'Defines whether a rate adjustment (offset) is applied to the CRS rate before distribution to this channel. \'none\' means the CRS rate is published as-is; \'flat_amount\' means a fixed currency amount is added or subtracted; \'percentage\' means a percentage markup or markdown is applied.']
  rate_offset_value decimal(10,2) [note: 'The numeric value of the rate offset applied to the CRS rate before distribution to this channel. Positive values indicate a markup; negative values indicate a markdown. Interpreted as a currency amount or percentage depending on rate_offset_type. Null when rate_offset_type is \'none\'.']
  rate_parity_enforced boolean [note: 'Indicates whether rate parity rules are enforced for this channel mapping, requiring that the rates distributed to this channel match the Best Available Rate (BAR) published on other channels. Critical for OTA contract compliance and rate integrity monitoring.']
  sell_limit varchar [note: 'Maximum number of rooms that can be sold through this channel per night under the current allocation configuration. A null or zero value indicates no sell limit is applied (free sell). Used to control channel-level inventory exposure and prevent overbooking.']
  sync_frequency_minutes varchar [note: 'Configured frequency in minutes at which rate and availability updates are pushed from the CRS to this channel. Lower values indicate near-real-time distribution (e.g., 5 minutes for OTA partners); higher values indicate batch distribution schedules.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this CRS channel mapping configuration record was most recently modified. Used for change tracking, incremental ETL processing, and audit compliance. Critical for detecting configuration drift in channel distribution settings.']

  Note: 'Mapping configuration between Sabre SynXis CRS and each distribution channel, defining how rate plans, room types, and inventory controls are translated and published per channel. Captures CRS property code, channel-specific rate plan codes, room type mapping, inventory allocation rules, sell limits, and last-room-availability (LRA) flags. Critical for ensuring accurate rate and availability distribution across all connected channels.'
}

Table channel.channel_rate_plan {
  channel_rate_plan_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique surrogate identifier for each channel-specific rate plan configuration record in the Silver Layer lakehouse. Primary key for this entity.']
  channel_contract_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.channel_contract. Business justification: Channel rate plans are negotiated and defined within the scope of a channel contract. The contract governs which rate plans (BAR, NRR, LRA, corporate, package) are available to a channel and under wha']
  fnb_revenue_center_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to fnb.revenue_center. Business justification: Channel rate plans with F&B inclusions (BB/HB/FB packages) must post meal revenue to the correct F&B revenue center for USALI departmental reporting and package revenue splitting. Revenue managers and']
  primary_distribution_channel_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.channel. Business justification: Each channel-specific rate plan configuration belongs to one distribution channel. Many rate plans per channel. Removes redundant channel_code, channel_name, and channel_type which can be retrieved vi']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Identifier of the hotel property for which this channel rate plan configuration applies. Enables property-level rate plan and channel management across a multi-property portfolio.']
  revenue_rate_plan_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to revenue.revenue_rate_plan. Business justification: Channel rate plans are channel-specific derivations of master revenue rate plans. The rate loading workflow — where revenue managers publish rates from the RMS to channel rate plans — requires this FK']
  seasonal_calendar_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.seasonal_calendar. Business justification: Revenue managers align channel rate plans to seasonal demand periods (peak/off-peak, blackout dates, LOS restrictions). The seasonal_calendar drives rate loading decisions — which rates are open/close']
  advance_purchase_days varchar [note: 'Minimum number of days in advance of arrival that a booking must be made to qualify for this rate plan on this channel. For example, a value of 7 means the guest must book at least 7 days before check-in. Supports advance purchase rate strategies and demand management.']
  approved_by varchar [note: 'Name or identifier of the revenue management or distribution team member who approved this channel rate plan configuration for publication. Supports governance, approval workflow tracking, and audit compliance for rate distribution decisions.']
  base_rate_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'The base room rate amount (in property currency) from which the channel-specific rate is derived. For BAR-derived plans, this is the current BAR value. For flat rates, this is the fixed rate. Expressed per room per night. Supports rate parity monitoring and channel pricing strategy analysis.']
  booking_window_end_date date [note: 'The last calendar date on which bookings can be made for stays under this channel rate plan. Defines the closing of the booking window. Nullable if the rate plan remains bookable indefinitely until the stay date.']
  booking_window_start_date date [note: 'The earliest calendar date on which bookings can be made for stays under this channel rate plan. Defines the opening of the booking window for this rate plan on this channel. Used for promotional and advance purchase rate plan management.']
  cancellation_policy_code varchar [note: 'Code referencing the cancellation and penalty policy linked to this channel rate plan. Examples: FLEX24H (free cancellation up to 24 hours), NRR-NOCANCEL (non-refundable, no cancellation), SEMI-FLEX48H (partial refund if cancelled 48+ hours prior). Critical for NRR and advance purchase rate plans.']
  channel_rate_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'The final channel-specific rate amount (in property currency) published to this distribution channel after applying the rate derivation method and adjustment. This is the rate visible to consumers on the channel. Per room per night. Core metric for rate parity compliance monitoring.']
  channel_rate_plan_status decimal [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the channel rate plan configuration. Active = currently published and bookable on the channel; Inactive = deactivated and not available; Suspended = temporarily paused (e.g., rate parity violation); Pending = awaiting activation or approval; Expired = past effective end date; Draft = configured but not yet submitted for distribution.']
  close_out_days varchar [note: 'Number of days before arrival after which this rate plan is closed out and no longer bookable on this channel. Complements advance_purchase_days to define the booking window. A value of 0 means the rate is bookable up to the day of arrival.']
  commission_rate_pct decimal(6,4) [note: 'The commission percentage payable to the distribution channel (e.g., OTA, GDS, travel agent) for bookings made under this rate plan. Expressed as a decimal percentage (e.g., 15.0000 = 15%). Critical for cost of acquisition analysis and channel profitability reporting.']
  connectivity_fee_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Fixed fee amount (in property currency) charged by the channel or connectivity provider per booking or per period for distributing this rate plan on the channel. Distinct from commission (which is percentage-based). Supports total cost of acquisition calculation.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this channel rate plan configuration record was first created in the system. Supports audit trail, data lineage, and compliance reporting requirements.']
  crs_rate_plan_code decimal [note: 'The rate plan identifier as assigned in the Sabre SynXis Central Reservation System (CRS). Used for cross-system reconciliation between the lakehouse Silver Layer and the operational CRS. Enables traceability of rate plan configurations back to the source system.']
  currency_code varchar [note: 'ISO 4217 three-letter currency code for the rate amounts on this channel rate plan. Examples: USD, EUR, GBP, AED. Supports multi-currency channel distribution and rate parity analysis across international markets.']
  days_of_week_applicable bigint [note: 'A 7-character binary string indicating which days of the week (Mon-Sun) this rate plan is applicable on the channel. Each position represents a day: position 1=Monday through position 7=Sunday. \'1\' = applicable, \'0\' = not applicable. Example: \'1111100\' = Monday through Friday only. Supports weekday/weekend rate differentiation.']
  effective_from date [note: 'The date from which this channel rate plan configuration becomes active and the rate plan is published to the channel. Defines the start of the rate loading schedule for this channel-rate plan combination.']
  effective_until date [note: 'The date on which this channel rate plan configuration expires and the rate plan is no longer published to the channel. Nullable for open-ended configurations. Supports rate loading schedule management and seasonal rate plan publishing.']
  is_package_rate decimal(9,4) [note: 'Indicates whether this channel rate plan is a package rate that bundles room accommodation with additional inclusions (e.g., breakfast, spa credit, parking, F&B voucher). True = package rate with inclusions; False = room-only rate. Supports package revenue attribution and channel mix analysis.']
  is_rate_parity_applicable boolean [note: 'Indicates whether rate parity rules apply to this channel rate plan configuration. True = this rate plan is subject to rate parity monitoring and must match rates across applicable channels; False = exempt from parity (e.g., opaque rates, member-only rates, negotiated corporate rates). Supports rate parity compliance management.']
  is_refundable boolean [note: 'Indicates whether bookings made under this channel rate plan are eligible for a refund upon cancellation. True = refundable (flexible rate); False = non-refundable (NRR). Key attribute for consumer transparency and rate plan classification.']
  last_loaded_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this rate plan was most recently successfully loaded or updated on the distribution channel. Supports rate loading schedule management, troubleshooting, and audit of channel rate distribution operations.']
  max_los varchar [note: 'Maximum number of nights a guest may stay under this rate plan on this channel. Nullable if no maximum stay restriction applies. Used in conjunction with min_los to define the eligible stay window for this channel rate plan.']
  min_los varchar [note: 'Minimum number of nights a guest must stay to be eligible to book this rate plan on this channel. A value of 1 indicates no minimum stay restriction. Length of Stay (LOS) restrictions are a key Revenue Management System (RMS) tool for yield optimization.']
  notes varchar [note: 'Free-text field for operational notes, special instructions, or contextual information about this channel rate plan configuration. Examples: rate loading exceptions, channel-specific negotiation notes, promotional campaign references, or revenue strategy rationale.']
  rate_adjustment_type varchar [note: 'Indicates whether the channel-specific pricing adjustment is a markup (rate higher than base, e.g., to cover OTA commission) or a markdown (rate lower than base, e.g., promotional discount). NONE indicates no adjustment is applied and the base rate is published as-is.']
  rate_adjustment_unit varchar [note: 'Specifies whether the rate_adjustment_value is expressed as a PERCENTAGE of the base rate or as a fixed AMOUNT in the property currency. Determines how the channel-specific rate is computed from the base rate and adjustment value.']
  rate_adjustment_value decimal(10,4) [note: 'The numeric value of the rate adjustment applied to derive the channel-specific rate from the base rate. Interpretation depends on rate_adjustment_unit: if PERCENTAGE, this is the percentage (e.g., 15.00 = 15%); if AMOUNT, this is the absolute currency amount. Used in conjunction with rate_adjustment_type to compute the final channel rate.']
  rate_derivation_method varchar [note: 'The method used to calculate the channel-specific rate from the base rate. FLAT = fixed absolute rate amount; PERCENTAGE = percentage markup or markdown applied to a base rate; BAR_DERIVED = derived as a percentage or offset from the Best Available Rate (BAR); YIELD_MANAGED = dynamically set by the Revenue Management System (RMS); NEGOTIATED_FIXED = fixed contracted rate for corporate or wholesale agreements.']
  rate_loading_status varchar [note: 'Operational status of the rate plan loading process to the channel. Loaded = successfully transmitted and active on the channel; Pending Load = queued for transmission to the channel; Load Failed = transmission error requiring remediation; Not Loaded = not yet submitted; Deactivated = previously loaded but now removed from the channel.']
  rate_parity_group_code varchar [note: 'Code identifying the rate parity group to which this channel rate plan belongs. Rate plans within the same parity group are monitored for price consistency across channels. Enables grouping of comparable rate plans for parity compliance reporting.']
  rate_plan_code varchar [note: 'The externally-known alphanumeric code identifying the rate plan as configured in the Central Reservation System (CRS) and Property Management System (PMS). Examples: BAR, NRR, LRA, CORP001, PKG-BB. This is the business identifier used across Sabre SynXis CRS and Oracle OPERA PMS for rate loading and distribution.']
  rate_plan_name varchar [note: 'Human-readable descriptive name of the rate plan as displayed in the CRS and channel interfaces. Examples: \'Best Available Rate\', \'Non-Refundable Rate\', \'Last Room Availability Corporate\', \'Bed and Breakfast Package\'.']
  rate_plan_status decimal(18,6)
  rate_plan_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the rate plan by its commercial structure. BAR = Best Available Rate (dynamic public rate); NRR = Non-Refundable Rate (discounted, no cancellation); LRA = Last Room Availability (guaranteed availability for corporate); CORPORATE = negotiated corporate rate; PACKAGE = bundled rate with inclusions; PROMOTIONAL = limited-time promotional rate; WHOLESALE = net rate for tour operators; NEGOTIATED = contracted rate; OPAQUE = channel-opaque pricing. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: BAR|NRR|LRA|CORPORATE|PACKAGE|PROMOTIONAL|WHOLESALE|NEGOTIATED|OPAQUE — promote to reference product]']
  room_type_applicability varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of room type codes to which this channel rate plan applies. If null or \'ALL\', the rate plan applies to all room types at the property. Examples: \'STD,DLX,STE\' or \'ALL\'. Supports room-type-specific channel pricing strategies.']
  stay_date_end date [note: 'The latest arrival date for which this channel rate plan is valid. Bookings must have an arrival date on or before this date. Nullable for open-ended rate plans. Supports seasonal and promotional rate plan management.']
  stay_date_start date [note: 'The earliest arrival date for which this channel rate plan is valid. Bookings made under this rate plan must have an arrival date on or after this date. Supports seasonal rate plan publishing and blackout date management.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this channel rate plan configuration record was most recently modified. Supports change tracking, audit trail, and incremental data processing in the Silver Layer lakehouse.']

  Note: 'Channel-specific rate plan configurations defining which rate plans (BAR, NRR, LRA, corporate, package) are published to which channels, with channel-specific pricing adjustments, markup/markdown rules, and rate loading schedules. Captures rate plan code, channel applicability, rate derivation method (flat, percentage, derived from BAR), advance purchase restrictions, and cancellation policy linkage. Supports rate parity compliance and channel-specific pricing strategy.'
}

Table channel.booking_source {

  attribution_hierarchy_level varchar [note: 'Numeric level in the booking source attribution hierarchy used for revenue reporting roll-ups.   booking_window_max_days varchar [note: 'Maximum advance booking window in days applicable to this booking source, as configured in the CRS. Applicable when connectivity_fee_applicable is True. Used alongside commission_rate to compute total cost of acquisition (COA) per channel.']
  connectivity_fee_applicable decimal(18,2) [note: 'Indicates whether a GDS or channel connectivity fee is charged per booking for this source, in addition to or instead of a commission.   contract_start_date date [note: 'Effective start date of the distribution agreement or contract with this booking source partner. Used for contract lifecycle management, commission rate validity tracking, and channel activation scheduling in SAP S/4HANA contract management.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this booking source record was first created in the data platform. Used for data lineage, audit trail, and reference data change management. Conforms to ISO 8601 format (yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss.SSSXXX).']

  currency_code varchar [note: 'ISO 4217 three-letter currency code in which commissions and connectivity fees for this booking source are settled. Used for multi-currency commission processing in SAP S/4HANA accounts payable and foreign exchange reconciliation.']
  deactivation_date date [note: 'Date on which this booking source was deactivated or retired from the CRS and PMS. Null for currently active sources. Used for channel lifecycle management, historical reporting continuity, and audit trail maintenance.']
  gds_code varchar [note: 'Standard GDS identifier code for the booking source when the channel is a Global Distribution System participant.   geographic_scope varchar [note: 'Defines the geographic reach of this booking source: global (worldwide distribution), regional (specific world region), domestic (single country), or property_specific (single property only). Used for channel distribution strategy and regional channel mix analysis.']
  iata_code varchar [note: 'IATA-assigned numeric agency code for travel agency or OTA booking sources participating in IATA-governed distribution. Used for agency commission processing, GDS segment attribution, and travel agency performance reporting. Null for non-agency sources.']
  inventory_update_frequency varchar [note: 'Frequency at which room inventory and rate availability are pushed or synchronized to this booking source channel. Real-time channels receive instant updates via API; others receive batch updates. Impacts overbooking risk management and rate parity compliance.']
  is_direct_channel boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this booking source is a direct brand channel (True) or an indirect intermediary channel (False). Direct channels include brand website, brand app, call center, and walk-in. Used for direct booking ratio KPI tracking and cost-of-acquisition benchmarking against indirect channels.']
  last_room_availability boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this booking source has Last Room Availability (LRA) contractual rights, meaning the channel must be offered inventory even when only the last room is available. LRA is a common contractual obligation in corporate and GDS agreements. Impacts inventory control rules in IDeaS G3 RMS.']
  marketing_attribution_model varchar [note: 'Defines the marketing attribution model applied to bookings from this source for campaign effectiveness measurement and marketing ROI (Return on Investment) reporting.   payment_model decimal(18,2) [note: 'Defines the payment collection model for this booking source: merchant (OTA collects payment from guest and remits net to hotel), agency (hotel collects and pays commission to channel), net_rate (channel marks up a net rate), or direct_bill (corporate direct billing). Impacts revenue recognition, accounts receivable, and cash flow management.']
  pms_source_code varchar [note: 'Source code as configured in Oracle OPERA PMS for this booking source. Used for front desk reservation attribution, daily operations reporting (DOR), and property-level channel mix analysis. May differ from CRS source code due to property-level configuration.']
  preferred_partner_tier varchar [note: 'OTA or channel partner tier classification indicating the level of preferred partnership status. Preferred partners typically receive enhanced placement, lower commission rates, or co-marketing benefits. Used for OTA partnership management and channel strategy prioritization.']
  rate_parity_monitored boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this booking source is subject to rate parity monitoring as part of the OTA contract or channel distribution agreement. When True, the Revenue Management System (RMS) and channel manager enforce rate parity rules to prevent undercutting on this channel. Critical for OTA contract compliance.']
  rate_parity_type varchar [note: 'Specifies the rate parity obligation for this booking source: full_parity (rates must match all channels), narrow_parity (rates must match other OTAs but may differ from direct), or no_parity (no rate parity obligation).   sort_order varchar [note: 'Numeric sort order for displaying booking source records in PMS, CRS, and reporting tool dropdown lists and channel mix reports. Lower values appear first. Used for UI configuration in Oracle OPERA PMS and Sabre SynXis CRS administration screens.']
  source_category varchar [note: 'Standardized sub-channel category classifying the booking source by interface type and traveler segment. Drives cost-of-acquisition attribution, commission tier assignment, and channel mix optimization analysis. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: ota_desktop|ota_mobile|gds_corporate|direct_web|direct_app|voice|group|wholesale — promote to reference product]']
  source_code varchar [note: 'Externally-known alphanumeric code uniquely identifying the booking source within the Central Reservation System (CRS) and Property Management System (PMS).   source_description varchar [note: 'Detailed narrative description of the booking source, including its operational context, target traveler segment, and how it integrates with the distribution ecosystem. Used for onboarding documentation and channel strategy reference.']
  source_name varchar [note: 'Human-readable display name of the booking source as used in reporting dashboards, revenue management analysis, and channel mix reports. Examples: \'Expedia Desktop\', \'Amadeus GDS Corporate\', \'Brand Direct App\'.']
  supports_best_available_rate decimal(9,4) [note: 'Indicates whether this booking source is eligible to receive and display the Best Available Rate (BAR) as distributed through the CRS. Table channel.inventory_allocation {
  inventory_allocation_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique surrogate identifier for each inventory allocation record in the channel distribution system. Primary key for the inventory_allocation data product.']
  channel_contract_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.channel_contract. Business justification: Channel inventory allocations (allotments) are typically governed by a channel contract — the contract defines the allotment terms, release dates, and obligations. Linking channel_inventory_allocation']
  channel_rate_plan_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the rate plan associated with this inventory allocation. Determines which pricing rules apply to the allocated inventory on this channel.']
  inventory_channel_room_type_id varchar
  inventory_control_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to revenue.inventory_control. Business justification: Channel inventory allocations distribute sell limits and overbooking caps set by revenue-domain inventory control records. This FK supports the core channel inventory distribution workflow, enabling r']
  primary_channel_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the distribution channel (OTA, GDS, direct, voice, etc.) to which this inventory allocation applies. Sourced from Sabre SynXis CRS channel configuration.']
  primary_channel_room_type_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the room type (e.g., standard king, deluxe double, suite) for which inventory is being allocated to the channel.']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the property for which inventory is being allocated. Links to the property master record in Oracle OPERA PMS.']
  rate_restriction_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to revenue.rate_restriction. Business justification: Channel inventory allocations (stop-sell, CTA, CTD, min/max LOS) are operationally triggered by revenue-domain rate restriction records. Revenue managers need to trace which rate restriction drove a c']
  seasonal_calendar_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.seasonal_calendar. Business justification: Channel inventory allocations are governed by seasonal demand periods — blackout dates trigger stop-sell, peak seasons alter overbooking limits, and LOS restrictions change by season. Linking allocati']
  action_type varchar [note: 'The type of inventory control action that generated this record. CREATE indicates a new allocation was established; UPDATE modifies an existing allocation; CLOSE applies a stop-sell or close-out; REOPEN lifts a restriction; RELEASE returns unsold inventory to the pool; OVERRIDE applies a manual revenue management override.']
  active_status varchar [note: 'Current operational status of this channel inventory allocation. Active allocations are enforced by the channel management system.']
  allocated_rooms varchar
  allocated_units varchar [note: 'The total number of room nights (units) assigned to this channel for the specified stay date range and room type. Represents the allotment block size or sell limit granted to the channel.']
  allocation_reference_number bigint [note: 'Externally-known alphanumeric reference number assigned by the Central Reservation System (CRS) or Property Management System (PMS) to uniquely identify this inventory allocation action. Used for cross-system reconciliation between Sabre SynXis CRS and Oracle OPERA PMS.']
  allocation_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle state of the inventory allocation record. ACTIVE indicates the allocation is live and controlling channel availability; INACTIVE means it has been superseded; EXPIRED means the stay date range has passed; CANCELLED means it was manually revoked; PENDING means it is awaiting activation.']
  allocation_type varchar [note: 'Method by which inventory is allocated to this channel for this room type. POOLED = shared inventory pool, ALLOCATED = fixed allocation, FREESALE = unlimited access, BLOCKED = no access.']
  allotment_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the inventory allotment method applied to this channel. FREE_SELL allows the channel to sell without a fixed block; ALLOCATION assigns a fixed block of rooms; STOP_SELL halts sales on the channel; CLOSE_OUT removes all availability; ON_REQUEST requires manual confirmation before booking is confirmed.']
  applied_by_user varchar [note: 'The username or employee identifier of the revenue manager or system user who applied this inventory control action. Used for audit trail, accountability, and change management reporting.']
  available_rooms varchar
  available_units varchar [note: 'The number of room nights currently available for sale on this channel, calculated as allocated_units minus consumed_units. Represents the real-time sellable inventory for the channel on the specified stay dates.']
  cancellation_count varchar [note: 'The number of bookings cancelled on this channel allocation since the last reporting snapshot. Used to track net pickup and assess channel-level cancellation patterns for demand forecasting.']
  channel_allocation_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Percentage of total room type inventory allocated to this channel. Used for allocation-based inventory management strategies.']
  channel_type varchar [note: 'The category of distribution channel for this allocation. OTA (Online Travel Agency), GDS (Global Distribution System), DIRECT_WEB (brand.com), VOICE (call center), GSO (Global Sales Office), WHOLESALE (tour operators/wholesalers), METASEARCH (Google, Trivago, etc.). Supports channel mix optimization analysis. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: ota|gds|direct_web|voice|gso|wholesale|metasearch — 7 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  commission_rate decimal(5,4) [note: 'The commission rate (expressed as a decimal, e.g., 0.15 for 15%) payable to the distribution channel for bookings made under this allocation. Used for cost of acquisition analysis and channel profitability reporting.']
  connectivity_fee decimal(18,2) [note: 'The fixed or per-transaction connectivity fee charged by the GDS or CRS for distributing inventory through this channel. Expressed in the property\'s local currency. Used for total cost of distribution analysis.']
  consumed_units varchar [note: 'The number of allocated room nights that have been booked or consumed by the channel as of the last system update. Used to calculate remaining availability and monitor channel pickup performance.']
  created_date date [note: 'Timestamp when this allocation record was created in the system.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this inventory allocation record was first created in the system. Provides the audit trail creation timestamp for data lineage and compliance purposes.']
  currency_code varchar [note: 'The ISO 4217 three-letter currency code applicable to financial fields (connectivity_fee) in this allocation record (e.g., USD, EUR, GBP). Ensures consistent multi-currency reporting across global properties.']
  days_out varchar [note: 'The number of days between the allocation action date and the stay_date_from (booking window). Used in revenue management analysis to understand how far in advance inventory controls are being applied relative to the arrival date.']
  effective_end_date date [note: 'Date when this channel inventory allocation configuration expires. Null for currently active allocations.']
  effective_start_date date [note: 'Date when this channel inventory allocation configuration becomes effective.']
  effective_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this inventory allocation action became effective and was applied to the channel. Represents the business event timestamp when the allocation, stop-sell, or restriction was activated in the CRS.']
  is_closed_to_arrival boolean [note: 'Indicates whether arrivals are blocked on the first date of the stay period for this channel and room type. When TRUE, guests cannot check in on the stay_date_from date, preventing new bookings that start on that date.']
  is_closed_to_departure boolean [note: 'Indicates whether departures are blocked on the stay_date_to date for this channel and room type. When TRUE, guests cannot check out on that date, preventing bookings that end on that date.']
  is_rms_generated boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this inventory allocation action was automatically generated by the Revenue Management System (IDeaS G3 RMS or Infor EzRMS) as opposed to being manually entered by a revenue manager. Supports analysis of automation adoption and RMS recommendation acceptance rates.']
  is_stop_sell boolean [note: 'Indicates whether a stop-sell control has been applied to this channel for the specified stay dates and room type. When TRUE, the channel is prevented from accepting new bookings regardless of remaining available units.']
  last_modified_date date [note: 'Timestamp when this allocation record was last updated.']
  last_room_availability boolean [note: 'Indicates whether Last Room Availability (LRA) is contractually required for this channel. When TRUE, the channel must be offered the last available room at the property, typically a contractual obligation with certain OTA or corporate accounts.']
  lift_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this inventory allocation action was lifted, reversed, or superseded. Null if the allocation is still active. Used to track the full lifecycle of each inventory control action.']
  lra_enabled_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether Last Room Availability is enabled for this room-type-channel combination, overriding property-level LRA settings.']
  max_los varchar [note: 'The maximum number of nights a guest is permitted to stay under this allocation. Enforced when restriction_type is MAX_LOS. Null indicates no maximum stay restriction is applied.']
  maximum_los_override varchar [note: 'Channel-specific maximum length of stay restriction for this room type, overriding property-level defaults.']
  min_los varchar [note: 'The minimum number of nights a guest must stay to be eligible to book under this allocation. Enforced when restriction_type is MIN_LOS. A value of 1 means no effective minimum restriction.']
  minimum_los_override varchar [note: 'Channel-specific minimum length of stay requirement for this room type, overriding property-level defaults.']
  overbooking_allowance varchar [note: 'The number of additional room nights above the physical inventory that this channel is permitted to sell as part of the property\'s overbooking strategy. A value of 0 means no overbooking is permitted on this channel.']
  overbooking_limit_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Maximum overbooking percentage allowed for this room type on this channel. Used for revenue management optimization.']
  pickup_count varchar [note: 'The number of new bookings received on this channel allocation since the last reporting snapshot. Supports pickup reporting and demand forecasting in the Revenue Management System (RMS).']
  priority_rank varchar [note: 'Priority ranking for this channel when allocating inventory for this room type. Lower numbers indicate higher priority.']
  rate_parity_enforcement_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether rate parity rules are actively enforced for this room type on this channel.']
  rate_parity_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether rate parity compliance is enforced for this channel allocation. When TRUE, the allocated inventory must be offered at rates consistent with other channels per rate parity agreements. Used for OTA contract compliance monitoring.']
  reason_code varchar [note: 'Standardized code identifying the business reason for the inventory control action (e.g., HIGH_DEMAND, GROUP_BLOCK, OVERBOOKING_PROTECTION, RATE_PARITY_VIOLATION, CHANNEL_PERFORMANCE, MAINTENANCE). Used for revenue management analysis and audit reporting. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: HIGH_DEMAND|GROUP_BLOCK|OVERBOOKING_PROTECTION|RATE_PARITY_VIOLATION|CHANNEL_PERFORMANCE|MAINTENANCE|FORECAST_ADJUSTMENT|COMPETITIVE_RESPONSE — promote to reference product]']
  reason_description varchar [note: 'Free-text narrative providing additional context for the inventory control action beyond the standardized reason_code. Captures specific business justification entered by the revenue manager or system.']
  release_date date [note: 'The date on which any unsold allocated inventory is released back to the general property inventory pool. After this date, the channel no longer holds exclusive rights to the allocated units, enabling the property to sell them through other channels.']
  restriction_type varchar [note: 'The type of booking restriction applied to this inventory allocation. MIN_LOS enforces a minimum Length of Stay (LOS); MAX_LOS enforces a maximum LOS; CLOSED_TO_ARRIVAL (CTA) prevents new arrivals on the specified date; CLOSED_TO_DEPARTURE (CTD) prevents departures; FULL_PATTERN_LENGTH requires exact stay duration; NONE means no restriction is applied.']
  sell_limit varchar [note: 'The maximum number of room nights the channel is permitted to sell regardless of total property availability. Acts as a cap to prevent overselling on a specific channel and supports channel mix optimization.']
  sold_rooms varchar
  stay_date date
  stay_date_from date [note: 'The first date of the stay period for which this inventory allocation is effective. Defines the start of the date range over which the allocated room nights apply.']
  stay_date_to date [note: 'The last date of the stay period for which this inventory allocation is effective. Defines the end of the date range over which the allocated room nights apply.']
  stop_sell_flag boolean
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when this inventory allocation record was last modified. Tracks the most recent change to the allocation for audit trail and change management purposes.']
  version_number varchar [note: 'Monotonically incrementing version counter for this inventory allocation record. Incremented each time the allocation is modified, enabling optimistic concurrency control and historical version tracking in the Silver layer.']

  Note: 'Transactional records of inventory (room nights) allocated to specific channels per property, room type, and date range, including all inventory control actions (allocations, stop-sells, close-outs, and restrictions). Captures allocation quantity, sell limit, allotment type (free-sell, allocation, stop-sell), release date, consumed vs. available units, restriction type (minimum LOS, closed to arrival, closed to departure), reason code, applied-by user, effective and lift timestamps. Supports channel-level inventory controls, allotment management, revenue management restriction actions, and prevents overselling across distribution channels.'
}

  channel_rate_plan_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.channel_rate_plan. Business justification: Channel bookings use channel-specific rate plans. The channel_booking table currently has rate_plan_id pointing to channel.revenue_rate_plan (cross-domain) and rate_plan_code (STRING). Adding channel_']
  commission_schedule_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.commission_schedule. Business justification: Each channel booking is subject to a specific commission schedule that governs the commission rate applied. Linking channel_booking to commission_schedule enables direct traceability from a booking to']

  guest_profile_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the guest profile record associated with this booking. Enables guest-level channel attribution, loyalty linkage, and lifetime value analysis. PARTY_REFERENCE per TRANSACTION_HEADER canonical role.']

  booking_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the channel booking transaction. Drives channel performance reporting, cancellation rate analysis, and no-show tracking. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: confirmed|cancelled|modified|no_show|waitlisted|tentative — promote to reference product if additional statuses are required]']
  booking_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The exact date and time when the booking was received through the distribution channel. BUSINESS_EVENT_TIMESTAMP per TRANSACTION_HEADER canonical role. Used for booking pace analysis, lead time calculation, and channel demand pattern reporting.']
  cancellation_policy_code varchar [note: 'The code identifying the cancellation policy applicable to this booking (e.g., FREE_CANCEL_24H, NRR_NON_REFUND, FLEX_48H). Determines penalty applicability and refund eligibility for cancelled bookings.']
  cancellation_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The date and time when the booking was cancelled. Populated only when is_cancelled is True. Used for cancellation lead time analysis and channel cancellation pattern reporting.']
  channel_commission_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'The commission amount payable to the distribution channel partner for this booking. Represents the cost of acquisition for channel-sourced bookings. Part of MONETARY_TRIPLET per TRANSACTION_HEADER canonical role.']
  channel_type varchar [note: 'High-level classification of the distribution channel category through which the booking was received. Enables channel mix analysis and cost-of-acquisition benchmarking across channel categories. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: OTA|GDS|direct_web|voice|corporate|wholesaler|metasearch|travel_agent — promote to reference product if additional types are required]']
  check_in_date date [note: 'The scheduled guest arrival date for the stay associated with this booking. Used for stay date demand analysis, length-of-stay (LOS) calculation, and revenue period attribution.']
  check_out_date date [note: 'The scheduled guest departure date for the stay associated with this booking. Combined with check_in_date to derive length of stay (LOS) and average length of stay (ALOS) metrics.']
  commission_amount decimal(15,2)
  commission_rate_pct decimal(7,4) [note: 'The commission rate percentage applied by the distribution channel for this booking (e.g., 15.00 for 15%). Used for commission structure analysis, channel cost benchmarking, and contract compliance monitoring.']
  connectivity_fee_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'The per-booking connectivity or transaction fee charged by the channel technology provider (e.g., GDS segment fee, CRS transaction fee). Included in total cost-of-acquisition calculation alongside commission.']
  corporate_account_code varchar [note: 'The corporate account or negotiated rate code associated with this booking, if applicable. Used for corporate channel performance analysis, negotiated rate compliance monitoring, and corporate account revenue attribution.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The timestamp when this channel booking transaction record was first created in the Silver layer data product. RECORD_AUDIT_CREATED per TRANSACTION_HEADER canonical role. Used for data lineage, audit trail, and ETL reconciliation.']
  crs_booking_reference varchar [note: 'The unique booking identifier assigned by the Central Reservation System (Sabre SynXis CRS). Used for cross-system reconciliation between CRS and PMS booking records.']
  currency_code varchar [note: 'The ISO 4217 three-letter currency code in which the booking was transacted by the distribution channel (e.g., USD, EUR, GBP). Required for multi-currency revenue reconciliation and FX conversion in financial reporting. Part of MONETARY_TRIPLET per TRANSACTION_HEADER canonical role.']
  gds_segment_number bigint [note: 'The segment identifier assigned by the Global Distribution System (GDS) for bookings originating through GDS channels (e.g., Sabre, Amadeus, Travelport). Used for GDS billing reconciliation and travel agent attribution.']
  gross_booking_value decimal(18,4) [note: 'The total gross value of the booking as received from the distribution channel, inclusive of all room charges before deduction of channel commissions or fees. Expressed in the booking currency. Part of MONETARY_TRIPLET per TRANSACTION_HEADER canonical role.']
  is_cancelled boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this booking has been cancelled (True = cancelled, False = active). Used for channel-level cancellation rate analysis and net booking volume reporting.']
  is_modified boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this booking has been modified after initial confirmation (True = modified, False = original booking). Used to track modification rates by channel and assess channel data quality.']
  is_rate_parity_compliant boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the booked rate is compliant with the rate parity agreement for this channel (True = compliant, False = parity violation detected). Critical for OTA contract compliance monitoring and channel rate parity management.']
  last_modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The timestamp when this channel booking transaction record was last updated in the Silver layer data product. RECORD_AUDIT_UPDATED per TRANSACTION_HEADER canonical role. Used for change data capture, incremental load processing, and audit compliance.']
  lead_time_days varchar [note: 'The number of days between the booking timestamp and the check-in date. Stored as a business attribute to support lead time distribution analysis by channel, demand forecasting, and last-minute booking pattern identification.']
  length_of_stay_nights varchar [note: 'The number of nights for the booked stay, derived from check-in and check-out dates. Stored as a business attribute to support LOS-based rate restriction analysis, minimum stay controls, and ALOS reporting without requiring date arithmetic at query time.']
  net_revenue_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'The net revenue retained by the property after deduction of channel commission from the gross booking value. Primary metric for channel contribution analysis and cost-of-acquisition benchmarking. Part of MONETARY_TRIPLET per TRANSACTION_HEADER canonical role.']
  number_of_guests varchar [note: 'The total number of guests included in this booking. Used for occupancy analysis, per-guest revenue calculations, and channel demand pattern reporting.']
  number_of_rooms varchar [note: 'The number of rooms included in this booking transaction. Typically 1 for FIT (Free Independent Traveler) bookings; may be greater for group or multi-room bookings received through a channel.']
  ota_confirmation_number bigint [note: 'The booking confirmation number assigned by the Online Travel Agency (OTA) platform (e.g., Booking.com, Expedia). Used for reconciliation with OTA partner systems and commission invoice matching.']
  pms_confirmation_number bigint [note: 'The externally-communicated confirmation number generated by the Property Management System (Oracle OPERA PMS) for this booking. Serves as the primary guest-facing booking reference. BUSINESS_IDENTIFIER per TRANSACTION_HEADER canonical role.']
  rate_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the rate type applied to this booking. BAR (Best Available Rate), LRA (Last Room Availability), NRR (Non-Refundable Rate), corporate, package, promotional, or group. Critical for rate parity monitoring and revenue strategy analysis. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: BAR|LRA|NRR|corporate|package|promotional|group — 7 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  source_country bigint [note: 'The ISO 3166-1 alpha-3 country code of the origin from which the booking was made through the channel. Used for geographic demand analysis, international vs. domestic channel mix reporting, and targeted marketing attribution.']
  travel_agent_iata_number bigint [note: 'The 8-digit IATA (International Air Transport Association) accreditation number of the travel agency that made this booking. Used for travel agent commission processing, GDS attribution, and agency performance reporting.']

  Note: 'Transactional record of each booking received through a distribution channel, capturing channel-level booking metadata including channel identifier, booking source, OTA confirmation number, GDS segment number, booking timestamp, property, room type, rate plan, stay dates, gross booking value, channel commission amount, net revenue to property, and booking modification/cancellation flags. Primary fact table for channel contribution and cost-of-acquisition analysis.'
}

Table channel.commission_schedule {
  commission_schedule_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique surrogate identifier for each commission or fee schedule record in the channel distribution cost management system. Primary key for the commission_schedule data product.']
  booking_source_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.booking_source. Business justification: Commission schedules can be defined at the booking source level — for example, a different commission rate may apply for bookings originating from a mobile app vs. desktop web vs. GDS segment within t']
  channel_contract_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to channel.channel_contract. Business justification: Commission schedules define the commission terms negotiated in channel contracts with OTA partners and GDS providers. Adding nullable channel_contract_id FK links commission schedules to their governi']
  channel_rate_plan_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the specific rate plan (BAR, LRA, NRR, package, negotiated corporate) to which this commission schedule is scoped. Null indicates the schedule applies to all rate plans for the channel partner.']
  market_segment_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to revenue.market_segment. Business justification: Commission schedules in hospitality are differentiated by market segment (corporate, leisure, group). Revenue and finance teams reconcile commission costs by segment for P&L reporting. The denormalize']
  ota_partner_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the distribution channel partner (OTA, GDS, CRS, channel manager, direct booking engine) to which this commission or fee schedule applies. Links to the channel partner master record.']
  primary_commission_channel_id varchar
  property_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the specific property or hotel to which this commission schedule applies. Null or a portfolio-level sentinel value indicates the schedule applies across all properties (chain-wide agreement).']
  seasonal_calendar_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.seasonal_calendar. Business justification: Commission schedules commonly have seasonal tiers — higher commissions during off-peak to stimulate demand, lower during peak. Linking commission_schedule to seasonal_calendar allows automated commiss']
  applies_to_cancellations boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the commission or fee is still payable when a booking is cancelled (True = commission owed on cancellations, False = commission waived on cancellations). Critical for NRR (Non-Refundable Rate) commission accrual and cancellation cost management.']
  applies_to_no_shows boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the commission or fee is payable on no-show bookings (True = commission owed on no-shows, False = commission waived). Affects no-show revenue net-of-commission calculations and OTA contract compliance.']
  approved_by varchar [note: 'Name or identifier of the authorized approver (e.g., VP Revenue Management, CFO) who approved this commission schedule for execution. Required for SOX financial controls compliance and audit trail.']
  approved_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this commission schedule was formally approved for activation. Part of the SOX-compliant approval audit trail for financial commitments.']
  auto_accrual_enabled boolean [note: 'Indicates whether commission and fee accruals under this schedule are automatically calculated and posted to the GL upon booking confirmation (True) or require manual accrual processing (False). Supports automated AP accrual workflows in SAP S/4HANA.']
  billing_frequency varchar [note: 'Frequency at which the channel partner invoices the property for commissions or fees: monthly (most common for OTA commissions), weekly, per_booking (real-time deduction), quarterly, annual (common for connectivity subscription fees). Drives AP accrual scheduling and cash flow forecasting.']
  booking_window_max_days varchar [note: 'Maximum advance booking window (in days before arrival) for which this commission schedule is applicable. Null indicates no maximum booking window restriction. Used in conjunction with booking_window_min_days for last-minute rate commission scoping.']
  booking_window_min_days varchar [note: 'Minimum advance booking window (in days before arrival) for which this commission schedule is applicable. Used for LOS (Length of Stay) and advance purchase rate plan commission scoping. Null indicates no minimum booking window restriction.']
  commission_basis varchar [note: 'The unit basis on which the commission or fee is calculated and accrued: per_booking (one charge per reservation), per_room_night (charge per occupied room night), per_segment (GDS per-segment charge), per_transaction (CRS per-transaction charge), per_period (fixed charge per billing period regardless of volume). Drives accrual engine logic.']
  commission_rate_pct decimal(5,2) [note: 'Negotiated commission rate expressed as a percentage of the applicable revenue base (e.g., 15.0000 = 15%). Applicable when fee_structure is \'percentage\'. Represents the contractually agreed OTA or agent commission rate. Confidential as it reflects negotiated commercial terms.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this commission schedule record was first created in the system. Used for audit trail, data lineage, and SOX financial controls compliance.']
  effective_end_date date
  effective_from date [note: 'The calendar date from which this commission or fee schedule becomes contractually binding and applicable to bookings. Used to determine which schedule version applies to a given booking date for accrual and invoice reconciliation.']
  effective_start_date date
  effective_until date [note: 'The calendar date on which this commission or fee schedule expires and is no longer applicable. Null indicates an open-ended agreement with no defined expiry. Used for schedule versioning and contract renewal tracking.']
  fee_currency_code decimal(18,2) [note: 'ISO 4217 three-letter currency code in which the flat fee or tiered threshold amounts are denominated (e.g., USD, EUR, GBP). Required for multi-currency AP reconciliation and cost-of-acquisition reporting.']
  fee_structure decimal(18,2) [note: 'Defines how the commission or fee is calculated: percentage (applied as a % of booking revenue or room revenue), flat (fixed monetary amount per booking or period), tiered (rate varies by volume or revenue thresholds), per_unit (fixed amount per room-night, segment, or transaction unit). Determines the accrual calculation method.']
  fee_type decimal(18,2) [note: 'Classification of the cost type captured by this schedule: commission (percentage of booking revenue paid to OTA/agent), per_segment_fee (GDS per-segment charge), per_transaction_fee (CRS per-booking transaction fee), connectivity_fee (channel manager or switch connectivity charge), subscription_fee (fixed periodic platform fee), override_commission (negotiated override above standard rate). Drives AP coding and cost-of-acquisition (COA) categorization.']
  flat_fee_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Fixed monetary fee amount per booking, segment, transaction, or billing period, expressed in the schedule currency. Applicable when fee_structure is \'flat\' or \'per_unit\'. Used for GDS per-segment fees, CRS per-transaction fees, and connectivity subscription fees. Confidential as it reflects negotiated commercial terms.']
  gl_account_code varchar [note: 'The General Ledger account code in SAP S/4HANA to which commission and fee expenses are posted for financial reporting under USALI. Ensures correct P&L classification of distribution costs (e.g., OTA commission expense, GDS fee expense) per USALI departmental accounting.']
  los_min_nights varchar [note: 'Minimum Length of Stay (LOS) in nights required for this commission schedule to apply. Null indicates no LOS restriction. Supports commission scoping for extended-stay or minimum-stay rate plans.']
  max_commission_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Contractual cap on the commission or fee amount payable per booking or per billing period. Applicable for schedules with a commission ceiling clause. Expressed in fee_currency_code. Confidential as it reflects negotiated commercial terms.']
  min_commission_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Contractual minimum commission or fee amount payable per booking or per billing period, regardless of the calculated percentage amount. Applicable for schedules with a commission floor clause. Expressed in fee_currency_code. Confidential as it reflects negotiated commercial terms.']
  negotiated_by varchar [note: 'Name or identifier of the internal team or individual (e.g., Revenue Management, Channel Distribution, Procurement) responsible for negotiating this commission schedule. Used for accountability tracking and contract ownership.']
  notes varchar [note: 'Free-text field for capturing additional context, special contractual conditions, negotiation history notes, or exceptions associated with this commission schedule. Not used for structured data; intended for operational reference by Revenue Management and AP teams.']
  payment_terms_days decimal(18,2) [note: 'Number of days from invoice receipt within which payment to the channel partner is due (e.g., 30 = Net 30). Used in AP aging analysis and cash flow management per SAP S/4HANA payment terms configuration.']
  rate_parity_monitored boolean [note: 'Indicates whether rate parity compliance is contractually required and actively monitored for bookings under this commission schedule (True = rate parity clause in effect). Supports rate parity monitoring workflows and OTA contract compliance management.']
  revenue_base decimal(18,2) [note: 'Defines the revenue component on which the commission percentage is calculated: room_revenue (room charges only), total_revenue (all charges including F&B and ancillaries), net_revenue (after discounts and taxes), gross_revenue (before deductions), f_and_b_revenue (food and beverage charges only). Critical for accurate commission accrual and invoice reconciliation.']
  schedule_code varchar [note: 'Externally-known alphanumeric code uniquely identifying this commission or fee schedule, used in AP reconciliation, contract references, and channel partner communications (e.g., OTA-EXP-COMM-2024, GDS-SAB-SEG-FEE).']
  schedule_name varchar [note: 'Human-readable descriptive name for the commission or fee schedule, used in reporting dashboards, AP workflows, and channel profitability analysis (e.g., \'Expedia Standard OTA Commission FY2024\', \'Sabre GDS Per-Segment Fee Q1 2024\').']
  schedule_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle state of the commission schedule: active (currently in force), inactive (temporarily suspended), pending (approved but not yet effective), expired (past effective_until date), terminated (cancelled before expiry), draft (under negotiation, not yet approved). Drives AP processing eligibility and accrual inclusion.']
  tier_1_rate_pct decimal(7,4) [note: 'Commission rate percentage applicable when booking volume or revenue falls within the Tier 1 threshold band in a tiered fee structure. Confidential as it reflects negotiated commercial terms.']
  tier_1_threshold decimal(18,4) [note: 'Lower volume or revenue threshold (in booking count or currency amount) that triggers the Tier 1 commission or fee rate in a tiered fee structure. Applicable when fee_structure is \'tiered\'. Confidential as it reflects negotiated commercial terms.']
  tier_2_rate_pct decimal(7,4) [note: 'Commission rate percentage applicable when booking volume or revenue falls within the Tier 2 threshold band in a tiered fee structure. Confidential as it reflects negotiated commercial terms.']
  tier_2_threshold decimal(18,4) [note: 'Upper volume or revenue threshold that triggers the Tier 2 commission or fee rate in a tiered fee structure. Applicable when fee_structure is \'tiered\'. Confidential as it reflects negotiated commercial terms.']
  updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when this commission schedule record was last modified. Used for change tracking, audit trail, and incremental data pipeline processing in the Databricks Silver Layer.']

  Note: 'Master and transactional records for all channel distribution costs — the single source of truth for OTA commissions, GDS segment fees, CRS transaction fees, channel manager connectivity fees, and per-booking cost accruals. Captures commission/fee structures (percentage, flat, tiered), negotiated rates per partner, applicable rate plans, effective date ranges, property scope, fee types, billing frequencies, and per-booking accrual records with amounts in local and base currency. Supports commission invoice reconciliation, AP processing, total cost-of-acquisition calculation, technology cost management, and channel profitability analysis. Encompasses all cost types previously tracked separately (connectivity fees, per-segment fees, per-transaction fees) in a unified cost management product.'
}
