  maintenance_issue_flag boolean [note: 'Boolean indicator whether maintenance issues were identified during the inspection that require handoff to the maintenance department (e.g., broken fixtures, HVAC problems, plumbing issues).']
  notes varchar [note: 'Additional free-text notes and observations recorded by the inspector, including positive feedback, special conditions, or contextual information for operational reference.']
  outcome varchar [note: 'Final result of the inspection: pass (room meets quality standards and is released), fail (room requires re-clean), or conditional_pass (minor issues noted but room released with follow-up required).']
  priority_level bigint [note: 'Priority classification for the inspection based on guest arrival time, room type, and operational needs: urgent (VIP or immediate check-in), high (same-day arrival), normal (next-day arrival), or low (future availability).']
  quality_score decimal(5,2) [note: 'Numerical quality score assigned to the room based on inspection criteria, typically on a 0-100 scale, used for GSS (Guest Satisfaction Score) correlation and housekeeper performance tracking.']
  reclean_required_flag boolean [note: 'Boolean indicator whether the room requires re-cleaning due to deficiencies identified during inspection. True indicates the room failed inspection and must be re-cleaned before guest occupancy.']
  room_release_flag boolean [note: 'Boolean indicator whether the room has been formally released as inspected and made available for guest check-in. True indicates the room is ready for sale and occupancy.']
  room_release_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The precise date and time when the room was released as inspected and made available for guest occupancy, critical for RevPAR (Revenue Per Available Room) and inventory availability tracking.']
  room_status_after varchar [note: 'The room status set after the inspection is completed, typically inspected (if passed) or dirty (if failed and requires re-clean), critical for PMS (Property Management System) room availability updates.']
  room_status_before varchar [note: 'The room status immediately prior to the inspection, typically clean (post-housekeeping) or dirty (pre-cleaning), used for status transition tracking and operational workflow validation.']
  scheduled_date date [note: 'The date on which the inspection was scheduled to occur, used for planning and workload management.']
  scheduled_time timestamp [note: 'The precise date and time when the inspection was scheduled to begin, enabling time-based operational coordination.']
  special_request_notes varchar [note: 'Free-text notes capturing any special guest requests or room preparation requirements that the inspector must verify (e.g., hypoallergenic bedding, extra amenities, accessibility features).']
  start_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The actual date and time when the inspector began the room inspection, used for duration calculation and operational analytics.']

  Note: 'Quality inspection record capturing the formal review of a cleaned room by a housekeeping supervisor or inspector before the room is released as \'inspected\' and made available for guest check-in. Records inspection outcome (pass/fail), deficiency items identified, re-clean required flag, inspector identity, inspection timestamp, and final room release status. Critical for GSS (Guest Satisfaction Score) and service quality management.'
}

  ffe_category varchar [note: 'Classification of whether the maintenance issue involves FF&E (Furniture Fixtures and Equipment) assets: furniture (movable items), fixtures (installed items), equipment (operational devices), or none (building systems).']

  guest_impacted boolean [note: 'Indicates whether a guest was directly impacted by the maintenance issue (True) or if the issue was identified during routine cleaning of a vacant room (False).']
  guest_notified boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the guest was notified about the maintenance issue and any impact to their stay (True/False).']
  handoff_status varchar [note: 'Current workflow state of the maintenance handoff: pending (awaiting engineering review), acknowledged (engineering notified), assigned (technician assigned), in_progress (work underway), completed (issue resolved), cancelled (no longer needed).']
  last_modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'System timestamp when this maintenance handoff record was last updated. Format: yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss.SSSXXX.']
  photo_attached boolean [note: 'Indicates whether photographic documentation of the maintenance issue was captured and attached to the request (True/False).']
  reported_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when the maintenance issue was identified and logged by housekeeping staff. Format: yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss.SSSXXX.']
  request_number bigint [note: 'Business-facing unique reference number for tracking and communication (e.g., MR-2024-001234).']
  requires_parts boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the maintenance repair requires ordering or retrieving replacement parts (True) or can be completed with on-hand materials (False).']
  requires_vendor boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the maintenance issue requires external vendor or contractor support (True) or can be handled by in-house staff (False).']
  resolution_notes varchar [note: 'Detailed notes from the maintenance technician describing the work performed, parts replaced, and final resolution of the issue.']
  room_status_impact varchar [note: 'Impact of the maintenance issue on room availability: out_of_order (room cannot be sold or occupied), out_of_service (room temporarily unavailable), sellable_with_note (room can be sold with guest notification), no_impact (room remains fully available).']
  safety_hazard boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the maintenance issue poses an immediate safety hazard to guests or staff (True/False), requiring urgent attention per OSHA standards.']
  source_inspection_type varchar [note: 'Type of housekeeping activity during which the maintenance issue was identified: routine_cleaning (daily service), checkout_inspection (post-departure check), quality_inspection (supervisor review), guest_complaint (guest-reported issue), preventive_maintenance (scheduled inspection).']
  urgency_level bigint [note: 'Priority classification for the maintenance request: critical (immediate safety hazard or room unusable), high (impacts guest experience significantly), medium (noticeable but not blocking), low (cosmetic or minor).']
  warranty_applicable boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the defective item or system is still under manufacturer or vendor warranty (True/False).']
  work_started_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when the assigned technician began work on the maintenance issue. Format: yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ss.SSSXXX.']

  Note: 'Operational record of maintenance issues identified by housekeeping staff during room cleaning or inspection, including defect type (plumbing, electrical, HVAC, furniture, fixtures), room location, urgency level, description, reported timestamp, and handoff status to the engineering/maintenance team. Represents the housekeeping-to-maintenance handoff workflow and tracks resolution to ensure room availability is restored. Distinct from engineering work orders which are owned by the property/facilities domain.'
}

Table housekeeping.attendant {
  attendant_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the housekeeping attendant record. Primary key for the attendant entity in the housekeeping domain.']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the property where this attendant is primarily assigned. Supports multi-property workforce management.']
  active_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this attendant record is currently active and available for scheduling and room assignments. Inactive records are retained for historical reporting but excluded from operational workflows.']
  ada_accommodation_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the attendant has an approved reasonable accommodation under the Americans with Disabilities Act. Accommodations may include modified duty assignments, assistive equipment, or adjusted productivity targets. Details of specific accommodations are maintained in confidential HR records.']
  attendance_points varchar [note: 'Current attendance point balance under the property\'s attendance policy. Points are typically assigned for absences, tardiness, and early departures, with progressive discipline triggered at defined thresholds. Points may expire after a rolling period (e.g., 12 months).']
  average_credits_per_shift decimal(5,2) [note: 'Rolling average of actual room credits completed per shift over the most recent evaluation period (typically 30 or 90 days). Used to track individual productivity trends and identify training needs or performance issues.']
  code varchar [note: 'Business identifier for the attendant used in daily operations, room assignment sheets, and housekeeping reports. Typically a short alphanumeric code displayed on badges and mobile devices.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this attendant record was first created in the housekeeping system. Used for audit trail and data lineage tracking.']
  emergency_contact_name varchar [note: 'Name of the person to contact in case of workplace emergency or injury. Maintained for employee safety and OSHA compliance.']
  emergency_contact_phone varchar [note: 'Phone number of the emergency contact person. Critical for rapid communication in case of workplace accidents or medical emergencies.']
  employment_status varchar [note: 'Current employment lifecycle status of the attendant. Active attendants are available for scheduling. On-leave includes FMLA, medical, and personal leave. Seasonal workers are employed during peak periods. Probationary status applies to new hires during their initial evaluation period.']
  hire_date date [note: 'Date the attendant was hired into the housekeeping department. Used to calculate seniority for union section bidding, vacation accrual, and tenure-based benefits.']
  language_skills varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of languages the attendant can speak and understand. Important for guest interaction, safety communication, and team coordination in multilingual properties. Format: ISO 639-1 language codes (e.g., en,es,fr).']
  last_performance_review_date date [note: 'Date of the most recent formal performance review. Most properties conduct annual or semi-annual reviews aligned with merit increase cycles.']
  last_updated_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this attendant record was most recently modified. Tracks the recency of data for change data capture and incremental processing.']
  locker_number bigint [note: 'Assigned locker number in the employee locker room where the attendant stores personal belongings, uniform, and equipment during their shift.']
  mobile_device_code varchar [note: 'Identifier of the mobile device (smartphone or tablet) assigned to the attendant for receiving room assignments, updating room status, reporting maintenance issues, and communicating with supervisors. Integrates with property management system mobile housekeeping applications.']
  notes varchar [note: 'Free-text field for operational notes about the attendant, such as special skills, assignment preferences, equipment needs, or temporary restrictions. Used by supervisors for day-to-day workforce management.']
  performance_rating bigint [note: 'Most recent performance evaluation rating for the attendant. Based on quality inspections, productivity metrics, guest feedback, attendance, and adherence to standards. Used for merit increases, promotion decisions, and performance improvement plans.']
  role_type varchar [note: 'Primary housekeeping role classification. Determines work assignment types, productivity benchmarks, and labor cost allocation. Room attendants clean guest rooms, turndown attendants provide evening service, house persons handle heavy cleaning and linen transport, supervisors oversee sections, inspectors perform quality checks, and public area cleaners maintain lobbies and common spaces.']
  section_assignment varchar [note: 'Current section or floor assignment within the property. Sections are typically organized by floor, wing, or building. Section assignments may be permanent (based on seniority bidding) or rotational.']
  seniority_date date [note: 'Date used for calculating seniority ranking within the housekeeping department. May differ from hire date due to transfers, breaks in service, or union contract provisions. Critical for section bidding rights and shift preference allocation.']
  shift_assignment varchar [note: 'Current shift assignment for the attendant. AM shift typically covers morning checkout cleaning, PM shift handles afternoon turnovers and turndown service, night shift performs deep cleaning and public area maintenance. Split shifts cover peak periods. On-call attendants fill in for absences.']
  target_credits_per_shift decimal(5,2) [note: 'Productivity benchmark expressed as the target number of room credits the attendant should complete per shift. Room credits vary by room type: standard rooms = 1.0 credit, suites = 1.5-2.0 credits, checkout rooms = 1.2 credits, stayover rooms = 0.7 credits. Used for performance evaluation and labor cost per occupied room (CPOR) calculation.']
  termination_date date [note: 'Date the attendant\'s employment ended. Null for active employees. Used for historical workforce analysis and rehire eligibility determination.']
  uniform_size bigint [note: 'Uniform size for the attendant used for ordering and inventory management of housekeeping uniforms. Format varies by property (e.g., S/M/L/XL or numeric sizing).']
  union_classification varchar [note: 'Union job classification code as defined in the collective bargaining agreement. Determines pay grade, work rules, and assignment restrictions. Examples include classifications for different room types, shift differentials, and specialized duties.']
  union_member_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the attendant is a member of a labor union. Determines applicability of collective bargaining agreement provisions, grievance procedures, and union-specific benefits.']

  Note: 'Housekeeping-domain operational profile of a room attendant or housekeeping staff member, capturing their role (room attendant, turndown attendant, house person, supervisor, inspector, public area cleaner), section certifications (suite-qualified, VIP-certified), language skills, productivity benchmarks (target credits per shift by room type mix), seniority date for union section bidding, union membership status and CBA classification, training completion records for chemical handling and blood-borne pathogen protocols, and current shift assignment status. This is a domain-specific operational view — the full employee master record (payroll, benefits, personal details) is owned by the workforce domain.'
}

  Note: 'Operational record of lost and found items discovered during room cleaning or public area maintenance. Supports guest service recovery, property liability management, and jurisdictional unclaimed property regulations.'
}

  maintenance_request_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the maintenance request created as a result of issues identified during this housekeeping work order.']
  profile_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the guest currently occupying the room or who requested the service, if applicable.']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the hotel, resort, or vacation property where this work order is assigned.']
  room_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the specific guest room or space that requires housekeeping or maintenance service.']
  stay_history_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to guest.stay_history. Business justification: Stay-level maintenance cost reporting and service recovery tracking require linking work orders to the specific guest stay. Enables analysis of total maintenance spend per stay and correlation with gu']
  vip_designation_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to guest.vip_designation. Business justification: VIP guests require priority work order handling and escalation management. Linking work_order to vip_designation enables VIP service SLA compliance reporting and replaces the denormalized vip_service ']
  actual_completion_time timestamp [note: 'The actual timestamp when the work order was completed by the assigned staff member, used for calculating service duration and labor costs.']
  actual_start_time timestamp [note: 'The actual timestamp when the assigned staff member began working on this work order, captured for labor tracking and performance analysis.']
  amenity_replenishment_required boolean [note: 'Boolean flag indicating whether guest amenities (toiletries, coffee, water) need to be replenished during this service.']
  cancellation_reason varchar [note: 'Free-text explanation of why the work order was cancelled, such as guest checkout, do-not-disturb request, or operational changes.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The timestamp when this work order record was first created in the system, used for audit trails and operational reporting.']
  guest_request_notes varchar [note: 'Notes capturing specific requests made by the guest related to this work order, such as extra towels, hypoallergenic products, or do-not-disturb preferences.']
  inspection_result varchar [note: 'Outcome of the quality inspection indicating whether the work met quality standards, failed inspection, or passed with conditions.']
  inspection_score decimal(5,2) [note: 'Numerical quality score assigned during inspection, typically on a scale of 0-100, used for performance tracking and quality metrics.']
  inspection_time timestamp [note: 'The timestamp when the completed work was inspected by a supervisor or quality assurance team member.']
  labor_cost_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'The calculated labor cost for this work order based on employee hourly rates and service duration, used for Cost Per Occupied Room (CPOR) calculations.']
  linen_change_required boolean [note: 'Boolean flag indicating whether full linen change (sheets, pillowcases, towels) is required for this work order, used for linen inventory planning.']
  maintenance_handoff_required boolean [note: 'Boolean flag indicating whether this work order identified issues requiring handoff to the maintenance department, such as broken fixtures or equipment malfunctions.']
  modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The timestamp when this work order record was last modified, capturing any updates to status, assignments, or other attributes.']
  priority varchar [note: 'Priority level assigned to the work order based on guest arrival times, room status, and operational urgency.']
  room_status_after varchar [note: 'The room status after the work order was completed and inspected, reflecting the final state for property management system updates.']
  room_status_before varchar [note: 'The room status at the time the work order was created, capturing the initial state for status transition tracking.']
  scheduled_completion_time timestamp [note: 'The target timestamp by which the work order should be completed, often driven by guest check-in times or operational deadlines.']
  scheduled_start_date date [note: 'The date when the work order is scheduled to begin, used for planning and resource allocation.']
  scheduled_start_time timestamp [note: 'The precise timestamp when the work order is scheduled to begin, enabling time-block scheduling and shift management.']
  service_duration_minutes varchar [note: 'The total time in minutes spent completing the work order, calculated from actual start and completion times, used for labor productivity analysis.']
  source_system_code varchar [note: 'The unique identifier for this work order in the source operational system, used for data lineage and reconciliation.']
  special_instructions varchar [note: 'Free-text field containing specific instructions or notes for the housekeeping staff, such as guest preferences, allergy alerts, or special cleaning requirements.']
  supply_cost_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'The total cost of housekeeping supplies and amenities consumed during this work order, including linens, toiletries, and cleaning materials, used for CPOR tracking.']
  work_order_number bigint [note: 'Externally-visible unique work order number used for tracking and reference by housekeeping staff and property management systems.']
  work_order_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the work order tracking its progression from creation through completion and inspection.']
  work_order_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the work order indicating the nature of service required: routine cleaning, deep cleaning, quality inspection, maintenance handoff, turndown service, or mid-stay refresh.']

  Note: 'Master reference table for work_order. Referenced by work_order_id.'
}

Table housekeeping.maintenance_request {
  maintenance_request_id varchar [pk, note: 'Primary key for maintenance_request']
  facility_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to property.property_facility. Business justification: Maintenance requests are filed for all facility types — pool, gym, spa, parking structures. maintenance_request has room_id but no property_facility_id. Hotel engineering tracks requests by facility f']
  fnb_outlet_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to fnb.fnb_outlet. Business justification: Engineering teams log maintenance requests for F&B outlet equipment (kitchen appliances, bar refrigeration, HVAC). Linking to fnb_outlet enables outlet-level cost allocation, SLA tracking, and complia']
  follow_up_maintenance_request_id varchar [note: 'Self-referencing FK on maintenance_request (follow_up_maintenance_request_id)']
  profile_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the guest who reported the maintenance issue, if applicable.']
  property_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the property where the maintenance request originated.']
  room_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the specific room where maintenance is required.']
  acknowledged_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when the maintenance request was acknowledged by the maintenance team.']
  actual_cost_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Actual total cost incurred for completing the maintenance work, including labor and materials.']
  actual_duration_minutes varchar [note: 'Actual time in minutes spent completing the maintenance work.']
  actual_start_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Actual date and time when maintenance work began.']
  assigned_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when the maintenance request was assigned to a technician or vendor.']
  category varchar [note: 'Functional area or trade specialty required to address the maintenance issue.']
  closed_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when the maintenance request was formally closed in the system.']
  completed_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when the maintenance work was completed.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'System timestamp when the maintenance request record was first created in the database.']
  currency_code varchar [note: 'Three-letter ISO 4217 currency code for all monetary amounts in this request.']
  estimated_cost_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Estimated total cost for completing the maintenance work, including labor and materials.']
  estimated_duration_minutes varchar [note: 'Estimated time in minutes required to complete the maintenance work.']
  guest_impact_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the maintenance issue impacts guest experience or room availability.']
  inspection_completed_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when the post-maintenance quality inspection was completed.']
  inspection_notes varchar [note: 'Notes and observations recorded during the post-maintenance quality inspection.']
  inspection_passed_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the completed maintenance work passed the quality inspection.']
  inspection_required_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether a quality inspection is required after maintenance work is completed.']
  issue_description varchar [note: 'Detailed narrative description of the maintenance problem or issue reported.']
  labor_cost_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Cost of labor for the maintenance work performed.']
  last_modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'System timestamp when the maintenance request record was last updated in the database.']
  location_description varchar [note: 'Detailed description of the specific location within the property or room where maintenance is needed (e.g., bathroom sink, ceiling near window).']
  maintenance_request_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle state of the maintenance request in the workflow from creation through completion.']
  materials_cost_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Cost of materials and supplies used in the maintenance work.']
  priority varchar [note: 'Urgency level assigned to the maintenance request, determining response time and resource allocation.']
  recurring_issue_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this is a recurring maintenance issue that has been reported multiple times.']
  reported_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Date and time when the maintenance issue was first reported or the request was created.']
  request_number bigint [note: 'Externally-visible unique business identifier for the maintenance request, typically displayed to staff and used in communications.']
  request_status varchar
  request_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the maintenance request based on the nature of work required.']
  resolution_description varchar [note: 'Detailed narrative of the actions taken to resolve the maintenance issue.']
  resolution_notes varchar
  room_out_of_order_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the maintenance issue requires the room to be marked as out-of-order and unavailable for occupancy.']
  safety_hazard_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the maintenance issue presents a safety hazard requiring immediate attention.']
  scheduled_start_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Planned date and time when maintenance work is scheduled to begin.']
  target_completion_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Service Level Agreement (SLA) target date and time by which the maintenance request should be completed based on priority.']
  warranty_claim_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the maintenance work is covered under equipment or vendor warranty.']

  Note: 'Master reference table for maintenance_request. Referenced by maintenance_request_id.'
}
